# بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم
*Source: KASHKOLE, Binder 34 (Quranic Studies), Chapter 163. 11 topics. Language: ur.*

<!-- section 1 (id=5734, raw_sort=1): Meaning of the word Allah -->
We completed the Istiaaza. which was about seeking Allah's protection from all kinds of evil. And now that we've done that. the next logical step. after asking Allah to protect us from external threats. is to ask Allah to bless us with the correct internal thoughts.  and that is what Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem and the Fateha is all about. So in other words we can say that Aozubillah and Bismillah. they both work in cooperation with each other.  And that is ofcourse the whole point.  We begin by seeking refuge from the evil because we want to get rid of the bad first. Once we've done that. once we've entered Allah's protection. the next thing to do is to now ask Allah for the good. 

And this actually is the entire premise of our religion. Islam stands on these two primary pillars of negative and positive. rejection and acceptance.  Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:فَمَن يَكْفُرْ بِٱلطَّغُوتِ وَيُؤْمِنۢ بِٱللَّهِ فَقَدِ ٱسْتَمْسَكَ بِٱلْعُرْوَةِ ٱلْوُثْقَىٰ⟫

Whoever rejects the false gods . the false dieties and accepts allah . that is the one who has held on to the strong hand hold.

So we have to first reject evil.  and only AFTER we've done that. we can affirm the good. And you can see that this concept.  is perfectly aligned with our kalima. What is our kalima?
⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ . You can see it has two parts. ⟪ar:لا الہ⟫and ⟪ar:الا اللہ⟫ .  The first part of ⟪ar:لا الہ⟫ deals with the eradication of the negative. We first negate everything that is bad. we negate all false gods by saying.  ⟪ar:لا الہ⟫. And only then. the second part comes into play. which is the affirmation of the one true god. ⟪ar:الا اللہ⟫. Thats what the sequence of this kalima teaches us. We have to negate or reject evil first. only then the affirmation can take place. why? Because unless and until we negate the bad. it is not possible to affirm the good.

When we fall sick. the doctor first has to work on eliminating the disease. Once the disease has been eradicated. only then he works on improving the patients health. A teacher first has to remove a student's misconceptions before he can establish new concepts. You have to take down an old broken-down disfunctional structure. before building a new working structure in its place. so this principle of ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ . is a universal principle. You will find it working everywhere. Similarly the Istiaaza and the Basmallah. they both work together to accomplish the same goal. Istiaaza is the removal of all evil. and therefore it must precced the Basmallah . which is the establishment of all good. with the names of Allah who is Rehman and Raheem.

---

Importance and virtue of BARR

Now there is SO much to be said about the importance and virtue of the Basmallah. It is the essence of Surah AlFateha.  I told you earlier. quoting the hadees of Rasul Allah (SallalAllahu Alyhi wa Aalihee wa Sallam)  that Surah AlFateha is the essence of Quran. And there is another VERY famous saying of Maulana Ali. in which he says.

⟪ar-quote:إن كل ما في الکتب السماویۃ، في القرآن⟫. Indeed whatever exists in all previous divine books. their essence.  exists in the Quran
⟪ar-quote:و كل ما في القرآن  في فاتحة الكتاب⟫. And everything that is in the Quran. is in the opener of the book. meaning Surah AlFateha
⟪ar-quote:و كل ما في الفاتحة في البسملة⟫. And everything that is in the Fateha. is in the Basmallah. the very first ayah of the Fateha.
⟪ar-quote:و كل ما في البسملة في الباء⟫. And everything that is in the Basmallah. is in it's letter Ba. which is the first alphabet of the Basmallah.
⟪ar-quote:و انا النقطة تحت الباء⟫. And I am the dot under the Ba.

This is a very profound statement by ⟪ar:سید العارفین⟫ . the master of al knowers. In other words Maulan Ali says. the entire Quran is condensed in the Ba of Bismillah. And regarding the Basmallah. Maulana Ali AS said to one of his sahabi. Ibn Abbas that
⟪ar-quote:لو شئت لأَوْقَرتُ سبعين بعيراً من باء بسم الله الرحمن الرحيم⟫

If I want.  I could tell you so much about the Ba of Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem. that 70 camels would have to be loaded with books containing that knowledge.

This statement alludes to the amount of knowlede that has been encapsulated. and condensed into just the Ba of Basmallah. And this is not just an exagerated or hyperbolized statement. Our duaat have actually written volumes on the Ba of Basmallah.

For this session. I'm only going to describe a part of this statement of Maulana Ali. where he calls the Basmallah. the essence of Surah AlFateha. First of all let's understand what he mean by the essence. I'll give you a very simple example of how to understand this statement. If you ask me. Asif Mamu. tell me everything that Allah wants from me. How do I understand who Allah is and what He expects of me. I'll say. Read all the revealed books. Read the Taura, Injeel, Zaboor, Psalsm of Solomon and you'll know what he wants from you. You tell me. No No. that's too much. Give me a summerized version of all of those books. So then I'll say. Fine read the Quran. Everything that is described in all of these divine books. has been summarized in the 114 surahs of the Quran. You say. No Mamu. that's still too much. I've got homework to do. TV shows to watch. I have to play tennis. I got so many more important things to do.  I can't sit and read 114 huge chapters. Give me something simpler. I'll say . Ok fine. just understand Surah AlFateha. Just understand the 7 verses of Surah AlFateha. and you'll understand the essence of the Quran. Because the remaining Quran is simply an explanation of these 7 verses. Everything the Quran talks about is summarized in the 7 verses of the Fateha.

Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem. talks about the identifying the creator and his primary attributes. The name of Allah who is intensely merciful. consistently merciful

Hamdu. mentions the praise of Allah and how we must be grateful to Him for all his blessings

Rehman AlRaheem. describes his mercy

Malik YaumAlDeen. talks about the day of judgment and everything that'll happen on that day

Iyyaka Nabud wa Iyyaka nastaeen. is an explanation of how to enter the servitude of Allah. and how to gain the rank of becoming his slave and seekig his help. through prayers and supplications

Ihdina. is about seeking his guidance for the straight path that leads to success.

Siraat. talks about the stories of three kinds of people. those who were successful. those who incurred Allahs wrath and finally those who went astray.

That's it! That's the entire Quran in 7 verses for you. You say Mamu. I know 7 seems like a small number to you. but I have the memory of a gold fish. So I can't remember so much stuff. Can you simplify it further for me? So then I'll say. Fine Goldie! . If you can't remember All of that. just remember Allah. and his two primary attributes of mercy that he has identified himself with. AlRehman and AlRaheem. He is intensely merciful and He is consistently mercifuly. Because the entire Fateha. the entire Quran. All revelated divine scriptures are nothing more than the identification of of Allah. and the description of his intense and constant mercy. His Rehmaniyat. and His Raheemiyat.  Because it is the merciful that showers you with his blessing for which you need to be grateful to him and praise Him. It is the merciful who is going to establish the day of reckoning. It is the merciful who helps. who provides guidance. who leads people to success. identifies the true path from the false path. Who shows us what path to walk on and what not to walk on. The entire Fateha is a mainfestation of Allah's Rehmaniyat. his intense mercy. and His Raheemiyat. His constant mercy.

So forget everything else. Just remember the name of your creator that is Allah. And understand that he is intensely merciful . and He is consistently merciful. That's it. This name Allah and his 2 primary attributes of mercy. That's what deen and Islam is all about.

This is the meaning of this extremely eloquent statatment of Maulana Ali.
⟪ar-quote:إن كل ما في الکتب السماویۃ في القرآن⟫. Indeed the essence of all previous divine books exists in the Quran
⟪ar-quote:و كل ما في القرآن  في فاتحة الكتاب⟫. And everything that is in the Quran. is in the Fateha
⟪ar-quote:و كل ما في الفاتحة في البسملة⟫. And everything that is in the Fateha. is in the Basmallah

So the entire essence. the meaning of all previous divine scriptures has been summarized and condensed in the 114 surahs of the Quran. And the essential meaning of the 113 surahs has been condensed into the 7 verses of Surah AlFateha. And then the 6 verses of AlFateha have been condensed into the Basmallah.

And then he further goes to say that the Basmallah is further condensed into the letter Ba of the basmallah and I am the dot under the Ba. I'll explain this part later. But for now. I hope you understand what he means by saying that the essence of all previous divine scriptures has been condensed and reduced to this once statement. ⟪ar:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫.

Now as things get condensed. the surface area shrinks but what happens to density? It increases right? And if this density is of something that is extremely percious. what happens to it's value? It's value increases. It becomes even more precious.

So if the Basmallah. contains the essence of all previously revealed divine scriptures. including the Quran itself. You can imagine how dense and how lofty and valuable this statement must be. And then you can imagine how denese the Ba of Basmillah must be.  if it is the essence of the entire divine mass. So just like the big bang theory. you can see that this Ba. in reality. is the singularity.  that exploded into this enormous universe of revealed scriptures. SubhanAllah. Just as the entire universe came into existence from an exteremely dense mass. this entire universe of religion also originated from this incredibly divine mass of the letter Ba. And Maulana Ali says. I am the dot under that Ba. SubhanAllah. InshaAllah I'll explain what this means in a future session.

But I think if you just really comprehend and think about what I just told you. then this in itself.  is enough to appreciate the power and the strength of the Basmallah. No wonder this statement preceeds every single act that we do in our daily life. There is no divine action that is done without reciting the Basmallah. In fact Rasul Allah (SallalAllahu Alyhi wa Aalihee wa Sallam) said that
⟪ar-quote:کُلَّ شَئیٍ أَبتَر بِدُونِ بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫

Every act is rejected . it is disfigured. deormed . if not preceeded with Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem.

---

Now the Basmallah consists of 4 words. Bsm Allah AlRheman and AlRaheem. Well Technically 5 words. The BA, Ism,

Love - hope and fear

Of these words. the most important. the most virtuous. the most magnificent word is obviously "Allah". Everything else. all the other words revolve around this central word. Allah. So I thought it would be best to begin our discussion with this word. What does the word Allah mean. And what are these 99 names of Allah. Because Allah itself is a name. isn't it? Allah is the name of the diety that we worship. So then if Allah is a name. why does he need these other 99 names?. And why do we say. With the name of Allah the intensely merciful the consistently merciful?. Why not just with Allah the merciful? Or with the help of Allah the most merciful?.  Why the NAME of Allah? If I'm working on a project with Hussain. I wouldn't say. I completed this project with the name of Hussain. I wouldn't do that. I would just say I completed this project with Hussain. So then why does this verse insist on the name of Allah?.  What does the name sybolize?

And also who is Allah to us? How do we see Him in our lives? . Do we see him the way he should be seen?. Do we give him the place he deserves?. Do we truly love him? Do we truly love Allah? In fact. What does it even mean to love Allah?. What are the primary components of love?

So let's think about love in the worldly senese. Think about two people who are madly in love. What is the most important thing for a lover?. The satisfaction and happiness of his beloved. That's ALL that matters to a lover.  If I truly love someone. the ONLY thing that will matter to me. the ONLY thing I will be obsessed with. will be what? . To make my beloved happy.  Even if that means going against my own will and desires. That's what true love is. An obesssion about the happiness and satisfaction of my beloved.  at any cost. Why? . Because I recognize the importance of that person in my life. I recognize the need for my beloved's love. and I will do everything in my power to keep that person in my life. and make sure.  that person is  ALWAYS happy with me. Isn't that true?. In one sentence. that's the philosophy of love. An obsession for the happiness of the beloved.

And the output. or the manifestation of true love. is in the form of hope and fear.

Hope that my beloved will be pleased with my efforts. Hope that my efforts will be good enough for my beloved.  Why do you see guys buying flowers. writing poems in their blood. trying desperately to impress the girl they love? Why?. Hope! Hope that she will accept that gesture. Hope that she will find that effort satisfactory. and increase in her affection for him.  Hope that she will reward him with more care. more love. more affection. So that's how love manifests. in the form of Hope.

And then also Fear. Fear that I may not accidentally do something to offend the one I love. to displease her in anyway. So that she does not get upset with me. Or reject my efforts.

or punish me.  And what is the GREATEST of all punishments for a true lover? Do you know what it is? . It's Abandonment. There is nothing more painful for a lover. than when his beloved abandons and rejects him. When the beloved does not return the love.  Fear of abandoment is the greatest of all pains for a lover. Getting whipped and stoned and beaten and burnt is nothing. The real torment. the greatest of all fears for a lover. is the rejection from his beloved. A poet says.

⟪ar-quote:و مِنَ الشَّقاَوةُ أن تحبَ.⟫⟪ar-quote:وَ مَن تُحِبُّ يُحِبُّ غَيرَك⟫

The greatest of misery is when you love someone and that person does not return your love. or loves someon else

So these are the three primary emotions of love. Love, hope and fear.⟪ar:حب،و الرَّجاء والخوف⟫ . Now the question is. Do we have this relationship of love with Allah?. When we are dealing with Allah in our day to day lives. do our actions manifest in the form of hope and fear. Are we obsessed in our hopes of pleasing him?. Do we fear. or are we even concerned about displeasing him. or about offending or angering him? If not. Why not? . What's missing? . How do we develop that awareness of Allah. that will lead us towards that kind of love?

And then what are the conditions and obligations of love? What are the rights of the beloved? As Maulana Ali said.

⟪ar-quote:عَرَفتُمُ اللہ فَلَم تُأَدُّو حَقَّہُ⟫

You claim to know Allah.  but you do not fulfill his rights. That's the first problem. Because Allah say.

⟪ar-quote:فَعلَم! أنَّہُ لا الہ الا اللہ⟫

Know that there is no god but Allah. And knowing that there is no God but Allah.  and saying that there is no God but Allah.  are two different things. You see. Because even the hypocrite says La ilaha illa allah. But knowing and saying are two completely different things. So Maulana Aلi says that you claim to know Allah.  but you do not fulfill his rights upon you.

So we need to learn about that. We need to gain that knowledge. Because knowledge of Allah engenders love. That's the nature of knowledge of Allah. The more we will know about Allah the more we will love him. The more we know about his messenger the more we will love him. The more we know about Maulana Ali. the more we will love him.  Knowledge engenders love.

Now the lover is ALWAYS obedient.  to the beloved. That is the very nature of love. If you have somebody who claims they love you.  and then they never do what you ask. Then you should know that that is a false claim. They don't love you. They're just giving you lipservice. Because the very nature of love.  is that you do with the beloved asks.

⟪ar-quote:اِنَّ المُحِبُّ لِمَن یُحِبُّ، مُطِیعُ⟫

because the one who loves somebody. is always obedient to that person.

A poet came to a woman and told her about his friend who was madly in love with her. She asked the man. Tell me about this friend  of yours who claims to love me.And don't detract and don't embellish.Just give me the straight truth. and so the poet said.

⟪ar-quote:اِن کَانَ یَظُنُّ الموتُ بِالظَّمَا وَ قَال لَك لا تَشرِبُ المآءَ وَلَم یَرِدِ⟫

If he thought that he would die from thirst. And you said. Don't drink. He wouldn't drink.

That's the state of a true lover. The one who claims to love.  and the one who actually loves.  are two different things. Many people claim to love.

Shakespeare said. Love is not love Which alters when it alteration finds,   Or bends with the remover to remove. O no! it is an ever-fixed mark that looks on tempests and is never shaken;.  That's love. Love is not something that changes when the situation changes. People claim to lose their faith. Some bad event occurs in their life and they lose their faith. You know. I lost my faith. They didn't have faith in the first place. Because you can't lose faith. You either have it or you don't. Because faith is tested in trials. That's when the metal of a person is shown. It's not when things are going well. Anyone and everyone is a believer when things are going well. It's when things are going horribly wrong that's the real test of faith.

So knowledge engenders and gives birth to love. So that's what we're going to try to do . That's what Surah AlFateha is all about. That's the goal of this surah. To develop an awareness of Allah. who is Allah . what does the love of Allah mean. How that love manifests in the form of hope and fear. What are the obligations and conditions of love.

So let's begin with the word Allah and first understand what this word Allah means. Because this is a name taken by Allah AWJ Himself. Usually names are given by somebody else. Nobody names himself. they are named by others. But Allah is a name taken by Allah Himself.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّنِىٓ أَنَا ٱللَّهُ لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّآ أَنَا۠ فَٱعْبُدْنِى وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ لِذِكْرِىٓ ‎⟫

 Indeed, I am Allah. There is no deity except Me, so worship Me and establish prayer to remember me

So if He chose this name ALLAH for Himself. it must hold incredible significance and depth in it. So I want to begin by exploring this name Allah first. and then we'll go into his 99 names or attributes. and then finally look at the details of how the Basmallah is used. Why do we say it before we begin any action. It's supposed to create Barakah in our actions. so what does Barakah mean.Then there are the words AlRehman and AlRaheem. I'm actually going to leave these two words for later. Because we will encounter these two words again in the Fateha. AlRheman and AlRaheem.

---

Now let's take a look at the word Allah. Why did Allah choose this name to be his primary name? The Quran opens with the Fateha. and the Fateha opens with the Basmallah. بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم. In this very first verse of His very first Surah. He introduces himself with the name "Allah". And this name "Allah". is not just used in the basmallah. it is used in numerous other places in the Quran. Over 3500 times the word Allah is used in the Quran. There is no other name of Allah that even comes close to the quantity of times that this particular name "ALLAH" is mentioned.

Also interestingly. when we refer to him in our daily lives. We always use his actual name. Have you noticed that? . We ALWAYS call upon him by saying "ALLAH".  We say Oh Allah give me this.  Oh Allah help me with this.  Oh Allah protect me from that. So we always use His actual name. as opposed to other names like. Rehman. Raheem. Quddus. Salaam. Momin. We don't call upon him generally using these other names. even though they are his names as well. We almost always call upon him by His most glorified name.  when we are addressing Him or referring to him in our daily lives.

Now what does this word Allah mean? And BTW.  this is not a name that is unique to just our religion of Islam. Quite the contrary. this is the name that Allah chose for himself and mentioned it in every past scripture. even in the old and new testiments. we find the name Allah. in its hebrew form. In the old testement. we find that He refers to himself as eloh أِلَوہ. and ألوھیم . which are equivalent to the Arabic.  Allah and Allahumma. and in the new testiment as well. When they crucified Eisa (AS). the bible records his words as.

⟪ar-quote:الائی الائی لما سبختنی;  الائی الائی لما ترکتنی⟫

My Allah My Allah why did you abandon me?

So the name Allah is in fact the primary name.  that is not just specific to Islam.  but it has been used in every past religion, revelation and scripture. throughout the ages.  to all civilizations and to all prophets.

---

Linguistic meaning of ILAH and ALLAH

Now. To understand the word Allah. you must know something about Arabic. In the arabic language words are always based on tri-literal roots. For example you may have heard the word ⟪ar:عالم⟫or ⟪ar:علیم⟫. its mushtaq. These are derived from the tri-literal root word.⟪ar:علم⟫. meaning knowledge. So in Arabic. you'll always find words derived from two or three letter roots. So the word Allah too. actually comes from the three letter root word. "Ilah". Alif. Laam. Haa. Ilah. Which means diety. Allah. is actually AL + ILAH. THE DIETY. The definite article. Al and Ilah. combine to form. ALLAH. So in order to understand the meaning of the word Allah. we need to first understand the meaning of the word "ILAH".

Now the word Ilaah is a very rich word. It is a composite word and it has a slew of meanings in Ancient Arabic.

Primarily the word Ilah. comes from Alaha . ⟪ar:اَلَہَ یَعلُہُ⟫ . and the verb Alaha literally means to worship.  so Ilah is the entity that is the focus of worship and obedience. That's one meaning of the word ALAHA.

Another meaning.  Ilah is the one who you are completely devoted to. Someone you are completely loyal to.  Someone you turn to in your every single moment of happiness and grief. that is also an Ilah.

Another meaning of the word Ilah. is from ⟪ar:اَلِہَ⟫which is used for a child that is thirsty for the milk of its mother.  and is desperately crying for it. That's Aliha.  And the verbal meaning dervied from it is. the one that people desperately and inevitibly turn to.  when they are in need of help.  The one you turn to. in times of desperation. seeking their protection is also an Ilah. That's why one of the names of Allah is  ⟪ar:الصمد⟫.  Samad is the one that every being turns to for every need. and He himself is the one who has no needs.

Then another very beautiful meaning of the word Ilah.  is someone you are passionately in love with.  someone you cannot stop thinking about. Someone you are obsessed about. That person is also called Ilah. One of its derivates is (⟪ar:وَلَھَا⟫) Walaha.  which means to lose ones mind because of the loss of a beloved. In Urdu they say. ⟪ar:والھانہ محبت⟫. Mad love. That's also from Waliha.  That's why in Arabic the mother who loses her child is called ⟪ar:مُوَلَّا⟫.  this is mother who is suffereing that extremely excruciating pain and grief over the loss of her child. she is called ⟪ar:مُوَلَّا⟫. It's that kind of passionate and obsessive love . Because the one who loses Allah . who no longer has Allah in his life. would suffer from this type of ultimate grief and madness. The one who has felt the love of Allah. and then fallen from the grace of Allah . who no longer has that connection with Allah.  feels that he is going to lose his mind.  because now there is nothing left in his life to give him value. to give him meaning.  Because if you don't believe in allah. if you don't have a concept of an Ilah in your life. then your life has no purpose. so this is also one of the meanings of the word Ilah. To be passionately and obsessively in love with someone. Like a mother that loves its child. and is always obsessed about its safety. So you see . this extreme form of love.  is already embedded in the word ilah.

You know the story of Hazrat Ayyoob. He was put into great trials to test his faith. According to a hadees of Rasul Allah (SallalAllahu Alyhi wa Aalihee wa Sallam) . once Allah mentioned the patience and gratitude of Hazrat Ayyoob AS to his angels. So Iblees spoke to Allah and said.  that the only reason he is greateful to you is because you have blessed him with so much. You have given his so many posessions. children. that's the only reason he's greateful to you. If you take it away. you'll see he's no longer going to be greateful.

So Allah started taking things away from him. He took his posessions away. His house collapsed right in front of his eyes killing his children. Can you imagine that? And when he saw that happen right in front of his eyes. do you know what instinctively came out of his mouth? . AlHamdulillah. That's what he said. And then not just that. he got this horrible disease where his body got infected with worms. they would eat his flesh. And InshaAllah we'll talk about these trials when we study AlRehman AlRaheem. Why are prophets put into trials. why are we put into trials. It's a very interesting and eye opening topic.

But the point is. Allah put Hazrat Ayyoob through this extremem form of trial to test his faith and love of Allah. And he succeeded with flying colors. And when his test was completed. Allah asked him to bathe in this spring water that he set out for him. He took a bath in it and his disease was completely cured.

The reason I bring this up. is years later someone asked him. How is your health now Ayyoob?. He sighed and replied. The days of my illness were more beloved to me than these days of health. The man was shocked to hear that. He asked how come? . Ayyoob replied. that when I was ill. every single day Allah would ask me . How are you doing today Ayyoob? And since I've been cured. Allah no longer asks me that. And I miss that love and care from Allah. This is Waliha. This is Muwalla. Extreme . passionate love! . That a person is driven to insanity without the beloved. So that's another meaning of Ilah.

And also literally speaking. not linguistically. but literally.  the word Ilah me something that you lean on. Something that you put your entire weight on. When you're exhausted and you lean on something and put your entire weight on it.  that thing is literally called ⟪ar:الہ⟫. So you see the word Ilah means many things.

Also another derivative of the word Ilah. is  ⟪ar:وَلِھَا یعلُہُ⟫. ⟪ar:وَلِھَا⟫which means to become astounded. to become astonished. to become amazed.  And thats because when we try to think of Allah. we will become amazed and astonished. and come to the realization that we cannot understand who is Allah AWJ is. Allah is the one that if you try to comprehend Him . you will fail. if you try to walk towards him. you will tire yourself out but never reach him. if you let your thoughts and imaginations fly towards him. you will break your wings in that attempt.  but still not be able to reach him. Allah is an entity that is beyond comprehension.

This is why in the very first khutba of the Nahjul Balagha. Maulana Ali praising Allah says. And this is one of the Hamds I read in the beginning of our sessions.

⟪ar-quote:الحَمْدُ للهِ الَّذَي لاَ يَبْلُغُ مِدْحَتَهُ القَائِلُونَ⟫Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah whose worth cannot be described by speakers,

⟪ar-quote:وَلاِ يُحْصِي نَعْمَاءَهُ العَادُّونَ⟫whose bounties cannot be counted by those who attemp to count them

⟪ar-quote:ولاَ يُؤَدِّي حَقَّهُ الُمجْتَهِدُونَ⟫and whose rights of obedience cannot be fulfilled by those who strive to do so

⟪ar-quote:الَّذِي لاَ يُدْركُهُ بُعْدُ الهِمَمِ⟫the one. who the flights of intellect cannot approach

⟪ar-quote:وَلاَ يَنَالُهُ غَوْصُ الفِطَنِ⟫and the plunge to the depths of comprehension cannot reach;

⟪ar-quote:الَّذِي لَيْسَ لِصِفَتِهِ حَدٌّ مَحْدُودٌ⟫He is the one. whose description contain no limits

⟪ar-quote:وَلاَ نَعْتٌ مَوْجُودٌ⟫for whom no praise. no eulogy exists,

⟪ar-quote:وَلا وَقْتٌ مَعْدُودٌ⟫for whom no time is ordained

⟪ar-quote:وَلا أَجَلٌ مَمْدُودٌ⟫and for whom no duration is fixed.

⟪ar-quote:فَطَرَ الخَلائِقَ بِقُدْرَتِهَ⟫He brought forth creation through His power,

⟪ar-quote:وَنَشَرَ الرِّيَاحَ بِرَحْمَتِهِ⟫He dispersed winds through His Compassion,

⟪ar-quote:وَوَتَّدَ بِالصُّخُورِ مَيَدَانَ أَرْضِهِ⟫and made firm the shaking earth with rocks.

So that's the meaning of the word Ilah. To become astonished and dumb-founded. 

Another meaning that comes from the same derivative is ⟪ar:وَلاَہَ یَلِیہُ⟫. and this means to be raised up!. Because the one who believes in Allah . he has raised himself up.  in this world and in the next world. He is the one who will be honored. in this life and the after life.

So those are some of the meanings of the word Ilah. So you see it's a VERY comprehensive term.

Let's go over these meanings again. What is an Ilah?.  An Ilah is a deity that is worshiped.He is the one who we submit our will to. An Ilah is someone who becomes the focus of our complete devotion and loyalty. Ilah is someone who we turn to for protection and refuge in desperate times. Ilah is someone we are passionately in love with. someone we are obsessed about. Ilah is someone who's glory and magnificence astounds and astonishes us. Someone we realize is so LOFTY. So beyond our capabilities of comprehension and understanding. that we would be dumb-founded. everytime we would try to approach him. An Ilah is someone we lean on.  or put our weight on.

---

Linguistic meaning of AL-ILAH

Now that we understand what the word Ilah means. now let's understand the difference between Ilah and Allah. Like I said. Allah is actually THE ILAH.

The word ILAH is generic. All its meanings can be taken in the generic sense. If you take the meaning of worship. I could worship many gods. like the Hindus do. if you take the meaning of devotion and loyalty. I can be devoted and loyal to many people. many causes. I can be devoted to many projects at the same time. In the meaning of love. there can be serveral people that I love. There can be several people I could turn to for help in desperate times.  I can lean on many things in a lifetime. So the word Ilah is a generic term that can appy to multiple entities. You understand?

But when I apply this definite article "THE" . to the word Ilah. When I add this "AL" called ⟪ar:علامت المعرفۃ⟫ in Arabic. to the word Ilah. It no longer remains generic. it becomes specific. Just like in the English language. book can mean any book. but THE BOOK means one specific book. Car can mean any car. but when you add "THE". THE CAR. It's now one specific car. Same thing here. When you add the AL. which is same as the definite article "THE" in English. When you add this AL to Ilah. Now it's no longer any generic Ilah. It is now ONE particular Ilah. It is now exclusive. It has now become Allah.

That's what Allah is. where the AL and the Ilah both fuse together to form the exclusive word ALLAH.  The Al.  adds a clause of exclusivity to this generic Ilah. You understand? . So when I say Allah. the generic Ilah. now becomes exclusive. What does that mean?.  It means.  Allah is not someone I worship. It now means Allah is the ONLY entity that I worship. It is the ONLY entity that I do Sajdah for. Allah is not just someone I'm devoted to. It is not just someone I am loyal to.  Allah means the ONLY one I am devoted to. The ONLY one I am completely loyal to.  It does not mean someone I turn to in times of desperation. Allah becomes the ONLY one I turn to in times of desperation. He's not just someone I am passionately in love with. He is the ONLY one I am obsessively and passionately in love with. He is not just one of the things I lean on. or depend on.  or put my weight on. Allah is the ONLY one I completely lean on and put my weight on.

You see how this AL. this exclusivity affects and changes the word Ilah?. And this is fundamental to our understanding of religion. Because this EXCLUSIVITY.  is the VERY concept that our Kalima is based on. La Ilaha Illah Allah. There is no Ilah. except THE ILAH. except Allah. We reject and deny all the generic Ilah. and affirm the ONE and ONLY exclusive Ilah. Our concept of Tawheed dictates that we do not believe in Allah as a diety in a hierarchy of dieties. That is not what we believe. We do not say Allah is a the ultimate diety in a hierarchy of dieties. NO!. Our concept of tawheed is that there is NO OTHER diety. ⟪ar:لا الہ⟫ . complete annhilation and extermination of all other dieties. ⟪ar:الا اللہ⟫. except THE one and only diety. which is Allah. This transferrence of Ilahiyat from generic to specific is the challenge of⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫.

### False Deities

Because we are the one's who create false gods in our lives. Think about it. We all have created false gods. generic Ilah's in our lives. in every meaning of the word.

I have chosen my desires. my caprice. my  ⟪ar:ھوی⟫. as my diety. as my Ilah. My desires is a diety that I worship. Who I constantly do Sajda do. I hand over my intellect in the hands of my desires and feelings and let it take control of me. I let that false diety rule me. I worship it . I submit to its every whim and desire. And that's why we have been given this sword of ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. With this sword of "La Ilaha". there is no diety. I cut down the idol of my desires. my caprice. my hawa. And replace it with the worship and submission to my ONE true and ONLY Allah.

There are many people I am devoted to in life. there are many people. many causes I am loyal to. But when I am placed in a situation where my devotion and my loyalty gets challenged.  and comes in conflict with my devotion and loyalty to Allah. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫.dictates that I negate and deny all my other devotion. I reject all my loyalties. and replace it with devotion and loyalty to the ONE and ONLY Allah. This is key to understand. My devotion and loyalty to Allah. is not a devotion in a hierarchy of devotions. It is the ONLY devotion and loyalty that I have. All other loyalties. are BECAUSE of my loyalty and devotion to Allah. You understand?

Similary. I am madly and passionately in love with this world. I am obsessed about it. I cannot stop thinking about it. I have made it and its pleasures a false god. I have made this world my Ilah. And now once again. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. necessitates that with the sword of La Ilaha. I cut down. reject and deny my love and obsession for this word. And target that passionate love towards the one it belongs to. and become completely obsessed about the one and only Allah.  That's Illa Allah.

I am astounded and astonished by the marvels of creation. by money.  by glory. by power. Yet another Ilah I have created. I must now replace that with ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. I must now be astonished and astounded ONLY about my creator. about my one and ONLY Allah.

There are many false gods I have created. Many Ilah that I have created. that I turn to for help. that I lean on. that I put my weight on. Now ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫.is the journey from that state of depending on false gods. to the state of ONLY turning to Allah for help in times of desperation. Only leaning on Allah. Only putting my weight on Allah.

Now understand. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. does not mean that I cannot turn to my parents or my loved ones for help. or I should not love anyone in this world other than Allah. Because that's all part and parcel of this life. It's part of Allah's design. The idea is that when confronted with Allah. in comparison with Allah. all these other relationships become false gods.

So even when I turn to someone for help. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. teaches me . that it is ONLY Allah who can help me. and the one I am turning to is only a means through which I am seeking Allah's help. Because what we end up doing is thinking that it is this person who is helping me. thus making him a false diety. we make him an Ilah. And that's where ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ comes into play. that . La Ilaha. it is not this person that is helping me. But Illa Allah . It is in fact Allah helping me through this person. You understand?

It is only Allah that can cure me of that which afflicts me. The doctor is just a  means by which Allah is curing me. But the second I see the doctor as being the one that cures. I have now turned him into a false god. into an Ilah. So now I have to use ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ . to break that idol. and place my gratitude. my hope and fear where it belongs.

Even though there are many I love in his world. but that love stems from my passionate love of Allah. I love them BECAUSE it makes Allah happy. Because in essence. Allah is the ONLY one I am passionately and obsesively in love with. 

Even though I am devoted to various poeple and various causes in life. but the origin of that devotion and loyalty comes from my devotion and loyalty to Allah. And if that devotion ever comes in conflict with my devotion to Allah. I will reject it and replace it with my devotion and loyalty to my one and only Allah.

THIS is the constant journey and the constant battle of ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. Replacing every false diety . replacing every false god that we have created. with THE ONE true diety. which is Allah.

In the previous session we talked about the meaning of Ilah and Allah. We learnt that Allah is actually the definite article "THE" applied to Ilah.  making it exclusive. But the underlying root word for Allah. is Ilah. Which is a VERY comprehensive term. and it has a slew of meanings.

My Ilah. for me. is someone I worship. someone I submit my will to.  Ilah is someone who is the focus of my complete devotion and loyalty. He is someone I turn to for protection.  and refuge in desperate times. My Ilah is someone I am passionately in love with. someone I am obsessed about. He is an entity who's glory and magnificence astounds and astonishes me. When I set out to understand him. and recognize him. I realize He is so LOFTY. so beyond my capabilities of comprehension and understanding. that I would be dumb-founded. everytime I would try to approach Him. An then finally. literally speaking. My Ilah is someone I lean on.  or put my entire weight on.

Now the usage of the word Ilah is very generic . It can be applied to mulitple entities at the same time. But when we say Allah. We add the definite Article THE to the word Ilah. and now it's no longer a generic entity. It is a VERY specific . VERY individualistic. It becomes ONE and ONLY One particular entity

And so our kalima. La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no ilah except Allah. It becomes a journey. A journey to break these idols that we create with out own hands. and apply each meaning to its true and sole owner. So

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no Ilah. except Allah. Meaning there is no other entity I worship. or submit myself to. except Allah.

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no other entity that is the focus of my complete devotion and loyalty. except Allah.

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no other entity that I turn to.  for protection.  and for refuge in desperate times. except Allah

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no other entity that I am passionately in love with. and obsessed about. except Allah

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no other entity that I am passionately in love with. and obsessed about. except Allah

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no other entity whose loftiness and glory. astonishes me. astounds me. startles and dazes me. whose loftiness overwhelms me.  except Allah

La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no other entity that I will put my weight on . that I will lean on completely . except Allah

This is the journey of La Ilaha Illa Allah. It's a very difficult journey. And every journey requires provisions. that helps you get through the journey. And the provision for this journey is knowledge of Allah. The more knowledge we have of Allah. the more we will be amazed by his glory. the more amazed and astonished we get. the more passionate our love will become for him. The more passionately we love him. the more we will become obsessed about him. The more we're obsessed about him the more we will worship him. and submit to his comamnds. The more we worship him. the more we will turn to him seeking his refuge. The more we find ourselves under his powerful shelter. the more we will lean on Him. the more we will put our weight on him.

And so Allah means ALL these things together. all at the same time. And this is the perfection of the Arabic language. There is SO much depth to the Arabic language which SO many people. including Arabs. don't appreciate. Because many Arabs have this compounded ignorance when it comes to the Arabic language. Just because they can speak dialectical Arabic. They make some assumptions about the language which are not true at all. And there are many Arabs who don't understand the subtleties.  and they really miss some of the extraordinary nuances of the Quran and rhetoric.
⟪ar:بلاغۃ معانی بدیعۃ والبیان⟫. These sciences really open up the power of the Quran to the person who studies it.

Now in the Arabic language if you look. That is a word that the ancient Arabs used.  for the non-arabs. They called them ⟪ar:عجمی⟫. Now ⟪ar:عجمی⟫. There is another word called ⟪ar:عجمی⟫. It is used in the Quran .⟪ar:بھیمۃٌ عجما⟫. Meaning dumb animal. So the word ⟪ar:عجمی⟫has come to mean that.  in the general sense. Someone who is a mute. or dumb.  But if you actually study the words Arab and Ajam. linguistically. The word ⟪ar:عجمی⟫. Comes from ⟪ar:عجمۃ⟫. Which does not mean to be dumb. It means to try by biting. To try by biting. Now if you look at the word Arab. It comes from the verb ⟪ar:عربَۃ⟫. Which means to cut. It means to cut. Or to eat fully. That's one of the meanings as well. So ⟪ar:عجمۃ⟫means to bite. Whereas ⟪ar:عربَۃ⟫means to cut. Now the difference between biting and cutting is that biting is not precise. Whereas cutting is very precise. So the nature of the Arabic language is that it is a very precise language.

Arabic is part of revelation

And in fact those who have studied Mabda Maad and Haqaiq know that Arabic is a language that was put into place. precisely so that it could absorb and consume the message of the Quran. The Quran was not revealed in one of the best languages that existed at the time. You know what I mean? I mean it's not like there were 50 languages out there.  and then from among them Allah chose Arabic because it was the best of those that existed. It's not like that. The Arabic language was specifically designed for the Quran. It was put in place before the time of the messenger. So that the Quran could be revealed in this precise language. Because the entire grammar of the Arabic language.  is based on events that occurred in the spiritual world. So this is not a language that came out off the ding-dong theory.Most languages that we have in place today are based on what they called the dingdong theory. It is actually a linguistic theory.  You can look that up. But the Arabic language is based on what's called ⟪ar:توقیفیۃ⟫. This is not a conventional language. One of the Orientalists have said that Arabic is the most artificial language that exists. All other languages are what's called pigeon languages. Where different people of original languages came together. and tried to communicate with each other. And then a new language got evolved. And this new language. was basically the mix of all these different words from different languages. For example Urdu Is a pegeon language. It is not an original language. All its words come from other languages such as Arabic and Persian and Sindhi.But Arabic on the other hand is not a pegeon language. It is not an arbitrary glutanated language. It is in a sense. a divine language. put in place for a divine message.

And so today I want to point out some of these incredible nuances and subtlties in the Arabic language. so that we can really appreciate its depth. And have some idea of how involved and sophisticated this language is. One of the most fascinating things about the Quran.  is that meanings go down to the letter itself. There is no other language that can do that. For instance you can look up a word in the Arabic language. And understand some of its meaning just by looking. at how its letters are pronounced. For example some of the great linguists of the Arabic language like Ibnul Faris. they've documented this entire science based on phoenotics. based on how letters sound.

So you take a word.  for instance like ⟪ar:نَفَسَ⟫. Nafasaa. is a word that is based on a root which is naa and faa. And then the third letter. it changes as the root changes to give different meanings. And it's actually based on the attributes of the letter itself. So you have ⟪ar:نَفَسَ⟫which means to blow or to breathe. And then you have ⟪ar:نفث⟫. Which is to blow lightly. Now if you observe the phenotic difference . between how the letters ⟪ar:س⟫and ⟪ar:ث⟫are pronounced. . ⟪ar:س⟫as pronounced in a very normal tone. Just like breathing. On the other hand ⟪ar:ث⟫is pronounced very softly. And therefore when it is added to the same root of Na and Faa. The meaning changes to become.  to blow softly. Because of the pronunciation of the letter ⟪ar:ث⟫. It's soft.

And then you have ⟪ar:نفح⟫. Which means breeze. breeze of the winds. So you get the ⟪ar:ح⟫sound . Which is in ⟪ar:ریح⟫. meaning winds. The sound that the winds make.  is in the pronunciation of the letter ⟪ar:ح⟫itself. ⟪ar:ریح⟫. You can hear the wind in the letter ⟪ar:ح⟫. This is incredible stuff. This is not a dingdong theory.  this is truly a divine language . It's amazing.

And then you have the word ⟪ar:نفخ⟫. Which is ⟪ar:استعلاء⟫. It is a very strong letter because of how the letter ⟪ar:خ⟫is pronounced . And because of the force in the letter khaa.  ⟪ar:نفخ⟫means to blow with forcefully. Now if you observe.  the sound the letter ⟪ar:خ⟫makes. It is explosive. Like a blast. ⟪ar:خ⟫. And it contains friction in it. It has a bang to it. And that's why you have the word . ⟪ar:خلق⟫. Which also begins with the letter ⟪ar:خ⟫and it means to create. Khalaq means to create. As Allah said.

⟪ar-quote:ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضَ⟫

Why is that? Because creation took place with a Big Bang. Right? Singularity exploded into this universe with the Big Bang. That is the ⟪ar:خ⟫in the word ⟪ar:خلق⟫.

So you have four words. ⟪ar:نَفَسَ⟫. nafasa. nafaHA. and nafaKHA. All taking meaning from the sound of the last letter. And you will find this throughout the Arabic language. It is very sophisticated in the way that Allah has designed. I mean you can't make this stuff up. It's just too incredible!! And these are signs of Allah. These are signs of Allah. placed into the very fabric of the one thing that was given to human beings. that was not give to any other creation. Language! Right?
⟪ar-quote:سَنُرِيهِمْ آيَتِنَا فِى ٱلأٓفَاقِ وَفِىٓ أَنفُسِهِمْ حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّهُ ٱلْحَقُّ⟫

We will show them . and keep showing them . our signs in the horizons and in their souls. until it becomes clearly manifest to them. that this message is the truth. These linguistic dimensions of the Quran are signs to prove that this is in fact a divine message.

### KALMIA is made from ILAH

Now if you look at the word Allah.We see that it is made up of two syllabels formed by a combination of three letters. Two Syllabels. All-Laah. And three letters. Alif. Laam. and Haa. Allah. Now look at how these words are pronounced. So you have 3 letters. Alif. Laam and Ha. The Alif or the Hamza.  is at the deepest articulation of the throat. The name of Allah is emanating from the point at which human vocalization is possible. It's coming from the depths of the vocal tract. And when you say Allah. It goes back to the Haa. Which is also at the depth of the vocal tract. Both the Hamza and Haa. are what's called Huroof AlHalq. Letters of the throat. Because they are articulated from the base of the vocal tract.  So the word Allah begins from the depths of the throat and it returns to the depths of the throat. But in the midst of it. You have the letter Laam. Which is articulated from the ceiling of the mouth. or the Lisaan. Look where you have to touch your tongue to pronounce the Laam correctly. This ceiling of your mouth. Now this is incredible. The name of Allah begins from the depth of the throat. goes all the way to the ceiling of the mouth. and then returns back to the same depth. It covers the entire spectrum of vocalization. From bottom to the top. And then back to the bottom. The entire spectrum is covered by the name Allah. Because he is the one that encompasses all. This is incredible stuff. Even the way his name is pronounced. points to his glory and magnificence!

And then some scholars have pointed out that. one of the things in the Greek language. Lu-Laan. Is a Greek word which means to soothe or to comfort. And it has been recognized throughout history that the Laa sound is a soothing and a comforting sound. Especially for children. And that's where you get the word Lullaby. And you get La La. This is what mothers sing to children. La La La La La la la. Because babies find it comforting. Why? Because it is a soothing sound. It brings a kind of tranquility (Sakeena) to the heart. So the name of Allah. Is actually something that brings tranquility and peace to the heart of a human being. when they say Allah. And also you'll find most meditations are based on the sound La. Because they believe it connects all the Meridian channels in the body. when you do that as a regular practice.

Now if look at our Kalima that our entire religion is based on. La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is constant repetition of the sound La. Because this is a sound of tranquility. Because it is a sound of comfort. Just as our religion. Islam. is a religion of peace and a religion of tranquility and comfort. And it's truly amazing.  that Allah  has developed his entire Kalima. Based on this comforting sound. Anybody in the world can recite this Kalima.

And then this Kalima . this statement. has 4 words.  made up of 12 letters. La . Ilaha. Illa. and Allah. But what's amazing is that this entire Kalima.  is made up of just three letters. Alif. Laam and Ha. And what word do these three letters combine to form? Ilahun. And when you recite the kalima. what are you saying? . La Ilaha Illah Allah. There is no Ilah. except Allah. And you're doing it.  with the very letters.  that make up the name Allah.

Allah is using the three letters of his name. Alif Laam and Ha.  to form this extremely eloquent statement. that is the basis of his entire divine revelation. This is just too perfect to be a coincidence. There is just too much perfection here. for it to be a random coincidence. Who can do this? Do you think any human being. individually or collectively is capable of this kind of perfection? It's impossible. This is clear proof that this is indeed a divine message. that is from Allah AWJ.

### All combinations of Allah are found in Quran

[diagram: Calligraphic decomposition diagram of the Arabic word 'الله' (Allah). Top-left box: the full 'الله'. To the right and below: the same word shown stripped progressively to 'الله', 'اله', 'له', 'ه'. Bottom-right box: the constituent letters 'ا ل ه' (alif, lam, ha).]
  (see ../images/002.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:الله · اله · له · ه · ال · ل · ه⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical diagram showing how the divine name decomposes letter-by-letter into ا ل ہ, central to Ismaili numerological-theological lessons on the divine name.

Another fascinating fact about this name "ALLAH". is that it is the ONLY.  most perfect.  4 letter name that exists in the world.  in the sense that no matter which letter you eliminate. it's meaning does not change. Normally in any language. when you start eliminating letters from a name. it's meaning changes.  For example "Jameel". it means beautiful. You take out the YA from it. it becomes Jamal. which means camel. You take out the Jeem. what's left behind is میل  which means dirt. You take out Meem. it becomes Jail. So no matter which name you choose. as soon you begin eliminating letters from it.  it's meaning starts changing.  But Allah is such a unique and amazing name. that no matter which letter you eliminate.  it's meaning does not change. And every variation . points to Allah Himself through an ayah of the Quran.

If I call his name Allah with all four letter. ⟪ar:ا ل ل ہ⟫. the Quran says.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّنِىٓ أَنَا ٱللَّهُ لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّآ أَنَا۠ فَٱعْبُدْنِى وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ لِذِكْرِىٓ ‎⟫. No doubt I am Allah. There is no Ilah except myself. Worship me and establish prayer to remember me

If I remove the first Alif. then what's left behind is ⟪ar:للہ⟫and the Quran says.

⟪ar-quote:لِلَّهِ مُلْكُ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ⟫. For Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth

If I remove the first laam. then what's left behind is Ilah. and the Quran says.

⟪ar-quote:وَهُوَ ٱلَّذِى فِى ٱلسَّمَآءِ إِلَهٌۭ وَفِى ٱلْأَرْضِ إِلَهٌۭ⟫. And he is the Ilah in the heavens and the Ilah in the earth

If I remove the first  alif and the first laam. what's left behind is ⟪ar:لہ⟫and the quran says.

⟪ar-quote:لَهُۥ مُلْكُ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ⟫. For him belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth

and if I drop everything. I drop the first alf, the first laam, the second laam.  and just leave behind the last Ha with its sound of Pesh on it. Hu . the Quran says.

⟪ar-quote:لَّآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ⟫

. There is no diety except Him

So Hu points to Allah. Lahu points to Allah. Ilah points to Allah. Lillah points to Allah. and Allah is Allah Himself. Every single variation of His name.  referenced by the Quran itself. All pointing to Allah himself SubhanAllah! What a magnificent word Allah chose to name himelf.
