[diagram: Numerological teaching diagram of 'la ilaha illa Allah'. Top-right green box shows the kalima with letter-spelling below it. Red 786 (the conventional numeric value of the basmala) sits left, with the equation 'بسم + الله + الرحمن + الرحیم → 7+8+6 = 21 → 2+1 = 3' linking the 3-letter-count to Allah's three names and three letters. To the right, individual letters ل / ا / ہ are shown with numeric value 5 each.]
  (see ../images/003.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:لا اله الا الله · بسم + الله + الرحمن + الرحیم · ل ال ہ ال ال ل ہ · ال ہ · ل · ا · ہ⟫
  *Note:* Numerological/letter-mysticism analysis tying the basmala's 786, the kalima's letter count, and the divine name's three-letter core.

You know in Arabic. there is a number attached to each individual letter. Alif is 1. Ba is 2. Jeem is 3 and so on. It's called Ilm AlAdad. The knowledge of numbers.  That's how you get the number 786 for Bismillah. If you add up the weight. or the number assigned to every single letter in the basmallah. it comes out to be 786. La Ilaha Illa Allah comes out to 165.  Ali comes out to be 110. Muhammad comes out to be 92. And that's why these numbers are sometimes used in place of the name itself.

Now the name Allah. has 2 syllabels and 3 letters.right? The 2 syllabels.  All--Laah. and the 3 letters. Alif Laam and Ha. Two and three is five. If you look at the number of times the 2 letters Alif and Laam are repeated in the Kalima. They are both repeated exactly 5 times. . .  The letter Ha is repeated twice. and those of you who know the Ilm Al-Adad. What's the weight of the letter Ha? What's the number assigned to the letter Ha? It's 5. And it's repeated twice in the Kalima. Once to balance out the Ilah and again to balance out the Laam. both of which are repeated 5 times.

Look at the number for Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem. Those of you who understand IlmAl-Adad. What's the total for Bismillah?  It comes out to 786. Now what is the sum of these 3 numbers? What is 7 + 8 + 6? .  It is 21 . It is 2 and 1 . And if you look at Bismillah AlRehaman AlRaheem. It has the one primary name of Allah. followed by this 2 attributes. 2 and 1. . And then what is 2 + 1? It's 3. The three letters Alif Laam and Ha. used to make up the name Allah. This is beyond incredible. Everything is connected with everything else in such mathematical perfection. And what I'm telling you is just the tip of the iceberg. There is SO much more that exists in these ayats. mathematically!. There is so much mathematical proof that exists in these ayats. that it elevates this message.  far beyond the shadow of any doubt.  that this could be manufactured by any human mind. It's impossible!

[diagram: Numerological diagram of the kalima 'la ilaha illa Allah'. Header shows the four constituent words with abjad letter-values (66, 32, 36, 31) summing to 99 inside a flower-shaped marker. Below, an exploding red star labelled '165' splits into the values 5, 60, 1, mapping to the 12 letters ل ل ہ ا (read individually). Connects 99 (sum of the four words) and 165 (letter-by-letter sum).]
  (see ../images/004.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:لا اله الا الله · ل ال ہ ال ال ل ہ⟫
  *Note:* Numerological breakdown of the shahada — 4 words = 99 (the famous '99 names'), 12 letters = 165 (which equals 11 × 15 or relates to the Imams).

Now if you add up the numbers of La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no Ilah except Allah. Now we know that Allah has 99 attributes. which are called اسماء اللہ الحسنی. Now look at this diagram of the kalima. Look at the weight of the numbers that make up La Ilaha and Illa. 31 + 36 + 32. They come out to be 99. You have And what's remaining? Allah! You have Allah and his 99 attributes.

Now what is the weight of the word Allah?. It's 66.  What is 6+6? 12!. How many letters is the kalima made up of? 12 letters! SubhanAllah! What's the weight of the entire kalima? 165, right? What is 1+6+5 ? It's also 12.

Now if you look at the numbers that make up the weight of the word Allah. You have 1 for Alif. 30+30 which is 60 for the two Laams. and then 5 for the Ha. Now in Ilm Al-Adad. when you have a number greater than 10. you take the primary number and separate it out from the number of times it is repeated. So for example you have 60 for the two laams. which is actually 6 repeated 10 times. So the primary number is 6. So now if you reduce it what numbers do you get? You get 1 for Alif, 6 for the two laams and 5 for the haa. which are the exact same numbers for the weight of La Ilaha Illah Allah. 1 6 5. in the same order.

This is just incredible. miraculous stuff. Who can come up with this kind of perfection? . This is truly Allah's words in action.

⟪ar-quote:سَنُرِيهِمْ آيَتِنَا فِى ٱلأٓفَاقِ وَفِىٓ أَنفُسِهِمْ حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّهُ ٱلْحَقُّ⟫

We will keep showing them our signs in the horizons and in their souls. until it becomes clearly manifest to them. that this message is the truth. SubhanAllah!

<!-- section 3 (id=5736, raw_sort=3): Being and Attributes -->
We are studying the first ayah of Surah AlFateha. which is the Basmallah. بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم. With the name of Allah. the intensely merciful. the consistently merciful. And we're studying the meaning of the word Allah in this statement. which comes from the word Ilah. When the definite article "THE" is applied to the word Ilah.  it becomes exclusive. And you get the word Allah. 

So then my Allah is the one I should completely submit to. the one I should be completely loyal to

⟪ar-quote:كَذَٰلِكَ يُتِمُّ نِعْمَتَهُ عَلَيْكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُسْلِمُونَ⟫

I will complete my blessings on you if you submit to me

My Allah is someone I turn to for protection and refuge in desperate times.

⟪ar-quote:وَإِمَّا يَنْزَغَنَّكَ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ نَزْغٌ فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ⟫

And if an evil whisper comes to you from Shaytan, then seek refuge in Allah. Indeed, He is All-Hearing and All-Knowing.

My Allah is then someone I am passionately in love with. someone I am obsessed about.

⟪ar-quote:قُلْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تُحِبُّونَ اللَّهَ فَاتَّبِعُونِي يُحْبِبْكُمُ اللَّهُ⟫

Oh Muhammad. Say to them. If you should love Allah , then follow me, [so] Allah will love you and forgive you your sins. And Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

My Allah is the one who's glory and magnificence astounds and astonishes me. When I set out to understand him. and recognize him. I realize He is so LOFTY. so beyond my capabilities of comprehension and understanding. that I would be dumb-founded. everytime I would try to approach Him.

⟪ar-quote:قُل لَّوْ كَانَ ٱلْبَحْرُ مِدَادًۭا لِّكَلِمَتِ رَبِّى لَنَفِدَ ٱلْبَحْرُ قَبْلَ أَن تَنفَدَ كَلِمَتُ رَبِّى وَلَوْ جِئْنَا بِمِثْلِهِۦ مَدَدًۭا⟫

Say, "If the sea were ink for [writing] the words of my Lord, the sea would be exhausted before the words of my Lord were exhausted, even if We brought the like of it as a supplement.

Then finall. My Allah is the one I lean on.  or put my entire weight on.

⟪ar-quote:إِن يَنصُرْكُمُ ٱللَّهُ فَلَا غَالِبَ لَكُمْ ۖ وَإِن يَخْذُلْكُمْ فَمَن ذَا ٱلَّذِى يَنصُرُكُم مِّنۢ بَعْدِهِۦ ۗ وَعَلَى ٱللَّهِ فَلْيَتَوَكَّلِ ٱلْمُؤْمِنُونَ⟫

If Allah helps you, none can overcome you: If He forsakes you, who is there, after that, that can help you? in Allah alone, then, Let believers put their trust.

So these are all the different meanings of the word Ilah. that applies exclusively to Allah when a definite article "THE" is applied to Ilah.  But of all these meanings. the most prominent and the most loft meaning is that

My Allah is the one I worship and obey.

⟪ar-quote:إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ⟫

It is You we worship and You we ask for help
⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ ٱعْبُدُوا۟ رَبَّكُمُ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَكُمْ وَٱلَّذِينَ مِن قَبْلِكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَّقُونَ⟫

O mankind, worship your Lord, who created you and those before you, that you may become righteous

[diagram: Teaching diagram about worship. A central green box reads 'عبادۃ / Worship', pointing upward with a red arrow to '(الله) معبود' (Allah, the Worshiped). Below, two callouts branch from worship: 'WORSHIP — Specific Religious Obligations at specific time intervals' and 'OBEDIENCE — All the time'.]
  (see ../images/005.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:الله (معبود) · عبادۃ⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical diagram distinguishing 'ibada (worship rituals at fixed times) from broader obedience (continuous).

So the word used here is ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫. which is commonly translated as worship. But the word actually means two things. The word ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫. means to worship and also to obey. both at the same time. And the Ilah. that is worshipped and obeyed. the one ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫is done for. is called ⟪ar:معبود⟫. The one who is worshipped AND obeyed.  And these words are not interchangable like in the English language. Instead they're both embedded inside one word in arabic inside the word ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫.

If you open any English Quran. A lot of oversimplified translations say there is no one worthy of worship except allah. right? thats the common translation. No one worthy of worship except Allah.  And when we think of the word worship. what comes to mind? . 5 prayers. fasting. zakaat etc. right? Those are all different forms of worship.  And we think that's it. We stop at those activities. And that's the point I want to highlight today. That the problem with this translation of the word Ibadah. in the meaning of worship. it does not necessarily include the concept of obedience . And especially obedience that stems out of love and trust. Because the word obedience can have a very negative connotation attached to it. people can be forced into obedience. Children are often bullied into obedience by the use of threats or worse. So sometimes obedience can have a very negative emotion attached to it. This is not the kind of obedience we're talking about here. We're talking abou the obedience that comes naturally from the product of all these definitions of Ilah. When you love someone passionately. you're obsessed about that person. when you are completely devoted and loyal to that person. when you can completely lean on that person. put your entire weight on that person knowing that he will not let you fall. When you're so impressed and amazed by the loftiness of that person's greatness. his magnificence. When you know that's the only person you can turn to for protection and refuge. Then what natrually comes out. of the product of all these emotions. is obedience. An obedience that stems from love. A lover's obedience. to make his beloved happy. One that is based on passionate love. complete and unshakable trust. You understand?

So ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫. and specifically ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫to an ⟪ar:الہ⟫.  has these two concepts embedded within it. worship AND obedience. both of which stem out of passionate love and not out of force or compulsion.

Now let's understand this concept of obedience. from the quranic point of view. I want you to observe the usage of the word Ilah in these ayahs. In the story of Moosa AS. one of the things Firon told his generals was.
⟪ar-quote:وَقَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلْمَلَأُ مَا عَلِمْتُ لَكُم مِّنْ إِلَهٍ غَيْرِى⟫

When they saw Moosa AS coming up.  and Firon noticed his authority over his generals weakening.  he said I don't see anyone else as an Ilah for you besides myself. Now when a king is talking to his generals and calling himself Ilah. is he thinking worship or obedience? He doesn't need them to make dua to him right now. What does he need? he needs their obedience . So in this ayah. the word ilah is being used in the context of obedience.

Then there is the ayah
⟪ar-quote:أَرَءَيْتَ مَنِ ٱتَّخَذَ إِلَهَهُۥ هَوَىٰهُ⟫

Have you seen the one who has taken his desires as his Ilah?

Lets make a list of some desires. Someone has some temptations, somebody has greed.  somebody is being offered a very lucrative haram business opportunity . .  they have that desire. to become rich. to become powerful. 

Now do people make a statue out of money. or power.  and then go and worship it? what do people do with their desires? they obey them! They have a scratch and they itch it.  like the ad for sprite says. obey your thirst.  The idea is when you have a temptaiton you don't worship it.  you obey it. .  Now sometimes one of those shades of meaning takes control over the other. but in some respect they are both present.

So now when we use the word Allah. which means THE Ilah. We now have a different meaning. He is the entity that is to be worshiped. AS WELL AS obeyed. And to put it in parctical terms. why are these two things important? . Lets say we are about to pray in 15 minutes. It's Fajr in 15 minutes and we have to do ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫. Now what kind of ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫is that considered? Worship or obedience?.  Worship, right?

But from then from Fajr until Zohr.  we may not be worshipping Him.  but we better be doing what? Obeying Him! . Between two prayers you and I are not necessarily worshipping Him.  but we better still be obeying Allah AWJ .  and this is why the concept of ibadah in islam is so comprehensive. You go and earn a halaal income by your job.  that is an act of obedience. You go to school and you sincerly accomplish the purpose of going to school. That's ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫. that's obedience of Allah. You obey. love and respect your parents. that's ⟪ar:عبادۃ⟫. You are kind to your siblings. generous to the needy. respectful to the elders. Those are all acts of servitude and slavery to allah SWT. Those are all acts of Ibadah.

And when it's time for salaah. and we stand before him in prayers. That is an act of woship. and that too is Ibadah. So you see Ibadah. is a very comprehensive term. And the concept of the word Allah. the one we do Ibadah for. is the one we constantly worship. and He is the one we are constantly in obedience to.

---

Now that we have some understanding of the name Allah. it's time to talk about His 99 attributes. I sent you this image in the previous session in which I showed you how La Ilaha Illa Allah has Allah and His 99 attributes .

[diagram: Duplicate of image 004 — numerological diagram of the kalima with 99 (four-word sum), 165 (letter sum), and 12-letter breakdown.]
  (see ../images/006.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:لا اله الا الله · ل ال ہ ال ال ل ہ⟫
  *Note:* Duplicate of image 004 in this chapter.

There is one thing I forgot to mention. which I'd like to now since we're on the topic. I showed you last time that the weight of the kalima. La Ilaha Illa Allah is 165. based on Ilm Al-Adad presented by Imam Jaffar AsSadiq AS. Now if you look at the numbers that make up the weight of the word Allah. You have 1 for Alif. 30+30 which is 60 for the two Laams. and then 5 for the Ha. Now in Ilm Al-Adad. when you have a number greater than 10. you take the primary number and separate it out from the number of times it is repeated. So for example you have 60 for the two laams. which is actually 6 repeated 10 times. So the primary number is 6. So now if you reduce it what numbers do you get? You get 1 for Alif, 6 for the two laams and 5 for the haa. which are the exact same numbers for the weight of La Ilaha Illah Allah. 1 6 5. in the same order.

Anyway. So Allah has 99 attributes. Commonly asked questions are.  what are these attributes? Does HE need these attributes.  or do WE need these attributes to understand him? So let's begin with a very basic undertanding of name and attributes. This is actually a very complicated topic. So today I just want to give a basic understanding of the difference between the name Allah and his 99 attributes. The concept of name and attributes is the same concept as noun and adjectives. And the combination of the two. help us understand the entity itself. right?

[diagram: Teaching diagram contrasting Soul and Body. Two human silhouettes (yellow on left = Soul, black on right = Body), both labelled 'ZAAT (noun)' and connected by a 'NAMED (John Doe)' arrow. Spiritual attributes (brave, kind, Doctor, patient) point to the soul; physical attributes (Slim, Dark, Handsome, Tall) point to the body. Bottom green box: 'ک + مثلہ' (the Quranic ka- + mithlihi).]
  (see ../images/007.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:ذات (noun) · ک + مثلہ⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical setup for the kalam discussion of how the Quranic phrase 'laysa ka-mithlihi shay' (Q42:11) negates both substance (zat) and attribute (sifa) likeness between God and creatures.

If we desire to gain a complete understanding or comprehension of an entity . scholars state that we need to understand its attributes. If we understand all the attributes of an entity. we understand the entity itself. In other words. to understand the noun.  I need to understand all its adjectives. and my knowledge of attributes is directly proportional to my knowledge or awareness of the entity itself. If I gain a partial understanding of the attributes. I will have a partial understanding of the entity.   I will still have some understanding. but it will be incomplete. 

This.  in Arabic is called ⟪ar:ذات⟫and ⟪ar:صفات⟫. Zaat is the "being". or the "entity" itself. and Siafaat are the attributes of that being or entity.  We as Human-BEINGS. we are a composite of a spirit and body.  So I have a soul and I have a body.  and these two things together is called "Zaat". and then each of these components have attributes. My soul has certain spiritual attributes. and my body has certain physical attributes. Once I have recognized the attributes and capabilities of my soul. I have essentially gained an awareness of the capabilities of my soul itself. Just as once I recognize and understand the attributes of my body. I understand my body. By understanding the Sifaat. I can understand the Zaat itself.

What you and I refer to in the first person. When I say. I am Asif. The "I" that I'm referring to is my Zaat. or my being.  You understand? It is always the Zaat. the being.  that is named. Asif is the name of my being . my essence. My being is the actual entity.  that is being identified by the name Asif.

If I'm meeting you for the first time. and we've never met before. and I introduce myself as . AsSalaamAlaykum. I am a teacher.  You will respond. WalaykumAsSalaam. you are also a weirdo. right? Because you don't introduce yourself by your attributes. You introduce yourself by your name. the name given to your existence.

Now attributes or sifaat are things that further describe your zaat. Does that make sense?

So for example if we know there is a guy named Zaid. we understand that the name of hiz zaat.  his being.  is Zaid. We can identify his being through his name.  and then we can get additional information about him.  through his spiritual and physical attributes.  Attributes that describe who Zaid is. He is intelligent. he is smart. he is witty. he has a fair complexion. he is slim. he is a tennis player. he is a brother. a son. a husband.  he is brave. he is handsome etc. 

Now between the being and its attributes. what is the essential entity?.  Between Zaat and Sifaat. which is the key thing?.  It's obviously Zaat. All these additional pieces of information that we have about Zaid. they only exist.  because Zaid himself exists. If there is no Zaid.  none of the attributes can exist.  Adjectives only exist. because the noun exists. If there is no noun. there can be no adjectives for that noun. You understand? So between the two things. the key element is Zaat. the entity itself. that is given a name. Zaid

Now let's say . we're having a conversation. and I say. Hey . Did you hear about Zaid. Now as soon as I said Zaid. assuming we're both talking about the same Zaid. just by the mention of his name. all his attributes just flash through your mind. don't they? Just by hearing Zaid's name. you know I'm talking about the Zaid who is intelligent. smart. has a fair complexion. is a tennis player. etc. So just by mentioning the name Zaid. I've essentially mentioned all his 52 attributes.

---

So it's the same thing with Allah. We know that a diety exists. and if He exists. He has a being. or a zaat. and that being needs to have a nam.   so that it can be identified. And therfore for the identification of his being. he chose the name Allah! Allah is the name of his Zaat. His being.  And this is the name . this name Allah. is how he introduced himself to us in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّنِىٓ أَنَا ٱللَّهُ لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّآ أَنَا۠⟫

No doubt. I am Allah. or I am THE ILAH.  There is not Ilah except me.

And then once there is a Zaat. there will obviously be what? Sifaat. Where there is a noun there are always going to be adjectives. So the name Allah. has 99 adjectives. 99 descriptions of who Allah is. Who is Allah? He is AlRehman. the intensely mercifuly. Who is Allah? He is AlRaheem the constantly merciful. Who is Allah? He is AlMalik. the king. Who is Allah? He is AlAzeez. the powerful. so there are 99 attributes.  or 99 adjectives that describe who Allah is. 

But the word Allah is the primary name. the name of the being. that encompasses in itself.  all the 99 attributes. The 99 attributes exist.  ONLY because Allah exists.  Just like when I said Zaid. all his attributes were included in his name.  Similarly when I say Allah. it is equivalent to my saying

⟪ar-quote:الرحمن، الرحيم، الملك، القدوس، السلام، المؤمن، المهيمن، العزيز، الجبار، المتكبر، الخالق، البارئ، المصور، الغفَّار، القهَّار، الوهَّاب ، الرزَّاق ، الفتَّاح ، العليم، القابض، الباسط، الخافض، الرافع، المعز، المذل، السميع، البصير، الحكم، الحکیم، العادل، اللطيف، الحلیم، الخبير، العظيم، الغفور، الشكور، العلي، الكبير، الحفيظ، الحسيب، الكريم، المقیم، الرقیب، الجلیل،  المجيب، الواسع، الودود، المجيد، الباعث، الشهيد، الوكيل، القوى، المتين، الولي، الحميد، المحصى، المبدئ ، المعيد، المحيي، المميت، الحي، القيوم، الواجد، الماجد، الواحد، الصمد، القادر، المقتدر، المقدِّم، المؤخر، الأول، الآخر، الظاهر، الباطن، الوالي، المتعال، البِر، التواب، المنتقم، العفو، الرؤوف، المالك الملك، ذو الجلال و الإكرام، المقسط، الجامع، الغني، المغني، المانع، الضار، النافع، النور، الهادي، البديع، الباقي، الوارث، الرشيد، الصبور ، الحنان، المنان، الدیان، البرھان،⟫

All these attributes. All these 99 attributes. are combined within this one name Allah! . That's why when we refer to Him by his name Allah. just by the mention of His name. we are mentioning All his attributes. You understand?

So in order for you to understand. I'm going to use a metaphore. But understand that this is just a metaphor. So don't confuse this with anything other than a metaphor.

If you look at light. We know that light is white. They call it white light. White light does not have a color. Now what happens.  is that if you get a prism. A prism is a medium of glass. And when this light. this white light.  when it hits the glass it refracts. It bends. There is a bending of the light. And then what happens is that the color spectrum shows up. You see a whole spectrum of colors. From violate to red and everything in between.

This is exactly the same thing that happens with creation. You have the light of Allah SWT. Because he is ⟪ar:اللہ نور السموت والارض⟫. . He is the light of the heavens and the earth. But what happens.  is when this light of Allah hits His creation. the divine attributes refract. in creation. So you get all of these different manifestations of Allah SWT's essence. That are manifesting in his creations. So in one instance you see that Allah is Kareem (the generous). And in another instance he is Jabbar (the compeller). In another instance he is Qahhar (the subduer). And another instance he is Azeez (the powerful). In another instance he is Muzil (the humiliator). In another he is Moiz (the bestower of honor). And he is.  all of these attributes. all at the same time.

We can only see these attributes one at a time in creation. Because they are a refraction of the divine essence of Allah. within his creation. So we see these individually. But Allah is all of these attributes. all at the same time. Just as a white light is all the seven colors.  at the same time.

So this world. then becomes a theatre.  for the  divine manifestations of these attributes. And this is how we come to know Allah. Not directly through him. But through his creations.

⟪ar-quote:لا تفکر فی اللہ . ولاکن تفکر فی خلق اللہ⟫

Don't reflect upon Allah. Instead reflect upon the creations of Allah. And as Maulana Ali said.

⟪ar-quote:العجز عن درك الإدراك إدراك . والبحث عن ذاتِهِ كُفرُ وإشراك⟫

The inability to know Allah IS the true understanding of Allah. And to try to discuss the essence of Allah is Shirk. It is assigning partners with them. It is shirk

And accepting our inability to know Allah IS the true comprehension of Allah. which is why the essential act of worship in Islam. is putting our intellects on the ground. And surrendering the capacity of the intellect to know Allah.

So the divine essence of Allah. refracts when it hits His creation. and splits into these 99 attributes. Because that is the only way . in which we can know Allah.  through the attributes of his creation. We know mercy because we have seen mercy in his creation. We know of generosity. because we have seen generosity in his creation. We know revenge. because we have seen that attribute within his creation. If that were not the case. there was no way for us to understand this concept of mercy. of generosity. of love. of abasement. of honor. of victory . of protection. Because we. as human beings.  need some practical example of that attribute in action for us to understand.

But these attributes within creation can cause confusion for us. Just as the components of white light can cause confusion. How can white light. be violet, Indigo, blue, green, yellow, orange and red at the same time?. Because Allah is Kareem (the generous). but then he is also Qahhar. (the subduer). He is Rehman and Raheem (Intensely merciful and consistently merciful). but he is also AlMuntaqim. the avenger. So how can these two attributes exist at the same time? How can someone who is Kareem. who is benevolent. how can he be Qahhar and Jabbar (the compeller) at the same time. How can Qahar. be Rahman. How can the subduer be intensely merciful at the same time. This seems like a paradox to us. But that's the very nature of the essence of Allah. He is all of those things.  all at the same time. 

So I'll give you an example. Rain. The Kareem . the benevolent. brings rain. as his mercy. But then he can use the same rain to deliver Azaab. He can use the same medium to deliver his wrath. causing floods and death and destruction. It's the same medium. Rain. In once instance it can be a source of Rehmah. of mercy . bringing life. But in another instance. he can use the same rain. and make t a manifestation of his Azaab. He can use it to bring death and destruction. As a scholar said.

⟪ar-quote:اِذَا الکریمُ . تَجَلّٰی بِسمِ المُنتَقِمِ⟫

When the generous one . manifests as the avenger. Al Muntaqim. is one of the attributes of Allah. It's when Allah takes people to account. He takes people to account for their actions. But even in doing so.  he does not lose his attribute of being AlKareem. the generous. Even when he is manifesting as the avenger. He is still AlKareem. Because that's what the Kareem does. The Kareem Alqaum. the most generous of a nation. can sometimes do things.  that people do not associate with generosity. Which is called tough love. But when he is manifesting as the avenger. that does not mean that he has lost his attribute of being generous. He is manifesting as the avenger BECAUSE he is generous. Just as parents scold and discipline their children.  BECAUSE they love them. And we as human beings find that paradoxical. How can you punish me if you love me?. Well! I am punishing you.  because I love you. And this is what Allah does.

---

<!-- section 4 (id=5737, raw_sort=4): Refraction of divine attributes in creation -->
Studying Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem. And in that statement. we're looking at the highest ranking word. the Ismul Jalalah. the most majestic name of all. Allah.

We said Allah comes from the root word Ilah. with the definite article THE applied to it making it exclusive. and personal.

So then my Allah becomes the one I should completely submit to. the one I should be truly loyal to. He is someone I turn to for protection and refuge in my desperate times. He is someone I am passionately in love with. someone I am obsessed about. He is beyond my imagination. and beyond my  capabilities of comprehension and understanding. He is someone who's glory and majesty dumb-founds me. everytime I try to approach Him. He is someone I can completely trust. lean on . put my entire weight on knowing that He will not let me fall.  And finally . and most important meaning of all . He is the one I worship. And I explained last time. worship or عبادۃ  in Arabic means two things. It means worship and it means obedience. both stemming from the product of all these different meanings of the word Allah .

---

After discussing the word Allah. we started talking about his attributes. The Quran gives us 99 attributes of Allah . And so we said that there is being and there are attributes. There is zaat and there are sifaat. Noun and adjectives. Allah is the name of the being. it is the name of the essence. And whenever there is an essence. it will manifest through its attributes. And in order to understand the essence or the being itself.  we need to first understand its attributes. Because without the attributes. there is no way for us to undertand the essence.

Once we understand all the attributes.  individually and independently. We can then put all of them together . to understand the capabilities of the essence itself. And as Gestalt stated . He's this famous German psychologist. He said. the whole is greater than the sum of its parts. Because what happens is that when you combine the power of these individual parts. these individual attributes. When they all come together.  to form a complete whole. that whole takes on a reality of its own. which is now independent of the parts.

So for example. I have a body that is made up parts. both internal and external components.  I can understand what these individual parts do. The eyes can see. the ears can hear. the tongue can taste and speak. the hands can do different things. legs allow me to move. the heart does this. the liver does that.  I can understand the capabilities of all these parts individually. And no doubt. they're all powerful in their own right. Even individually. they are all capable of amazing things.

But I cannot construct a building with these parts working independently. I cannot run a business. I cannot cure patients in a hospital.  or build computers. or travel into outer space. I cannot do any of those things. just by these parts themselves.  But when I put all these parts together. and they start working together. to accomplish a unified goal. When I start using their abilities collectively. now I have a body. an existence. than can do amazing and brilliant things. Hence the whole is always greater than the sum of its parts.

---

Now in the previous session. to explain the divine essence and its attributes.  I gave you the metaphor of white light. When white light hits a prism it refracts into its respective colors. If I can understand the attributes of these 7 lights independently . I can gain a complete understanding of white light itself. And professional photogrophers understand the importance of this. especially today in digital photogrophy.  Because they have to manipulate the settings of these 7 colors. or hues.  to achieve what's called white balance.

So using that analogy. in a very broad sense. not a literal sense. When the divine essence of Allah (SUBHANHU WA TA'ALA) hits its creation. It refracts into these 99 attributes. And it is only through these attributes.  that we can understand something about His essence. Because without these attributes there is no way for us human beings. to even get a vague idea of the essence .

If someone has never seen light. Let's say a child is born in a dark cave.  and he has never ever seen light. how will you explain the concept of light to him?. You can talk about it. or describe it all you want. but even your best description of light. will not even come close to the real experience of light. isn't it? So you have to experience light. to get even some understanding of it.

And then that experience of seeing and feeling light. that too is not the experience of the actual sun. which is the source. or the creator of that light. Light is just an attribute of what the sun has created. It is simply the experience of photons. generated by the sun. right?  So even when you and I experience light. we're not experiencing the power of the sun. we're experiencing an attribute of that which the sun has produced. You understand?

So Allah placed. a tiny refraction of his divine attributes within His creation. Because Allah is SO lofty. that we human beings. we do not posess the capability of understanding Allah's attributes directly. let alone his divine essence. So he refracted his divine essence. in the attributes of His creation. so that we could experience them. These attributes that we find within his creations. are His signs . that point back to his own divine attributes. And this is how we understand and experience. or rather. gain an inadequate . or feeble understanding. of the divine attributes of Allah.

Now how do we do this? . How is it possible to understand a creator through the attributes of its creation. I'll give you an example. and again. this is just a metaphor. an analogy that I'm using to explain a concept. So I'll need you to work with me here to understand what I'm trying to explain .

Martian and ipad

We human beings. we created computers. laptops .  We created iPads. These are all OUR creation. Now let's say one of these iPads . it finds its way over to the planet Mars. A Martian finds this iPad and now as he's interacting with it. he's thinking about . who created this. Now this Martian has NEVER EVER seen a human being before. It has no idea what a human being looks like. All it has is this iPad. So now just by observing the attributes. or features of this iPad.  what could a Martian possibly know about human capabilities.

So it could see that the iPad has a screen with a display. Based on that . it could conclude that the human species have the ability to see things. The have the ability of sight. Because if they could not see.  then why would they need a display. Then it observes that the iPad has speakers.  that produces sounds. therefore it concludes that the human species must also be able to hear . And since it has a volume control. so maybe human beings are capable of hearing a range of sounds. Then it looks at the keyboard. and the way the keys are designed. and maybe reaches the conclusion that human beings must have fingers. just because of the way in which all the keys are separated out.  Then it opens up the ipad. and starts studying its architecture. He sees that the iPad (like any other computing device) operates with binary signals. on and off . 1s and 0s. Based on that it could conclude that the human mind must think logically. in terms of binary signals. Positive and negatives. Yes and no. Benefits and disadvantages.

Then it notices that the iPad is very light and portable. So he could conclude that the human beings are capable of movement. They could move from one place to another. Which means maybe they have feet. You understand? So just by observing the capabilities of the iPad. the Martian may be able to make some intelligent guesses about its creator.   This iPad has these features . therefore its creator must have these capabilities.  you understand?

But no matter how much it studies and understands the structure. the architecture. and all the features of this iPad. There is no way for it to gain a complete understanding. of what a human being looks like. or is capable of.  How he thinks. His genetic makeup. How his body functions. All of that is impossible for the Martian to conclude just based on its observations of the iPad itself. But it could certainly gain some sort of preliminary understanding about the human being. Right?

The only way.  this Martian will be able to understand more about human beings. is if a human being describes himself to it.  Right? Now let's say this same Martian finds a book on human physiology and human psychology. Now by studying it.  the Martian can understand a lot more about the human species. than it was able to decipher just by reverse engineering the iPad.  The point I'm trying to make.  is that . just by observing the features and attributes of creation.  it is not possible to understand the creator. We need a description provided by the creator himself . to supplement or facilitate that preliminary understanding . that we gained through our observation and experience of interacting with his creation.

So in this example of the Martian and the iPad. we talked about 2 things. Its experience or logical deductions about human beings.  based on its interaction with the iPad. supplemented by his knolwedge of human physiology and psychology. But even with all this. the reality is. that the Martian still CANNOT gain a complete. 100% understanding of humans. because the Martian is not human. Books and descriptions and explanations can only tell you so much.

Forget Martians. look at us. You know there is constant research being done in the fields of animal physiology. animal psychology and behavior. And these researchers claim that they barely know anything. And this is a life form that is inferior to human beings. We can't fully comprehend the inferior forms. How is it then possible to fully understand our own creator?

So I hope with this example. I have formed the basis of the conversation I want to have with you today. As human beings. in order for us to understand the creator. we need two things. An experiential interaction with the attributes of His creation. supplemented by the description of that creation.  by the creator. And finally the realization. that both of these combined together. still are not enough to fully comprehend the creator. because the whole is always greater than the sum of its parts.

Because when it comes to understanding Allah. We are nothing more than Martians.  trying to understand Allah through His iPad. which is this universe. And even though we can understanding something about the attributes of Allah. THROUGH the attributes of His creation. But we cannot . can NEVER. understand Allah completely.  That's why Maulana Ali said.

⟪ar-quote:لا تفکر فی اللہ . ولاکن تفکر فی خلق اللہ⟫

Don't reflect upon Allah. Instead reflect upon the CREATIONS of Allah.

So Allah gave us his creation. this world. that we live in and interact with. AND He gave us a description of himself. through the Quran. in which Allah described Himself to us. through his attributes. So that with the combination of the two.  We combine our experience of our interaction with the attributes of His creation. which is the Zaahir (the external form). We combine it with the description of His divine attributes . the baatin (or the interior) . in order to gain some preliminary understanding of Him. enough to be able to approach Him. move towards Him. begin our journey towards Him. But will we ever be able to reach Him?. No. That's impossible

So now let's look at how we combine the zaahir and the baatin.  So for example the Quran tells us that Allah is merciful. He is Rehman and Raheem. the intensely and consistently merciful. 

وَإِلَهُكُمْ إِلَهٌۭ وَحِدٌۭ ۖ لَّآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ

Your Ilah is one. There is no ilah except Him. He is AlRheman and AlRaheem. Intensely merciful and consistently merciful.

Then the Quran tells us that Allah is Kareem. He is generous.

يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلْإِنسَنُ مَا غَرَّكَ بِرَبِّكَ ٱلْكَرِيمِ

Oh my beloved human being. what has deceived you against your generous master?

Quran says that he is AlRazzaq.

إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ هُوَ ٱلرَّزَّاقُ ذُو ٱلْقُوَّةِ ٱلْمَتِينُ

No doubt Allah is the one who is your provider. He is of immense power and very steadfast.

### Studying attributes of this world

So Allah uses these attributes to describe Himself in the Quran. Now when we observe his creations. rain is one of His creations. Pure water that falls from the sky. which is the source of all life on this planet. And when we observe rain.  we can find a reflection. or a refraction of these same divine attributes . in rain and the sky which is the provider of rain.

Because Rehma means mercy. and mercy is shown by the powerful to the weak. Allah is العزیز الجبار . The one of great might and of great power. And we know. that mercy. is an act of compassion shown by the powerful. towards the weak. Without that act. the weak would suffer. Rain definitely has that property. the property of mercy.  If the sky would hold back it's rain. we would not be able to survive. and there is nothing that we could do about it. In even though . all we do . is keep corrupting and polluting the ozone layer. still the Raheem. the sky. it continues to bless us with its rehma . his mercy. by sending us water. So Raheem or Rehma. *mercy.*is the attribute of the sky. that sends us this mercy in abudnance. The sky is not stingy about showing its mercy. When it rains. it pours. that's generosity. that's Karam. an attribute of the kareem. So we find these attributes of Raheem and Kareem in one of Allah's creation. the sky! . And in what it produces. rain . or water. that is the source of all life.

Now this rain water is absorbed by the earth. which then produces vegetation. and vegetaton is the secondary source of life for animals and human beings. So the earth then . is reflecting the divine attribute of Razzaq . (the provider). Because it PROVIDES for the human beings and animals. It is also a manifestation of the divine attribute of AlMuqeet (the Nourisher). 

And when there is balance between the water that comes from the sky. and there is balance in the produce of the earth. There is Salaam. There is peace . there is tranquility. which is another divine attribute of the creator being reflected through His creation. SubhanAllah.  Then another thing we find abundantly in this universe. is balance. Everything is balancing out everything else. That's AlHakam. a divine reflection of the judge. The Arbitrator.

Look at the enormous size of this universe. Look at the expanse of this universe. That's a reflection of  AlAzeem (the magnificent). The ⟪ar:عالی⟫. the exalted. AlKabeer (the great). AlJaleel. the magestic. Look at the divine beauty reflected in nature. in sunrise. in sunset. on mountains . look at the beautiful colors of the sky. the raw beauty of nature. that's the Jameel. the beautiful.  manifesting Himself through his creation. Look at gravity. How it binds all creation to itself. No creation can escape the confines of gravity. Even those who temporarily can defy gravity. like the birds. What happens when they stop flapping their wings. Planes . what happens when they run out of fuel. they all eventually get subdued or compelled by gravity. why? Because He is AlJabbar. the compeller. And He is AlQahhar the subduer.

And we know today.  that human beings are the cause of every natural disaster happening all over the world. We're constantly messing with nature. which is leading to all sorts of environmental problems like global warming. over population causing depletion of natural resources. destruction of forests . Ocean acidification. increasing the acidity of the oceans that is killing ocean life. We human beings are the cause of most. if not all of the problems on this earth. Yet it takes a VERY long period of time for these problems to surface. It takes human beings to transgress against nature . and work in such selfish ways. long.  before its negative effects start showing up. Why is that? . We have to abuse our health a long time before its affects start surfacing.  Why don't these problems happen immediately? because He is Saboor (the extremely patient). He gives time. He gives relief for a long time. hoping that his creation may correct itself. Hoping that his creation may restore the balance.

But when they dont. He gets angry. and He needs to intervene.  When human beings become arrogant. and despite all the time given to them by the Saboor. they continue to inflict harm. then Allah uses THAT very creation. which they have harmed. He uses that same creation to humble them. and put them back in their place. The victim now becomes the avenger. Rain that was supposed to be a source of his mercy. can now become a source of death and destruction. The earth . actually created to sustain and nourish human beings. by the Razzaq. and the Muqeet. it can now shake and quake . and destroy everything upon it. That's the manifestation of the generous one as the avenger. AlMuntaqim

⟪ar-quote:اِذَا الکریمُ . تَجَلّٰی بِسمِ المُنتَقِمِ⟫

When the generous one . manifests as the avenger.

Warning us. Don't take advantage of my mercy. because I can get angry too. And nothing angers me more. than injustice. and when I get angry. I will put you back in your place. because I am AlHakam. (the judge). I am AlQadir. (the all able). I can do whatever I want . I am Muqtadir (the dominant).  Even though my inherint quality is ⟪ar:النافع⟫(the benefactor). But I can also be AlDarr. The distressor. the harmer.

Then we see that Everything . every creation on this planet has a life span. It originates . and then it inevitable perishes. Who created?. Who perished?. That's المبدع and المعید. The originator and the Returner. And through this temporal state of his creation. He manifested Himself as AlHaye. the ever living. By the constant state of change that he put into his creation . He manifested as AlBaqi (the Immutable). the one who never changes. SubhanAllah.

So Allah's divine attributes . are reflected THROUGH his creation. Allah sent His divine revelation . the Quran. and in that He described who He is. through his divine attributes. The ayats of Quran are his Batini signs. And then He created this entire universe around us . manifesting those divine attributes as his zaahiri . physical signs (آیات الکونی). So that we can experience the manifestation of His divine attributes through his creation. He combined the Zahir and the Batin for us. why? Because He is ⟪ar:الظاہر⟫and He is ⟪ar:الباطن⟫. SubhanAllah.

So I hope you now understand. how the divine essence of Allah. His zaat. refracts when it hits His creation. and splits into these 99 attributes. And how through the attributes of His creation . we are able to experience. a little bit. a very small fraction. of the reflection of His divine attributes. 

But what's VERY VERY VERY important to understand. is that just because we understand a little bit from the reflection of his divine attributes. through the attributes of his creation. we cannot confine him within the attributes of His creation. We cannot say that Allah is Raheem. He is Kareem. He is Salaam. just like rain . We cannot do that. We cannot say He is AlJabbar. just like gravity. Because if we do that. we are now reducing him . or bringing him down. to the level of His creation . In the example of the Martian I gave earlier. this would be similar to the Martian thinking . that human beings are like the iPad . Or that the capabilities of the iPad. truly reflect the capabilities of the human being itself. Because nothing could be further from the truth. We human beings are WAY WAY WAY more powerful and capable than the iPads we created. The iPad is just a mere reflection of our capabilities. isn't it? So it's the same thing with Allah. We cannot equate the attributes of His creation.  to his divine attributes. The mercy we see in this universe through this creation. is NOTHING like Allah's mercy . His mercy is WAY beyond comprehension. What we are seeing is nothing more than a tiny reflection.  of a fraction of his divine mercy. His mercy is incomprehensible. His powers are incomprehensible. His majesty. His magnificence. His compassion. His love. His generosity. His divinity. is WAY WAY WAY beyond anything we can ever comprehend .

This is really important to understand. because we are VERY limited in the mental images we can create.  So when we looked at the attributes of the sky for example. we got a point of reference . a mental concept of this attribute called mercy. for generosity . for peace and tranquility. So rain is merciful. But how merciful? Human beings are merciful . but how merciful? merciful like the rain?. If not. then merciful like who? like me? like you? like Him? Like her? Like them? What is the level of Allah's mercy. What is the most most most merciful creation you can imagine? Is Allah merciful like that creation?  If yes! then we just brought Allah . down to the level of THAT creation. because now that thing or that person is equal or a partner in this mercy of Allah . Rain and Allah become EQUALLY merciful . And that is the very definition of Shirk. To associate partners with Allah. That's Shirk.  You understand?

And this is the shirk we are constantly negating . and purifying Allah . through our kalima. This is what subhan Allah means. Subhan comes from the word Sabh. which means great distance or being far from something. Also the word sabaha. which means to swim. Because when someone is swimming. they are always on top. there is always a distance between him and the bottom of the ocean. And from the same root word we get the word Tasbeeh. Creating a distance between Allah and his 99 attributes. Look at what we do in our daily tasbeeh. 33 times we affirm AllahuAkbar. Allah is great. Why is He great? Because of his divine attributes.  AlHamdulillah. All praise and gratitude is for Allah . Why do we praise Him? What are we grateful to Him? Because of his divine attributes. SubhanAllah. He is lofty and there is a great distance between us and Him. Why is that? Because of his divine attributes. And then after declaring and affirming his 99 attributes. what do we finally say? La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no one. No Ilah. No creation reflecting his divine attributes. Illa Allah. except Allah. We are negating all the attributes of His creation from Him. We are purifying him . of any and all resemblance . that we may conceptually or intellectually have with His creation.

And He himself says.

⟪ar-quote:هُوَ ٱللَّهُ ٱلَّذِى لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ٱلْمَلِكُ ٱلْقُدُّوسُ ٱلسَّلَمُ ٱلْمُؤْمِنُ ٱلْمُهَيْمِنُ ٱلْعَزِيزُ ٱلْجَبَّارُ ٱلْمُتَكَبِّرُ⟫

He is Allah , there is no Ilah other than Him. He is the Sovereign, the Pure, the Perfect, the Bestower of Faith, the Overseer, the Exalted in Might, the Compeller, the Superior.  .

and then after saying all this . what does he say?

## ⟪ar-quote:سُبْحَنَ ٱللَّهِ عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ⟫

He is Exalted above whatever they associate with Him.

What is it that they associate with Him? . They associate the attributes of His creation with Him. And the entire concept of Tawheed is purifying Allah. from the attributes of His creation. And that's why the Kalima of Tawheed is . La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no Ilah except Allah.

Scholars say . that one way to understand the kalima. in the light of these divine attributes. is that you replace the word Ilah in that Kalima.  with all the divine attributes .  So instead of saying . La Ilaha Illa Allah. you now say . La Rehma Illa Allah. There is no creation that has mercy like the mercy of Allah . La Karam Illa Allah. There is no creation that has generosity like the generosity of Allah . La Salaam Illa Allah. there is no creation that can provide tranquility like the tranquility of Allah . La Jabar Illa Allah. There is no creation that can compell like the compulsion of Allah.  LanTiqaam Illa Allah. There is no creation that can avenge like the revenge of Allah.

And when you do this intellecutal exercise. for each and every attribute.  When you negate all these attributes of His creation . from the attributes of Allah AWJ. That's when you truly understand the meaning of La Ilaha Illa Allah. There is no Ilah. except Allah.  And when there is nothing that exists like Him. therefore I can NEVER completely understand Him. Because there can be multiple Ilah. sharing . or reflecting the divine Attributes of Allah. but they individually . and collectively. cannot compare to the very attribute of ALlah that they are reflecting.  And that's why the weight of La Ilaha Illa . is 99. It is the complete negation of 99 attributes reflected in.  and through his creation . before the affirmation of that one word Allah.

And referring to this inability. this incapability of human beings to approach Allah AWJ. Maulana Ali AS said.

⟪ar-quote:العجز عن درك الإدراكہُ إدراك . والبحث عن سِرِّ ذاتِهِ إشراك⟫

The inability to know Allah IS in fact the true understanding of Allah. And to try to discuss the essence of Allah is Shirk.

Because it is my inability. my incapacity to comprehend Him. and it is because of His superiority over me . that makes him worthy of my worhip . and that makes him worthy of my obedience.

> — **Quran 42:11** *(from image; see _provenance.json for validation)*
