  *Note:* Quran 42:11 — foundational tanzih (apophatic) verse. Decomposes the Arabic to show double-negation: 'not like Him', 'nothing'.

We are forced to negate. and purify Allah. of all the attributes we find in ourselves and His creation. because there is nothing comparable to Him. And He beautifully explains this to us. through one single word in the ayah.

⟪ar-quote:لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِ شَىْءٌۭ⟫

No matter how hard you try. no matter how high your imaginations fly. no matter how deep your thoughts dive.  there is no way you can ever understand my attributes.
⟪ar-quote:لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِ شَىْءٌۭ⟫There is absolutely nothing you can compare me to. SubhanAllah.

I want you to take a moment and think about this paradox . He created this magnificent universe around us . every single entity reflecting his divine attributes. for us human beings. with intellects. Why? To gain a semblance of understanding.  of his powers. His attributes. And then once we get that understanding. even if of a sub-atomic level. He says . ⟪ar:لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِ شَىْءٌۭ⟫. Whatever little . you now think you know about me. know that I am not like it. I am way beyond it. And what's so amazing. is that He does this . linquistically. through the use of one word. ⟪ar:كَمِثْلِهِ⟫. This is not a word that is commonly used . nor was it used in Ancient Arabia. This is a word only used in balagha. in eloquence of the Quran.

We've already established. that in order to understand something. we either need to compare in being (zaat). or in attributes (sifaat). From a grammatical stand point. the word ⟪ar:کمثلہ⟫is actually 2 words. KA and Mislihi. These are both words of comparison. KA is used for comparison. and Mislihi is also used for comparison. But it is never fused together in this manner.  as Allah has used it in this ayah. so let's try to understand the subtlty in the use of this word.⟪ar:کمثلہ⟫

In arabic when you want to compare someone in attributes. you add the letter KA.  Fo example. if I want to compare the bravery of Zaid with a lion. So if I want to say Zaid is brave like a lion. I will have to use the letter Ka to do that. I'll have to say.

⟪ar-quote:زیدٌ کل أسدِ⟫

Zaid is like a lion. what am I comparing here? I obviously don't mean that Ziad has fangs and claws and a tail and he roars. I'm not comparing zaid in his being to a the lion. I'm comparing his bravery to the bravery of a lion. that's why I'm using the letter Ka . ⟪ar:زیدٌ کل أسد⟫. So Ka is used to compare two things in attributes

But when I need to compare in Zaat. or in being. I can't use the letter Ka. Grammatically that would be wrong.  I will have to use the word Misl. So for example.

⟪ar-quote:الشبل مثل الاسد⟫

A cub is similar to a lion. The son of a lion is like the lion. Because here I am not comparing in attributes. I'm not comparing in Sifaat.  I am comparing in Zaat. I'm comparing the essence.  or the being itself.

So this is the rule of Arabic language. Ka and Misl are used very precisely. And we find this distinction all over Arabic poetry.  So for example this poet is praising the generosity of a king. which is an attribute. He's comparing the kings generosity to the ocean. so he uses the letter. Ka. he says. Kal Bahri.

⟪ar-quote:کل بحرِ یَقذِفُ لِلقریبِ لآلیۃ     جوداً و یبَعَثُ لِلبَعیدِ سحائِبا⟫

He says.  the king is generous like the ocean. when I move closer to him he gives me pearls. and when I move away from him he sends clouds filled with rain. Why does he use Ka?. Because he is comparing the attribute of generosity. But when the being or the entity. or the zaat. itself needs to be compared. the word Misl has to be used.

⟪ar-quote:أنا السُّروجِیُّ وَ ھذا وَلدی⟫   ⟪ar-quote:و الشِّبلُ فی الِمخبَرِ مِثلُ الاسد⟫

I am a lion and this is my son. no doubt the son of a lion is like the lion. so now because the comparison is in being. in Zaat. the poet uses the word Misl.

I hope all of you understand this subtely. because that's what makes this ayah so beautiful. Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِ شَىْءٌۭ⟫

To compare himself. Allah fuses both the Ka. and the Misl together. Ka-Mislihi. Ka is used for attributes. Misl is used for the being itself. So allah say. whehter you try to compare me in attributes. Ka. Or you try to compare me in being. Misl. It is not going to be possible.⟪ar:لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِ شَىْءٌۭ⟫  . There is nothing that exists. in attribute nor being.  that you can use to compare me to. You see the beauty of this word?

Ka. there is no one comparable to me in attributes

Mislihi - there is no one comparable to me in being

KaMislihi - there is no one you can compare me to in attributes or being. SubhanAllah!

---

<!-- section 5 (id=5739, raw_sort=5): Surah Ikhlaas -->
We're studying the highest ranking word. Allah. which is the Ismul Jalalah. the most majestic name of all names. which comes from the root word Ilah. It means THE ILAH .

So with this exclusivity clause applied to it. Allah is the one I completely submit to. the one I am truly and completely loyal to. He is the one I turn to for protection and refuge in my desperate times. He is the one I am passionately in love with. the one I am obsessed about. He is beyond my imagination. and beyond my  capabilities of comprehension and understanding. He is the one who's glory and majesty dumb-founds me. every single time . He is the one I can completely trust. lean on . put my entire weight on . with the certainty that He will never let me fall.  And finally . and the most important meaning of all . He is the one I worship. And my worship my عبادۃ . comprises of two things. worship and obedience. both stemming from the sum of all these different meanings of the word Ilah.

Then we learnt that for a creation to understand it's creator. it needs two things. One an experiential interaction with the creation. that reflects the attributes of the creator. supplemented by a description of the creator Himself. So we experience the attributes of Allah . through our interaction with His creation. which is this universe. And our experience is supplemented by His description. that he provides for us in the Quran. These two things together. help us understand our creator.

Then I explained how we must separate out . or distinguish the attributes of the creation. from the attributes of Allah. Because if we don't do that. we end up commiting shirk. and we partner the creation with the creator in those attributes. And Allah has no partner. He can have no partner . because

⟪ar:لیس کمثلہ شئی⟫. There is nothing comparable to Him. We looked at the linguistic beauty of the word کمثلہ . Ka is used to compare in attributes. and Misl is used to compare in essence. And Allah says. ⟪ar:لیس کمثلہ شئی⟫ . There is nothing comparable to me. neither in attributes. nor in essence. Both captured by this one word. ⟪ar:کمثلہ⟫.

---

AHAD vs WAHID

So if there is nothing comparable to Allah. Neither in essence. nor in attributes. What does that make Him?. That makes him unique!. And the arabic word for unique. is Ahad. But we also hear the term Wahid for Allah. which means one.  So the question becomes . is Allah Ahad?.  or is Allah wahid?. Is He unique? . or is He one? . To answer this question. let's turn to the Quran. What does the Quran say about this?

According to the Quran. Allah is both.  He is Ahad. AND He is wahid. Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:قل ھو اللہ احد⟫

Say He is Allah the unique.

But the Quran also says

⟪ar-quote:وَإِلَهُكُمْ إِلَهٌۭ وَحِدٌۭ ۖ لَّآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ⟫

Your ilah is one. there is no other diety except him and he is rehman and raheem.

Now the first thing we need to understand . is the difference between wahid and ahad. Wahid means one. So how come allah doesnt say ⟪ar:قو ھو اللہ واحد⟫. Say Allah is one! . That would have been true as well. wouldn't it?. We know the language of Quran is extremely precise. You can't change any single word in any single ayah. So this forces us to recognize that this word. Ahad. then must have been used in a very particular context.

To understand this better . we need to understand a little bit about the Arabic language. In the Arabic language.  certain words can only be used in a particular way.  and not in any other way.  If I say right now. Now listen carefully to this.

⟪ar-quote:لیس واحدٍ مَوجودٌ فی المسجد⟫

What word did I use? I used Wahid. There is not ONE in the masjid.  You know what that means in Arabic?. It means there is not one but 2, 3,4 in the masjid.  In other words what I'm saying.  is that there isn't JUST one. but there could be more than one in the masjid.  As opposed to that  if I say.

⟪ar-quote:لیس أَحدٍ موجودٌ فی المسجد⟫

You know what that means? It means. there is not a single person in the masjid.

When I say ⟪ar:لیس واحد⟫ . it means there isn't JUST one in the masjid.  there COULD be one. but probably there are more. But when I say ⟪ar:لیس احد⟫ . then what it means . is that there is not even a single one in the masjid. Ahad is ALWAYS used negatively.  It is never used in a positive sense. It always means. NOT anyone at all. NOT anything at all. For example Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:وَلَا يُشْرِكُ فِى حُكْمِهِۦٓ أَحَدًۭا⟫

NO ONE at all can be His partner in his command

⟪ar-quote:وَلَا يُشْرِكْ بِعِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِۦٓ أَحَدًۢا⟫

NO ONE at all commit shirk with Allah.

So Ahad is used as absolute negation. You understand? . When you want to absolutely negate. You use the word Ahad. But when you want to speak in the positive.  you use the word wahid. 

Now here is the interesting thing. In Surah Ikhalaas. Allahs says.  ⟪ar:قل ھو اللہ احد⟫. Say He is Allah the unique. Here ahad is NOT being used in the negative. It is being used in the positive. And this is very interesting.  Because the only place in the entire Arabic literation.  where this word is used in the positive sense.  without any further attribution.  is surah Al-Ikhlaas. Because the word Ahad . is NEVER used anywhere else in the entire arabic literature. in the positive way. except for Allah.  So linguistically speaking. Allah broke the rules for this word Ahad. when he used it for himself.

First let's understand what Allah is saying in the context of this word Ahad.

Ahad.  is a unique singular entity.  that cannot be compared to any other entity. That no other entity can compete with. Ahad is a singular entity for which no comparison is possible. no competition is possible. it doesn't have a synonym . it doesn't have an anytonym.  ANY sort of affiliation is ABSOLUTELY impossible for this singular entity.  that is Ahad. The one that has no second is Ahad! . The one for whom. a second is impossible. that's ahad.

Now back to the question of why Allah changed the grammatical rule when using this word.  In order to undestand that. we have to go back in time. and understand the ancient arab mentality first. Because this word .  Ahad . used for Allah AWJ. it created earthquakes among the Arabs. Because they too had gods. they believed in gods.  but for every one of their god.  they also had another god.  I can have my god . you can have yours.  They believed in Allah.  but then they said . He took angels as his daughters .  The christian community said he took a son.  So they attributed sons and daughters to Allah.  In some of the Hindu tradiations. what do they do?.  They say god BECAME the universe.  god is in the bug.  and in the tree.  and in the rock.  and the stone. god is running in my veins. right? This is similar to american transcendentalism in more recent times.   In American literature also. god is in the tree. or in nature or in us. etc. etc.

But what happens is. If you start comparing Allah AWJ with other things.  or you start pairing him.  or affiliating him with anything else. what gets lost? .  Ahad. Ahad gets lost! . And if you separate Allah from all attributions of human beings.  if you separate Allah from all attributions of ALL of his creation.  then what you gain as a result of that exclusion . is Ahad. This was a completely revolutionary concept of the uniqueness of Allah. This is a concept that Christians and jews and no other religion agreed with. .  They all said. 

we're ok with ⟪ar:قل ھو اللہ واحد⟫ . Say allah is one. that's fine. We can accept that.  When you study their aqeeda. when you study their creed. you'll find they don't have a problem with wahid. but what do they have a problem with? Ahad . They are NOT willing to accept   ⟪ar:قل ھو اللہ احد⟫.

So Allah broke this linguistic rule in this ayah. when he used the word Ahad for himself in the positive sense. Because what happens is . when you break a normal pattern of conversation. it alerts the listener. Forces them to pay attention. 

Another grammatical nuance is that. if you notice.  in the word ahad.  there is no AL. But it is in the word Samad. ⟪ar:اللہ الصمد⟫ .  We don't say. ⟪ar:اللہُ ‏صمدٌ⟫.

We say.  ⟪ar:اللہ الصمد⟫. Similary Allah could have said.  ⟪ar:اللہ الاحد⟫.  but the AL is omittied from Ahad.  even though it is in Samad.  So why not put Al over there too?. Well this is a grammatical difference.  and it has some rhetorical benefit.  The first benefit is.  that removing the AL and putting a tanveen on it.  puts an exclataion mark on the statement!

****He is Allah. AHAD!!! JUST THINK ABOUT THAT . HOW AMAZING THAT IS!!****

and that can be done in ancient arabic with a tanveen. You and I cannot do that in English. so we have to raise our volume . and bang our fist on the desk. to get that point across. But that is what Allah is saying when He says Ahad. The power of that word. is manifest in that tanveen.

The second thing.  is that tanveen is used conventionally for a khabar. the predicate of a sentence. and predicate is used when someone asks a questions. And ofcourse ahad was a response to the question. that the Arabs were asking at that time.  Who is allah? . And to appropriately answer the questkon.  the alif and laam are not there. You have to put the tanveen there.  Who is allah? He is Allah the unique!. 

And like I said. this was a huge sticking point for them. This is the one word. that got people beatings. This is the one word . that would get Hazrat Bilaal (RA) tortured.  It was THIS one word.  that got him pinned to the scorching sand of the desert. bare skin. with a heavy boulder placed on his chest.  All so that he could give up this one word. You may have read this story. His master tortured him this way.  to give up Islam.  He would pin him. bare back . with a heavy boulder on his chest. on the scorching heat of the desert.  And then he would whip him. And on every whip Hazrat Bilal would say. Ahadun Ahad! Ahadun Ahad! AhadunAhad.  Beat me as much as you want. With every lash. the word Ahad will come out of my tongue.!

So this was a huge point of contention for the ancient Arabs. Saying Allah was never the problem.  Accepting Allah as Ahad was the problem. And so what an amazing word Allah gave us to understand him!

Now the idea behind this word Ahad is. that Allah created human being with the knowledge of Himself. He inherintly put this goal in every single creation.  to want to willingly accept him as His master and to become his slave. The ultimate goal . in the life of a human being . IS to become Allah's slave. His ⟪ar:عبد⟫. That's what Allah created for. 

⟪ar-quote:وَمَا خَلَقْتُ ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ⟫

And I did not create jinn and mankind. except to become my slaves. ⟪ar:لِيَعْبُدُونِ⟫

ABD is a more desirable state

In fact. this is the greatest honor that Rasul Allah received. What do we say in the azaan and the Iqamah?. ⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد عبدہ و رسولہ⟫ . Muhammad (SAS) is the slave and messenger of Allah. Not messenger and slave. NOT  ⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد رسولہ و عبدہ⟫ . No. but ⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد عبدہ و رسولہ⟫ . slave first . messenger later.

The pride and honor of Rasul Allah was not in being Allah's messenger. It was in being His slave. And even when Allah called his beloved to the seventh sky on the night of Mairaj. The greatest honor bestowed upon any living soul. He did not call his messanger. He called his slave.

⟪ar-quote:سُبْحَنَ ٱلَّذِىٓ أَسْرَىٰ بِعَبْدِهِۦ⟫

Exalted is He who took His Slave.

His slave. not His messenger. Allah could have said . ⟪ar:سُبْحَنَ ٱلَّذِىٓ أَسْرَىٰ بِرسولہ⟫

Exalted is He who took His Messenger.

But no. Allah distinctly honored him with the title of his "slave". And that's why when Rasul Allah formulated his kalima. he placed the word Abd. before the word Rasool.

⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد عبدہ و رسولہ⟫ . He gave precedence to his slavery of Allah over his prophethood.

So to become Allah's slave. is the need . that Allah created every human being with. Just as he created us with thirst and hunger.  It is inherint in us. We can't escape it. But when our apetitie is not filled with healthy food .  what do we fill it with? . If we don't get the right meal.  are we going to say we're not going to eat at all? . No! . When a person is starving and there is no healthy food available. he will turn to whatever he finds his hands on .  Even if there is filth. barks of trees. will the human beings still start chewing on that?  He will !!.  When we lose sight of Allah AWJ.  and HE is no longer our goal.  then necessarily we will find a replacement. It is inevitabale. Necessarily we will have to aspire towards something else .  because that hunger that thirst is inherently placed within all of us. 

And for those . who chooses Allah. and find the love and slavery of Allah . What happens to them? Oh my god.

⟪ar-quote:ان صلواتی و نسکی و محیایا و مماتی لی اللہ رب العالمین⟫

It becomes very simple for them. The one who has really found Allah. his statement becomes. My salaah is for Allah. My sacrifice is for allah. My life is now for Allah. and My death is now for all. ALL is for allah . The way they live. The way they eat. The way they earn their living . The way they sleep. What they wanna do with their lives. Their long term goals. Their short term goals. What they are going to do with their kids. Why they're getting an education. Where they're going to work. EVERYTHING becomes for Allah.  Allah becomes their ultimate goals.

### Goals and idols

But for the one who doesn't have that goal.  They have to find another goal. And in old times it used to be idols.  there used to be some other religions. they would find some other god. But in our times.  it has become far more pathetic.  far more pathetic. Now we have someone who is obsessed with their body.  and they are working out 18 hours a day. and their only goal in life is to keep getting buffer and buffer. Stay on top. Keep in shape.  impress the girls. That has become their Ilah. Their body has become their ilaah. They've idolized their bodies.  They have become slaves of their own bodies.

Now we have someone whose entire life has become about money. Have we met people like that?.  They cannot talk about anything other than their bank balance.  and their cars.  and their branded clothes.  and their houses. They have nothing else in life they can talk about.  They have nothing else they can think about. And the moment they lose that money they become suicidal.  because that is all they ever thought about. .  Money has become their Ilah. their idol. that they worship. They've become slaves of their own money.

For some people its their children.  they live for their children. They live THROUGH their children.  My son came first. My daughter did this . My son did that.  That's all they can do.  boast about their kids.  day and night they think about their children. There is no other thought running in their mind.  There is no other goal in their life other than their children. . They create their ultimate purpose with their children.  They make their children . their Ilah.

There are kids who play 20 hours of video games. they become slacker . their goal becomes to entertain themselves. their nafs becomes their ilah.  they simply enjoy frying their brain cells sitting behind a screen.

When you don't find Allah.  you WILL find something else.   And you will run after it. And you will give your life to it. You will inevitably create an idol. start worshiping it and become a slave to it.  And we know what happens with ALL idols.  eventually they all break.

So these are the pshycological implications to understanding tawheed.  It is very easy to say Allah is one. He is unique.  But is He one in my life? . Is he THE one for me? . Is there really no one like Him. no other Ilah.  in my life.  or do I have some other Ilah . that I am running after? Is there some other thing . or some other person. that I put before Allah .

And Allah asks us this question rhetorically in the Quran

⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلْإِنسَنُ مَا غَرَّكَ بِرَبِّكَ ٱلْكَرِيمِ؟⟫

What deluded you from your gracious master? What was so important that you left me for it? SubhanAllah.

So when he uses this word ⟪ar:احد⟫it carries certain psychological implications with it.  It carries implications on our attitudes towards allah. And the way we think about our lives completely changes. After this realization. now suddenly there is nothing more important to me than making Allah happy. Nothing more important to me. than Allah being pleased with me. Nothing more important to me. than Allah forgiving me. Nothing more important to me. than Allah talking to me on the day of judgment.  and telling me that I am successful.  What becomes important is that He will look towards me. and tell me that I will not be from the one He will turn away from.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ يَشْتَرُونَ بِعَهْدِ ٱللَّهِ وَأَيْمَنِهِمْ ثَمَنًۭا قَلِيلًا.  أُو۟لَٓئِكَ لَا خَلَقَ لَهُمْ فِى ٱلْآخِرَةِ .

وَلَا يُكَلِّمُهُمُ ٱللَّهُ . وَلَا يَنظُرُ إِلَيْهِمْ يَوْمَ ٱلْقِيَمَةِ . وَلَا يُزَكِّيهِمْ . وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌۭ⟫

Allah will not talk to them on the day of judgment. may allah not make us from them.

So that's what we learn from this one word Ahad. ⟪ar:قل ھو اللہ احد⟫. Say. He is Allah the unique. Unique in my life . Unique in my heart. Allah has a place in my heart. in my life. in my work. in my thought process. in my decisions. in my prayers. in my sacrifice. my life. my death. in my existence. Allah has a place that no one else has. All of that is captured in this one word Ahad.

---

What makes Allah worthy of worship

Now let's look at the attributes of Allah. in the context of this word Ahad. One of the easiest place where we can become confused.  is when a word is used for Allah.  and is also used for us. For example Allah calls himself ⟪ar:علیم⟫. knowledgable! . Have you ever heard that word being used for a person also? . that a person is knowledgable? A person is ⟪ar:علیم⟫? Sure! . Allah calls himself ⟪ar:حکیم⟫. the wise! . Can a person also be called wise? Sure! Its possible! . Allah says. for example. He says that He is ⟪ar:غفور⟫. The forgiving! . Can you describe a person as being forgiving? . Yes you can!. It's the same with the other attributes of Allah.⟪ar:سمیع⟫. the one who hears everything . .⟪ar:بصیر⟫. the one who sees everything . Can these words be used for a human being also? Sure! they can!

But this. is now a  problem. Because the same word that is being used for Allah.  is now also being used for a human being.  Now there ARE certain attributes of Allah that are unshared. That apply exclusively to Him alone. Ahad. Samad. Rehmaan.  These are attributes that are exclusively used for Allah and not any human being. But a majority of the attributes of Allah. are shared by human beings as well.  For example one of Allah's name is ⟪ar:رؤف⟫. the compassionate. and ⟪ar:رحیم⟫. the merciful. But these same attribute are also used for Rasul Allah in the Quran.
⟪ar-quote:و بالمؤمنین رؤف الرحیم⟫

Now this seems to violate the defintion of Ahad. Because now the attributes of Allah are no longer unique. They are now shared with His creation. So how do we reconcile both these things? . Because sharing an attribute with Allah is what? . It's Shirk!. The greatest sin of all. So now how do we clearly understand this? If a word is used for Allah. and the same word is used for entities other than allah. then how do we NOT end up doing shirk?

So what I want you to remember. is 3 differences. If you remember these 3 things.  you will never fall into shirk.   So what we'll do InshaAllah . is use one attribute or name as a sample.  and then these 3 rules will apply to all the other attributes of Allah. Lets take the name knowledgable.  ⟪ar:علیم⟫.  So we say Allah is ⟪ar:علیم⟫. the Knowledgable. and we compare that to another human being that is also ⟪ar:علیم⟫. knowledgable.

### Timeless

Here's the first thing. Allah's attributes has no beginning and no end.  So if we take knowledge.  Allah's knowledge does not have a beginning.  meaning there was never a point when he was not knowledgable.  and it has no ending.  meaning there is never going to be a time . EVER . where he will not be knowledgable. Now compare that to your and my knowledge. . or the knowledge of all creation put together.  what does it have? . It has a beginning.  and it has an ending. That's the first difference . Allah's attributes are **timeless**.  All attributes of Allah are timeless. they don't have a beginning.  and they don't have an ending.  In contrast to that. ours is temporary. ours is  timed . they're caged. that's the first one.

### No Limits

The second.  is that Allah's attributes has no limits.  it has no confines.  His knowledge encompases everything.  there is nothing that he doesn't know.  As opposed to your knowledge.  and my knowledge. What does it necessarily have? . It has limits! Because I don't know what game you're playing on your phone right now. I don't know who you're texting right now.  I don't know what level of candy crush you're on right now. I don't know how many heartbeats I have left on this earth.  I don't know what will happen in the next 30 minutes. I have some knowledge.  but I don't have ALL the knowledge. as opposed to Allah who has ALL knowledge. without any limits

So the first difference is Allah's attributes are timeless.  and the second thing is that they are limitless.

### Inherently owned

Now the third.  and most important difference.  Everything that I have.  So talking about knowledge.  the knowledge that I have. It is not something I own. It is something that was given to me.  I wasn't born with it.  It was given to me by others. It does not inherently belong to me.  As opposed to Allah. when you talk about His knoweldge. it is his own . It inherently. innately . naturally. esseentially belongs to Him. It was not given to him by anyone else.  it is his own. It's part and parcel of his essence. It is not acquired.

So these are the three things to keep in mind when thinking of Allah's attributes. They are timeless. limitless. and inherent.

Now let's think about any of the other attributes of Allah. Let's take power.  ⟪ar:القوی⟫.  You can have a person who is strong.  But his power has a beginning and it has an end. whereas Allahs power has no beginning and no end.  The power of Allah has no limits. it is infinite. it is limitless. whereas the power of a human being has limits.  And then the power of Allah is essentially. fundamentally . his own.  He didn't get it from anyone else. it is His own. But the power of a human being comes from whom? From Allah Subhanahu Wa Ta'ala.

Now remember I told you. when we were looking at the definitions of the word Ilah. I said the greatest  of all meanins is . ⟪ar:أَلِہَ یَعلُہُ بِمَعنیٰ عَبَدَ یَعبُدُ⟫  . Ilah in the sense of the one that is worshipped. Now I'm tying that meaning with what we just learnt. So listen to this carefully.

How are Allah's attributes unique. how are they Ahad. in comparison to the attributes of his creation? . It is unique by 3 things. His attributes are timeless. limitless and inherently owned. And when you have these three features applied to an attribute. what do you get as a result of it? . You get PERFECTION. These attributes are PERFECT. BECAUSE they are timeless. because they are limitless and because they are inherently His own. so they will NEVER disappear. They will never change.

Because if these three things were not present. If He was not timeless. If He was not limitless. If he was not the inherent owner of these attributes. **He would not be worthy of my worship.**

I'll say that again. If He was not timeless. If He was not limitless. If he was not the inherent owner of these attributes. **He would not be worthy of my worship.**

If he was not ⟪ar:السمیع⟫. in this PERFECT sense.  He would not be worth of my worship. If He was not ⟪ar:بصیر⟫. in this PERFECT sense. He would not be worth of worship . If he was not ⟪ar:علیم⟫. in this PERFECT sense. If he were not ⟪ar:رحمن⟫. If he were not ⟪ar:رحیم⟫. If He were not ⟪ar:غفور⟫. and we can go on and on.  listing all of the 99 attributes of Allah. In other words if He was not PERFECT. in each and every one of these 99 attributes. He would not be worthy of my worship. 

It is the PERFECTION of these 99 attributes. that makes him AL-ILAH. That's the true meaning of .  ⟪ar:أَلِہَ یَعلُہُ بِمَعنیٰ عَبَدَ یَعبُدُ⟫. The one who is so magnificent. that he is worthy of worship!.

So Allah . because of His perfection . is the ultimate being who is worthy of worship and obedience. And this is why. linguistically. the highest meaning of the word Ilah. is the one that is worshipped. The diety that deserves to be worshipped. The one and only entity. that deserves to be called ALLAH. Because as I shared with you in one of the previous session. Allah combines all the 99 attributes with it.   And that's why He says in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:وَلِلَّهِ ٱلْأَسْمَآءُ ٱلْحُسْنَىٰ⟫

To this one name Allah. belong all the other beautiful names. To this one name Allah. belong all the other beautiful names. The name Allah. combines in itself. the power and the perfection of all the 99 attributes. that are timeless. limitless . and inherently belong to Allah. It is this PERFECTION. that makes Him worthy of veneration .  of prostration.  of love . of hope. of fear.  of dua. of being the one to lean on . being the one I can put my weight on. And finally the one who is worthy of my worship and obedience . And that is our Kalima as well. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ . There is no diety that is worthy of being an Ilah.  other than Allah who is THE ultimate Ilah.  That is what our kalima implies.

So if you keep these 3 distinctions in mind.  then you will maintain what Allah calls Ahad.  If you don't. then you will commit shirk each and everytime. Which BTW we do all the time. All the time!  .  We literally do it a 100 times every single day. Whenever we praise someone. or something. We make statements about the future. We fear someone or something. we are constantly committing shirk. Even if that is not in our hearts. But we are committing shirk with our tongues.

And that's why to counter that we have been given 3 words: ⟪ar:انشاء اللہ، ماشاء اللہ، سبحان اللہ، حمد للہ⟫ .

---

InshaAllah; SubhanAllah MashaAllah

First of all what do these words mean? . ⟪ar:انشاء اللہ⟫. IF Allah desires. ⟪ar:ما شاء اللہ⟫ . Whatever Allah desires or chooses. ⟪ar:سبحان اللہ⟫ . Exalted is Allah. Glorified is Allah.  ⟪ar:حمد للہ⟫. Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah

Again. ⟪ar:انشاء اللہ⟫. IF Allah wishes. If Allah chooses. ⟪ar:ما شاء اللہ⟫ . Whatever . or for whomever Allah desires . and. ⟪ar:سبحان اللہ⟫ . Exalted and Glorified is Allah. ⟪ar:حمد للہ⟫. Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah

Now let's look at these words individually. When I see something and appreciate it. For example I see a beautiful sunrise . or sunset or a beautiful waterfall. And I say. What a beautiful waterfall. What I'm inadvertantly doing. is I am using the word BEAUTIFUL for the waterfall. And BEAUTIFUL  is an attribute of Allah AWJ . He is Jameel. When I said the waterfall is beautiful. I just equated the beauty . the jamal. of the waterfall . with the Jameel. The Most beautiful. I just partnered the beauty of the creation. with the creator. Even that that was not my intention. I did not intentionally say that. But I still committed Shirk. Shirk means linguistically . "to partner". The urdu word "Shareek" comes from the Arabic root word shirk. It means to partner. to associate. to attribute.

So when I called the waterfall beautiful. I partnered it's beauty with Allah's beauty. And that's shirk . It's called shirk-e-Khafee. Hidden Shirk. There are 2 types of shirk. Shirk Jalee. That is manifest shirk. Like saying Christ is the son of Allah. or the tree and the cow god. That's clear and manifest shirk. But then partnering the attributes of creation. with the attributes of Allah. is also Shirk. It is shirk-e-khafee. Hidden shirk.  So by calling the waterfall beautiful. I just committed shirk-e-khafee.

But when I say. What a beautiful waterfall. SubhanAllah!. I immediately purified my statement . I immediately purified the timeless beauty of Allah. the limitless beauty of Allah. and the innate beauty to Allah. from the beauty of the waterfall . which is limted. which is bound in time. and which has an owner. I just exalted and glorified the beauty of Allah. over the beauty of the waterfall. In my saying SubhanAllah. I just consciously became aware of that fact. I reminded myself. that this beauty . this jamaal. is refracting the jameel. It is refracting the beauty of Allah AWJ. Immediately my focus shifts from the beauty of the waterfall. to the beauty of the Jameel. You understand? . And so now I'm using the attributes of creation. to turn towards Allah's remembrance. That is the idea behind saying SubhanAllah.

There are many who just use SubhanAllah as a parroted phrase. Oh SubhanAllah! SubhanAllah! SubhanAllah! . on everything they say it. But does their heart actually turn towards their master? . Are they consciously thinking and remembering Allah when they say it? . If not. then it's still shirk. It means nothing. So be mindful of this the next time you say SubhanAllah. A the mention of this word. your heart should switch its focus. It should shift from the object that you just praised. to the one who created the object. realizing that the object is simply refracting one of the beautiful attributes of Allah AWJ.

So that's SubhanAllah. Now the next one.

When I say. We will have a session again next week. In that statement . is the assumption. the knowledge. rather certainty of the fact. that there IS going to be a next week. Because ONLY Allah has knowledge of the unseen. Only Allah knows if I'm going to be around next week or not. If my skype will work next week or not. if my computer will work next week or not. If I'll have electricity next week or not. Because next week's session. is in the unseen future. And ONLY Allah has knoweldge of the future.

So by saying. We will have a session again next week.  I'm inadvertantly. unintentionally. partnering myself in the knowledge of the unseen that ONLY Allah has. I partnered myself.  in the knowledge of unseen . with Allah's knowledge. committing shirk.

But when I say. InshaAllah We will have a session again next week. IF Allah so desires. we will have a session next week.  Now by using the word InshaAllah. I have put my knowledge of the unseen . with Allah where it belongs. If Allah chooses . IF Allah so desires. we will have a session again next week. I've extracted all power from myself. and placed it with its rightful owner. Again. the word InshaAllah. shifted my focus from myself. to my creator. I am no longer a partner with Him in His knowledge of the unseen.

Now the last one. And I'm using this example for the benefit of both participants. the giver and the recepient.

When I say to one of you girls in the session. When I say for example.  You are very beautiful. You are gorgeous. What is your natural reaction going to be?. Oh Thank you! right? Heee Hee Heee.

But the question is. when I'm saying YOU are beautiful. who am I giving credit to for that beauty? . I'm giving you the credit. And when you say Thank you!. What are you doing? . You're accepting credit for that beauty. isn't it? . Why am I saying YOU are beautiful. And why are you saying thank you? . You didn't make yourself. You did not create your beautiful features. You did not choose your skin color. the color of your eyes. your hair. You have no part in it. So then why am I giving you credit for your beauty?. And why are you accepting it. by saying thank you?. 

One reason you're saying thank you. is because you either believe you own your beauty. You believe in your heart. it is YOU who made YOU look beautiful. OR. You could be saying thank you for the compliment I'm giving you . But even in that case. your question should be. Who am I.  to pay this compliment of beauty to YOU? Because that's what I said, didn't I? I said. YOU are very beautiful. We both know that you did not create yourself. So then who am I to assign that beauty to you?. And why are you accepting it with a thank you? . We're both taking assigning credit of beauty to the wrong object. Credit of your beauty belongs to your creator. When you praise a painting. you don't talk to the painting. do you? . You don't say. Mr. Painting. you are really awesome!. No you don't do that. You praise the artist who made the painting. Similarly you and I are all Allah's art work. So who is the true owner of our compliments? It's Allah.

Now if we switch these statements around. And I say. MashaAllah. You are very beautiful!. and in response to that . instead of saying Thank you . you say AlHamdulillah. Now what did we just do?. I just attributed your beauty. to the one who gave you that beauty in the first place. MashaAllah. You are beautiful BECAUSE Allah chose that beauty for you . My focus immediately shifted from you. to the one who created you! . And when you said . AlHamdulillah. Praise and gratitude be to Allah. You too shited your focus from yourself. your own beauty. to the one who made you beautiful. We both . just by using the word MashaAllah. and AlHamdulillah. changed our conversation from shirk. into worship. SubhanAllah.

What a beautiful religion we have!. What immense beauty there is in our humility towards Allah. This is true عبدیت. This is true slavery. true worship. And this can only be done. in the most complete sense.  by the one. who see's Allah as THE ILAH. This can only be done by the one who is passionately in love with Allah. who is obsessed about Allah. Who is completely dependent on Allah. Who is constantly turning to Allah.

---

Qul. is a lesson for the messenger himself and it is also he must go out an teach. this "teacher training" . When Allah says qul. he cannot just keep it to himself. he has to declare it. if allah say اعلم! ھو اللہ احد . then that is something for him to know. but when Allah say قل ھو اللہ احد . now it's not just for him. he has to go out and spread the word.

huwa. is a pronoun here. now a  pronoun is used instead of  a noun. So there is a pronoun and a noun in this ayah. you have Allah. there was no need for huwa. even without huwa. the sentence is complete. قل اللہ احد . that's a perfectly valid sentence. So then why is the word huwa "HE" used here?

A pronoun is used. when you already know is being talked about.  So for example. if I told you right now. you know! he graduated from college. your first question would be what? Who are you talking about? Who graduated from college? But when there is someone. who is so well known. that you don't even need to mention his name. then you can just use the pronoun. because it is so obvious who the subject is. and His greatness is so universally acknowledged . that there is no need to mention his name first. I can only say "he" and you'll know who I'm talking about. This is called شأن in arabic. because of the universally known greatness of the subject at hand. you can just say  huwa. So the huwa is a sign pointing to Allah's greatness of Allah AWJ.

And of course it is also a response to the qeustions. من ھو؟ who is he? ما ھو؟ what is here? and the answer to that is ھو اللہ احد . the one that you asked about is Allah.

If we further break this down grammatically. from a خبر مبتدا point of view. subject predicate. so then from an actual english translation. this ayah reads. Say! He is Allah . and then Say! He is Ahad. Allah is خبر الاولی and ahad is خبر الثانی . So from a grammatical point of view these are two sentences fused into one. so we would translat this. Say he is Allah. - comma - the unique!
