<!-- section 6 (id=5738, raw_sort=6): Allah is Samad -->
We're studying the linguistic meaning of the word Allah. We've been slowly building upon that concept. of what the word Allah means. what his attributes mean. Hopefully by now you have a more clear understanding who Allah is. and what he's supposed to mean to us. what place he's supposed to have in our lives. in our day to day transactions. I'll do a very quick recap of what we've discussed so far.

We talked about noun and adjectives. essence and attributes. He called himself. his essence. Allah

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّنِىٓ أَنَا ٱللَّهُ لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّآ أَنَا۠⟫

Indeed I am Allah. there is no deity except me

And then. when this divine essence . hits his creation. it refracts into these 99 attributes. so that WE. his creation could recognize somethings about him. I  gave the example of a Maritan and the ipad. that how the Martian is able to understand or experience certain attributes about human beings.  just by interacting with the iPad. And then when he finds a book describing human physiology and human psychology.  how he can combine both. his experience. and his knowledge about human beings.  to understand more about us. But we also saw that just understanding the iPad does not provide a completely understanding of the human capabilities.

Similarly we interact with this world. which is Allah's creation . And we experience some of Allah's attributes by interacting with his creation and nature. And then our experince is supplemented by the knowledge of the Quran. which is Allah's message. delievered to us by Him. through His messenger. in a language that we humans can comprehend. explaining who Allah is. The what. the how. and the why . of his creations. And he did this so we could intellectually reconcile the two things together. Allah says in the Quran He is merciful (raheem). and then we DO experience his mercy in the form of rain falling from the sky. providing for us means of a good life. and we say INDEED. Allah is merciful. The same for all other attributes of Allah. We find them manifest. in various different ways in his creations. We see them inside us. within our souls. as well as in the horizons. in the creations outside of us. And this is what Allah is referring to when he says.

⟪ar-quote:سَنُرِيهِمْ آيَتِنَا فِى ٱلأٓفَاقِ وَفِىٓ أَنفُسِهِمْ حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّهُ ٱلْحَقُّ⟫

I will keep showing them my signs. my proofs. through the attributes of my creation. in their own souls and in the horizons. meaning within themselves and all around them. I'll keep showing them these undeniable proofs. ⟪ar:حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّهُ ٱلْحَقُّ⟫ . until they are truly convinced. until it becomes perfectly clear to them. that this message is the truth.

And today . with the advancements that science has made. we are finding these attributes manifest even at cellular levels.

And why is this important to realize? . The reason it is important to understand this. is because Allah talks about a LOT of unseen in the Quran. doesn't He? . Stuff that we are incapable of seeing. proving while we're in this limited physical realm. So what He has done is. He has made what we can see. what we can understand. what we can experience . as PROOF . for that which we cannot. So basically He's saying. I'm telling you who I am . through my attributes that I have placed abundantly in my creation. They're manifesting inside you. and outside of you.  so that you can experience for yourself. And if what I'm saying about this physical. SEEN world is true. then what I'm saying about the Spritual. UNSEEN world must also be true. So he used what we CAN see and experience. as proof for that which we CANNOT see an experience. And he did all of this through the manifestation of his attributes all around us. And then he said. that even though you'll be able to get a small taste of my attributes. you can NEVER completely understand my divine attributes to their fullest extent. because ⟪ar:لیس کمثلہ شئی⟫ . there is nothing EXACTLY similar to him. ⟪ar:کمثلہ⟫ .  not in attributes. and not in essence.

So that's the first thing I want you to understand. WHY he designed everything this way. So that he could use what CAN be seen. as a evidence. as daleel. for that which CANNOT be seen. Because the unseen world is a much GREATER manifestation of his divine attributes.

Then we started studying Surah AlIkhlaas. which is THE MOST perfect description of how Allah is different from his creation.  Because when things become relatable. the human intellect tends to equate. Because human intellect computes. If A = B and B = C then C must be equal to A. right? . If two sides of a triangle are equal. the third has to be equal as well. So if the sky is mainfesting Allah's attributes. the sun, moon stars. the earth. if all of these are manifesting Allah's attributes. then they must all be gods. If human beings can manifest attributes of Allah. then why can't Jesus be the son of god?. because a son. resembles his father. right?

So Surah Ikhlaas responds to that line of thinking. using the word "AHAD". which we studied in the last session. Allah says. قل ھو اللہ احد . Say He is Allah the unique. And I explained to you how Allah is unique in his attributes. How even though creations can mainfest some of Allah's attributes. how they can never be equal to him. by virtue of 3 things. Allah's attributes are timeless. they are limitless. and they are inherently owned by Him. Meaning they were not learnt. because they they could have been forgotten. They were not given to him because then they could have been taken away. The are all part of his essence. like fragrance is part of a flower. You can't separate a flower from its fragrance. Like the SHAPE of a chair is a part of its body. You can't separate the shape of a chair from its body. Like cold is part of ice. You can't separate cold from ice. If they're separated . it will no longer remain ice. So these attributes are inherently. fundamentally His own. That's all encapsulated in the meaning of the word "Ahad".

meaning of Samad

Then after declaring His ⟪ar:احدیت⟫. His uniqueness. He says . ⟪ar:اللہ الصمد⟫ .Allah is AsSamad. So now let's understand this word Samad. It has a slew of meanings.

Linguistically. ⟪ar:الصمد⟫ is the one who is enough. He is ⟪ar:المقصود لقضاء الحاجات⟫.  He is the one who we constantly turn to.  to fulfill our needs and to answers all of our questions. That's the first meaning of the word ⟪ar:صَمَد⟫. Allah is someone who is enough for me to fullfills all my needs and answer all my questions.

Second meaning of the word ⟪ar:صَمَد⟫is . Someone or something . that you set as your goal. or your ultimate destination.  When you aspire to reach someone. When you aspire to please someone . When you make someone your final destination. they become ⟪ar:الصمد⟫.  So Allah is saying. He is the one . we should set as our ultimate goal. Allah is calling himself the ultimate goal for his creations. Everything action we do . it must be targetted towards Allah's pleasure.

Another meaning of Samad is the one who has no need for others. Someone nobody can overpower in any possible way. for example in battle. or rise above them in status . or in any other attribute. You cannot out-do them them in business or their leadership or their elloquence . That is also ⟪ar:صَمَد⟫. because no one can overcome Allah AWJ

Then scholars say .   ⟪ar:⟪ar:الصمد⟫الذی لا عیب فیہ⟫ . samad is the one who has no blemeshes.  or no faults in him. no impurities. And Allah is pure of faults and impurities.

It also implies. ⟪ar:عظیم الجلالۃ⟫ . The one incredible and great.  in terms of his glory and magnificence.

It also means⟪ar:الدائم الخالد⟫ . The one who is ever living.  and ever lasting.

So you see there are a bunch of meanings for the word samad. But if you can't remember all of these meanings. don't worry about it. It's OK. The ONLY meaning that I DO want you to remember for Samad.  is this. because it encapsulates the rest of the meanings in it.

Scholars say. something is samad. ⟪ar:شئیٌ الصمد. ھو مُصْمَد. لا جوف لہ⟫.  A thing is called Samad . when it is completely solid. and has no holes or no emptyness inside. Something that is through and through one pure thing .  like a pure brick of gold. a brick of pure gold could be called samad. . Or a boulder.  with no possibility of any air or water getting in. that is samad.  Something with no gaps whatsoever in its construction. that is called samad. . Something absolute and concrete and without any flaws. that is Samad.

And THIS meaning is very important to appreciate. Because what happens when there is a gap in something? . What happens when something is hollow. it cracks. Also when there is a gap. impurities can set in. corruption can set it. But when something has no gaps . when something is through and through. one solid block. it cannot crack. impurities cannot find a way in. And this is important to understand. because this is the state of each and every one of Allah's attributes. His attributes are not just Ahad . He is not just unique. they are also AsSamad . They are complete and whole . They are not lacking anything in them. So when He is Rehman. and He is Raheem. He is uniquely merciful. and He is through and through completely. ABSOLUTELY. merciful. There is no gap in His Rehma. for Zulm or injustice to set in. because he is Samad. You understand?. His Reham . his mercy is constant. and consistent. and intense. because he is Ahad and AsSamad.

Because an attribute is like a shell.  Is is possible that you give someone an attribute like "Noble". because that's because of what he seems on the outside. But then is it also possible that he could be pretending to be noble? . Or he may not be SO noble ALL the time. He has fits of rage from time to time. ? It's possible.  You can call someone POWERFUL. because of their rank and position. but could there be weakness inside them?.  It's possible. So we can give attributes to creation. and they can fulfill those attributes sometimes. maybe even most of the times. but never ALL the time. But when we call Allah.  by any of His attributes. BECAUSE he is AsSamad. BECAUSE there is no gaps or holes in His attributes.  He actually manifests . and fulfills each and every single one of His attribute.  in the MOST PERFECT and ABSOLUTE sense.  And that's why ⟪ar:الصمد⟫has the AL before it.  its because of the absolute. ⟪ar:اِستِغرَاق⟫.   meaning ABSOLUTELY . in no way shape of form does he lack anything.

So each and every attribute of Allah AWJ is unique (Ahad). by virtue of being timeless, limitless and the inherently owned. AND they are complete and absolute. through and through.  without any wholes or emptiness.  (samad). which makes them PERFECT. And these two qualities of ahad and samad. they both exist at the same time. Because is it possible for something to be unique and not absolute? Is it possible for something to be absolute and whole. but not unique? . Sure! Very easily possible. A brick of gold is samad. but it's not unique. there are several other bricks of gold. But Allah is Ahad and Samad. both at the same time. And this fact exists grammatically in these two ayats.  Grammatically these two ayahs are highlighting the word Ahad and Samad and putting an AND in between them. You know the difference between OR and AND right? . If Allah was ahad OR samad. then he could be one or the other. not necessarily both right? . But what Allah is highlighting in these two ayats. grammatically. is that he is BOTH at the same time. And I want to show you how.

So Allah says. قل ھو اللہ احد . Say he is Allah the unique. Then He says . اللہ الصمد.  Allah is samad. Now if you look at this grammatically . he did not need to use the word Allah again in the second ayah. because he mentioned Allah in the first ayah. He could have just used a pronoun. In fact even in the first ayah. He didn't need to use the word ھو. Why is he using a pronoun before using the noun?. Normally you use the noun first and then a pronoun. Mariam is in my sessions. She is my neice. I don't say. She is Mariam who is in my sessions. Mariam is my neice. right?

So Allah could have said . قل اللہُ احد. Say Allah is unique! And then in the next one he says. اللہ الصمد. instead of ھو الصمد . You understand? . There are INCREDIBLE taweelaat and Haqaiq behind this. unfortunately I'm not at liberty to discuss them. But I do want to hint towards these things. so that hopefully you will want to advance and find out why Allah said things this way. But for our purpose. these are to highlight the importance of these words Ahad and Samad. And grammatically what this does. in classical Arabic. when you bring back a noun when you could used a pronoun. is that it puts an AND in between the two qualities. and brings them on equal levels. Meaning Allah is ahad AND HE IS Samad. both at the same time. He is unique AND he is absolute. both at the same time.

And when you have someone or something that is unique AND absolute both at the same time. you have PERFECTION. So from this point on . when I use the word perfect for Allah AWJ. what it should mean to you is. PERFECT = Ahad + Samad. you understand? . Perfection for Allah's attributes should mean. Unique . by being timeless, limitless and owned. And ALSO complete and absolute. lacking nothing. Because nothing else in creation is Ahad and samad both at the same time. Therefore nothing else in creation is perfect . before the perfection of Allah.

Questions?

---

Another meaning in the word Ahad and Samad . that I want to point out . is that just because Quran mentions these 99 attributes. it does not mean that Allah only has 99 attributes. Someone in the group asked me this question. Why do we confine Allah in just these 99 attributes? . Isn't he exalted than that. to be confined in 99 attributes?.  It was an excellent question.  But I needed to explain ahad and samad before I could answer that question.

Using the metaphor of light. I said. white light refracts into its 7 component lights when it hits a prism. Similarly when the essence of Allah. hits this physical . and material plain. It refracts into these 99 attributes. so that WE human beings can experience them. so that WE can wrap our intellects around it. Bu that does not mean Allah is limited by. or confined to these 99 attributes. We are! . Our intellects are limited to them. Not Allah. He is way more exalted . and way more majestic . way more divine than these 99 attributes. These 99 attributes are what we human beings . of limited intellects. are capable of experiencing and understanding in this physical realm. And that too just a fraction of it.  Otherwise Allah's attributes are WAY exalted and infinite in number for us human beings to understand.  And Allah himself says in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:سُبْحَنَهُۥ وَتَعَلَىٰ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ⟫

Allah is way exalted . and way superior than what is attributed to him.  Because these attributes are confined in the physical realm. our intellects are confined in the physical realm. Allah is NOT. Allah is not confined in the physical realm. because He is the creator of the physical realm. Just like the martian cannot confine the human being to the features of an iPad . Similarly we human beings. our limited imagination cannot transcend this physical realm. So the best we can imagine. the best we can dream of . the best we can wrap our minds around. are these 99 attributes . You understand?. His uniqueness and his completeness. his absoluteness is not something our minds can comprehend.

---

I'll give you an example.  This is actually from the teachings of Maulana Ali AS. which was explained beautifully  by Hazrat Zia Ali sahab.

[diagram: Teaching diagram of the epistemological triad. A large green circle labelled 'علم / Knowledge' surrounds an image of Earth labelled 'معلوم / Known'. To the right stands a human silhouette labelled 'عالم / Knower'. A blue arrow at bottom-left reads 'Must exist'.]
  (see ../images/009.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:علم · معلوم · عالم⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical: 'ilm (knowledge) requires both ma'lum (known) and 'alim (knower); the trio is mutually entailed. Standard Islamic epistemology used to derive divine attributes.

You see. when we human beings think of these divine attributes. So let's take an example. Let's use the same example we used last time. which is knowledgable. When we human beings think about knowledge . we need that entity to exist . before we can gain knowledge about it. isn't it? . BECAUSE minerals and metals exist. that's why we have the knowledge of chemistry. Human body exists. diseases exist. medicine exists.  that's why we have the knowledge of physiology and medicine. Computers exists. that's why I'm a computer engineer. If computers didn't exist . knowledge of computers wouldn't exist. and I would not be able to acquire that knowledge to become a computer programmer. You understand? . So our knowledge is dependent on the existence of the entity. for which we are acquiring knowlege. If the entity didn't exist. there is no way we could be knowledgable about it. So then there are three components to our knowledge. The entity. called the معلوم . the knowledge of the entity . which is the علم.  and the one acquiring the knowledge. who is the عالم.  right? So there is علم. knowledge. the عالم . the knower. and the معلوم. the entity being known. And all of this is dependent on the existence of the entity.

So now when we think of Allah being knowledgable. of Allah being علیم. the question is what is he knowledgable of? . We can say. He has knowledge of the universe. So if he's knowledgable BECAUSE the universe exists. then does that mean he was not علیم when the universe did NOT exist? . Because we know this universe did not always exist. And then what happens when this universe one day will no longer exists? . Would he still be علیم then?. Will he still have complete knowledge of the universe. even when there is no universe?.

Do you see the problem here? . We human beings cannot process that. because we cannot think outside of these physical confines. Because for us to be knowledgable. we need the entity to exist first. and then we can gain knowledge of it to become knowledgable. But that's not the case with Allah. He is forever knowledgable. Because His knowledge is timeless.  He is forever He is infinitely علیم . because his knowledge is limitless. EVEN when there is no entity to be knowledgable of .  Because this attribute of being knowledgable. of being علیم . is part of his divine essence.

So Allah is علیم . not BECAUSE of his creation. He is not dependent on the existence of His creation to be علیم . He was  علیم before He created anything. He is علیم today. and he will remain علیم even AFTER His creation no longer exists.  Because His Ilm. His knowledge.  is not dependent on the existence of His creation.  You understand? .

Similarly Allah is powerful . but what does power mean? . We can only understand Allah's power in reference to how we see power. Because we too. as human beings.  share a time-bound. limited. and externally acquired version of Allah's divine attribute. We too are powerful. But we are powerful ONLY because that entity exists . which CAN BE over-powered. When we come across an entity that is insurmountable and overwhelming. we no longer remain powerful. But Allah is powerful even when there is nothing to be over-powered.

That's why in the sajda dua of Shafa. what do we say?

وارحم ذلی بین یدیک . Have mercy on my weakness before you.

و تضرعی الیک  and on my cries before you.

و وحشتی من الناس . and my panic and horror and trepidation is because of people.

و انسی بک. and my peace and tranquility is with you

And then we say.

یا کریم یا کائنا قبل کل شئی

Oh the one who is generous and the one who existed . BEFORE anything ever existed.

و یا کریم و  یا کائنا بعد کل شئی

And Oh the one who is generous and the one who will exist . AFTER everything will be destroyed. What a beautiful way to call Allah AWJ. Two attributes are mentioned here. Karam. Generosity and کائنا. His existence. Because this universe around us . is a refraction of these two attributes . These attributes answer the two MOST fundamental question about the existence of this universe. Why does this universe exist?. To show that Allah exists!. Why did he create this universe?. Because He is generous. SubhanAllah.

This universe exists to show. that Allah exists. and that He is generous. He is Kareem. Generosity is NOT something you HAVE To do . When you don't HAVE to do something. but you still do it. that's what makes you generous. isn't it? . Allah did not HAVE to create this universe for us to live in and enjoy. But He did it anyway . Why? . BECAUSE He is generous. And the magnificence. the glory . the majesty. the immense size of this universe is screaming . and pointing towards its creator . saying I exist. because my creator exists. And my immensity. my glory. my beauty. is a refraction of the majesty. the glory and the beauty of my creator.  SubhanAllah.

And look. even with us . Today we are called generous . BECAUSE we are able to give things. BECAUSE we are able to donate. to give money. But we first need to HAVE money. before we can GIVE it in charity. isn't it? . Would we be capable of generosity if we didn't have any money? . How would we manifest generosity without posessing THINGS to be generous with? . So we NEED created things . in order four generosity to EXIST. But Allah is generous. EVEN WHEN there was nothing to give . He was generous EVEN before he created this universe. And He will be generous. EVEN after this universe is long gone. He existed BEFORE this universe was created. And He will exist EVEN AFTER His creation is destroyed.

His generosity and His existence. is NOT BECAUSE of his creation. His CREATION is because of his generosity and existence . I'll say that again. His generosity and His existence. is not BECAUSE of his creation. His CREATION is because of his generosity and existence . so that it could experience his attributes.

So when we think about the attributes of Allah. we are forced to think of them within the boundaries of this physical realm. within the boundaries of our limited experiences. And no doubt Allah and his attributes are way beyond the confines of this physical realm . and they are way beyond the boundaries of our imaginations. So Allah is not confined to these 99 attributes. His capabilities are infinite. These 99 attributes are only those that are manifesting WITHIN this physical realm. so that WE human beings. can experience a tiny fraction of who Allah is. But Allah is way beyond the confines of time and space. and way beyond our limited understanding of what these attributes mean. And that's why He says.

وَتَعَلَىٰ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ

He is way above what you attribute to Him

سُبْحَنَ رَبِّ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَرْشِ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ

Glorified is the master of the heavens and the earth. the master of the throne.  from what you attribute to Him

and that's why He says.

لیس کمثلہ شئی

There is nothing that you can use as a point of reference.  to compare to me. Because nothing can be compared to me. Neither in my attributes nor in my essence.

---

After stating his ahadiyat and samadiyat. His uniqueness and completeness. Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:لم یلد ولم یولد⟫

He did not father anyone.  nor has he been fathered. The old english terminology. he did not beget nor was he begotten. 

I'll skip over the grammaticla nuances of this ayah. But just know that there is a LOT of beautiful commentary by scholars about why He didn't say .   ⟪ar:لا یلدُ ولا یُولَدُ.⟫Allah used the word Lam. and not La. . Why he used past tense and not present tense.

And Lam forces the meaning of a verb to the past tense. So I'm translating. He DID not beget.  nor WAS he fathered. So the first thing we need to figure out is the benefit of the past tense in this ayah.  Why use the past tense? . why not say. He DOES not father. and he IS not fathered? why not? Well! the latter makes logical sense.

⟪ar:ولم یولد⟫ . makes sense. because birth happens in the past. so that makes sense. But then why not protect the shirk from the future too by saying ⟪ar:ولا یلد⟫ . He does not give birth. The problem with He does not give birth is. that does not necessarily negate that he did not give birth . it does not eliminate the possibiltiy that he did not father. So it leaves room for shirk in the past. so that's why allah used لم یلد . he covered the past tense and he covered the future tense. SubhanAllah

Anyway. what I want you to understand for our purpose. is how this ayah connects with the previous two ayats. The first two ayats already established that He is ahad and samad. unique and absolute. which means there is not going to be anyone comparable.  Now having a child.  what does it do?. A human being begets a human being. a cat gives birth to a cat. a dog to a dog. an animal gives birth to an equal. to someone of the same species. right? We've already established that he can't have a second. thats not possible for him.  Because having a child.  being born even.  means that you have a beginning and an end. And when you are born.  it naturally implies that you will also die! and the fact that you wer BORN . implies that you did not exist in this world at some point .  and that takes away from godhood and from divinity itself. So we never attribute those things to allah.  Allah says in another place
⟪ar-quote:أَنَّىٰ يَكُونُ لَهُۥ وَلَدٌۭ ؟.  وَلَمْ تَكُن لَّهُۥ صَحِبَةٌۭ⟫

How can he have a son? When he doesn't even have an associate? . or a spouse . One word for a spouse is ⟪ar:صاحب⟫. and another word for that is ⟪ar:کفو⟫. and that's coming ahead in the next ayah. Allah says
⟪ar-quote:ولم یکن لہ کفواً احد⟫

So now . If he doesn't give birth. and he is not begotten. Now that the issue of kids is out of the way. what about the spouse?

On a side note. interestingly the word kufu.  in arabic literature.  is also used for an enemy.  that is equal to you in battle.  Like if two guys are equally good in a fight.  they're kufu. and it's also used in marriage. HAHA. Enemy says it all. I'm kidding.

So why is spouse a Kufu?. Because THEY are the ENEMY. I'm kidding .

The word kufu is used. when someone is comparable to you. someone can go toe to toe with you. someone who is on par with you.  has the same skills as you . Has the same status. the same ranking. the same social circles as you.  such a person is called a kufu.

So you generally marry someone who is compatible with you. same as you. same level of intellect. the same interests etc. such a couple is called kufu of one another. Now this word is used for Allah AWJ. ⟪ar:ولم یکن لہ کفوا احد⟫ .  and he never had any counterpart. anyone that can be compared to him. anyone that could go toe to toe with Allah AWJ . all of this . is in the details of one single word.  what word is that?.  Ahad! . ⟪ar:قل ھو اللہ احد⟫ . Ahad is the primary word. the entire purpose of the Surah. every other word we're learning is a consequence of that word. Allah is Ahad. He is Ahad. therefore he is samad. He is Ahad. therefore he does not beget a child nor has been begotten. He is Ahad. therefore there is no one comparable to him.

Remember I told you that Allah change the normal pattern of how the word "Ahad" is used in the first ayah. It is supposed to be used ONLY in the negative sense. but Allah used it in a positive way. It's the same thing with this ayah. Grammatically what should have been said was.
⟪ar:ولم یکن أحدٌ  کفواً لہ⟫

And there is no one comparable to him. That should have been the grammatically expected sequence of this sentence. The lahoo should have been at the end.  but Allah rearranged it. and brought it in the beginning.

Now here is something that is very cool. from a grammatical stand point . and this is one of the amazing benefits of grammer. its a geeky subject to study but the benefits of it SubhanAllah. they ayah reads. ولم یکن لہ کفوا احد

this is actually not the expected grammatical sequence. It should have been.

ولم یکن أحدٌ  کفواً لہ۔۔۔۔ that should have been the grammatically expected sequence of this sentence. but Allah rearranged the sequence of the words. Ahad is at the end. and lahoo is in the beginning . and kufu is in the middle . In the actual sequence . allah was to be mentioned at the end . the one who was counter parting him was to mentioned in the beginning . so what did Allah change this sequence?

In this sentence what is the most important entity? laho refers to Allah, kufu to the counterpart . and ahad anyone else . so of these which is the most valuable word? Laho! and part of Arabic Rhetoric. الاھم الاول . the most important should come first . therefore Allah mentions himself before everything else. and one of the meanings of Ahad is الاول . not just لیس لہ ثانی . the one who has no second. but also the one comes first. And even in this sentence Rasul Allah mentions Allah first. because if he had not done that. it would have literally negated the first ayah. SubhanAllah. Spoken text!

And the reason He did that. is ⟪ar:اختصاص⟫. to single out. It is ONLY Allah . who does not have a counterpart. meaning everyone other than Him will necessarily have what?. A counter part!. If there is a general. there will be another general. if there is a king. there will be another king. if there is a president there will be another president . if you have one false god you.  you can have another false god. there will be one rich person there will be another rich person . you'll have one planet there will be another planet. one star another star. Everything that is in existence. everything that is creation . will have a kufu . But it is ONLY Allah that does not have kufu. And where did we get the ONLY HE part? We got it from this grammatically re-arranged sentence
⟪ar:ولم یکن لہ کفوا احد⟫ . because the lahu is earlier.

Even though we don't understand classical Arabic. we are still forced to appreciate the eloquence of this message. It took me what.five. six. sessions to explain Allah to you. Allah does it in 4 short . and simple sentences. without losing a fraction of its meaning. We human beings are just not capable of such perfection. If Allah really open up our hearts. this is kalaam. this Quran. is truly miraculous. leaves us completely defeated. incapable of a response. We have not choice BUT to submit. SubhanAllah.

---

And now the last thing . to wrap up this topic of Allah.

In one of the previous sessions I mentioned that. saying the name Allah. is equivalent to saying all the 99 names of Allah . Allah = 99 names. Some of you asked me. How is that?. How is Allah the sum of all 99 names put together?. And I promised you . I'd answer this question in the final session . of the word Allah.  And now that you understand Ahad and Samad. you'll InshaAllah be able to really appreciate this.

Imagine 99 different colors. each color being unique (Ahad). and each color being absolute (Samad). When you combine all these 99 colors together. what do you get in the end?. You get the PERFECT ILAH. AL-ILAH. You get ALLAH. The perfection of ALL his attributes . And now you know what you have to think when you hear the word perfect for Allah. you have to think unique and absolute.   So the perfection of ALL his attributes unite together. to manifest the perfection of His one true essence. which is named ALLAH.

### Aligning ILAH with IKHLAS

Let's look at some examples. I want you all to keep all the different defintions of the word Ilah in your mind.

One of the meanings of the word Ilah is. someone I completely submit to. right? . Now when we look at the PERFECT attributes of Allah. We see that he is jabbar. He is qahhar. The compeller, the subduer. He is AlKhafid. The abaser. He is Ar-Rafi. The exalter. He is Al-Qawi. The extremely powerful . And what do you do to someone who is the compeller, the subduer, the abaser, the exalter, the extremely powerful. ALL of that in the most unique and absolute sense. What do you do to someone with those attributes? You submit to them.  You understand? And the one you submit to . is called an Ilah. So you see how this works?

When we study the linguistic meanings of any of these 99 attributes. we find that they all trace back to one of the different meanings of the word Ilah. it's really incredible!

So for example. Ilah is the one we turn to for protection and refuge in our desperate times. Why do we turn to Allah in times of desperate need? .  Because He is AlWakeel. He is the trustee. He is Al-Wali. the most protecting friend. He is المانع. . the one who prevents harm. So because of these perfect attributes. He being trustworthy in the most unique and absolute sense. He being Walee. my protecting friend in the most unique and absolute sense. He being Al-Main. the one who prevents harm from reaching me. What is my natural reaction to that? . I turn to him for all my needs. And the one I turn to for all my needs is what? . An Ilah!

Ilah is the one we are passionately in love with. and are obsessed about. The kind of love. that if I lose him . I would become  like the مُوَلّا. like the mother who goes insane by the loss of her child. Now why do I have this crazy love for him?. Because he is Rehman. he is intensely merciful. Because he his Raheem. consistently merciful. in the most unique and absolute way.  Because he is Ghaffar. the always forgiving . in the most unique and absolute way.  Because He is Sattar. the one who constantly covers up my faults and sins. Imagine if the world knew every horrible thing you and I have done. Imagine if the world knew the crap going through my head all the time. I would not have a single friend in this world. But Allah has protected me from others knowing my sins and my faults. Because he is Sattar. the one who covers faults.again in the most unique and the most absolute way. He is AsSaboor. the extremely patient one. He is Al-Wadood. the extremely loving one. He is AlMujib. the one who responds to my every prayer.

So BECAUSE he is intensely merciful. always merciful. always forgiving. constantly forgiving. extremely loving. Always listening to my needs . السمیع. Always keeping an eye out for me. protecting me. البصیر.  Because He is all these things to me.in the most unique and absolute sense of the word.  my natural reaction to all of this is what? . It is that I'm passionately in love with Him .  I'm always thinking about Him. Again a defintion of the word Ilah.

Because He is AlMalik. the king. Because He is AlMutakabbir. the greatest. Because He is Al-Jaleel. the majestic. in the most unique and absolute way.  I am in awe of him. I am dumb founded by his glory. which is another meaning of the word Ilah.

So you see the word Ilah . encompasses the qualities of all 99 attributes. And because when it comes to Allah. these attributes are ahad and samad. they are unique and absolute. it makes him THE ILAH . or ALLAH for me. This is why calling him Allah. is equivalent to calling him by all his 99 names. because all 99 attributes . trace their meanings back to one of the various meanings of the word Ilah. AllahuAkbar. This is incredible. You can't make this stuff up!! . It's just too perfect.

I hope now you understand the relationship of the word ALLAH. with his 99 PERFECT attributes. ALL His attributes . connect back to one of the various meanings of the word Ilah. And this is why calling out to Him by his most majestic name ALLAH. is the same as calling him by his 99 attributes.  And BECAUSEHe is Allah. BECAUSE He is Ahad and Samad in all his attributes. What do we say? . We say . La Ilaha Illa Allah. We say. there is NO DIETY. There is NO ONE who is Ahad and Samad. Who is unique AND absolute. Both at the same time. Except ALLAH. THE ILAH. Now check this out.

[diagram: Numerological teaching diagram: two green boxes show 'صمد' (with abjad value 134) and 'احد' (with value 13). Below: '12 = 1+3+4 + 1+3'. A blue double-arrow at the bottom contains 'لا اله الا الله / 12 Letters', tying the digit-sums to the kalima's 12-letter count.]
  (see ../images/010.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:صمد · احد · لا اله الا الله⟫
  *Note:* Numerological link: digit-sums of al-Samad (134→1+3+4=8) and al-Ahad (13→1+3=4), totaling 12 — equal to the kalima's letter count.

And this is one of the reasons why this Surah is called Surat Al-Ikhlaas. Because Ikhlaas means sincerity. And sincerity is when we do something COMPLETELY and ONLY for the sake of Allah. Sincerity is when we make Allah unique in our lives. We put him BEFORE everything in our lives.  Ikhlaas. comes from the root word Khalasa. which means to make pure. And how do you make something pure?. By removing impurities. The more we understand the meanings of ahad and samad. the more we bring the practical applications of these two words in our daily lives. the higher we will rise in spiritual ranks. All progression. in spiritual ranks. All the ranks of Jannah. are based on our creation of Ikhlaas.  The greater our ikhlaas. the higher will be our ranks in the eys of Allah. That is the true purpose of creation. That is the true test before us. To come in the midst of creation. to come in the midst of temptations. And then to give up those temptations and desires. COMPLETELY . WILLINGLY . UNAPOLLOGETICLY . for the sake of Allah. That is the TRUE worship. And nobody reached the heights of Ikhlaas. Nobody practed the true principles of Allahs ahadiyat and samadiyat . other than Rasul Allah and Maulana Ali.

May Allah grant us all the knowledge. the wisdom. and create within us the burning need. to put Allah before everthing and everyone else.

<!-- section 7 (id=5742, raw_sort=7): Heart -->
---

⟪ar:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫

We studied the meaning of the word Allah. I hope by now you all have a good understanding of what this incredible word means.  linguistically. as well as what it's supposed to mean in our lives. The word Allah represents a concept. A concept of what Allah is supposed to mean in our lives. We also looked at how the meanings of the 99 attributes. they all tie back to one of the meanings of the word Allah.  These 99 attributes are a refraction of Allah's divine essence in this physical realm. ALL of Allah's creations. not just us human beings. but anything and everything that has been created . they're all manifesting the divine attributes of its creator.

Why have these attributes been placed within them? . It's placed in them as a reminder. as a reminder. as a SIGN. so that the creation never forgets who their creator is.

Isn't that what a sign or a logo is?. It's a reminder. That's all it is.  If you have any of the apple products. you will surely have the logo of an apple on it. Flying windows if you have a microsoft product. Every company imprints its logo on its product. so that the consumer never forgets who created that product.

So Allah . refracted his divine attributes in HIS products. within his creation. And then he gave us human beings . the intellect . the consciousness. to witness those attributes. Because no other creature. other than human beings. is fully aware of its existence. Human beings are the ONLY creation . that have been given this gift of awareness. And so He put his signs. his attributes.  all around us . and within us. . ⟪ar:سَنُرِيهِمْ آيَتِنَا فِى ٱلأٓفَاقِ وَفِىٓ أَنفُسِهِمْ⟫ .  so that we could constantly recognize these signs. and keep getting reminded. Reminded of what? . ⟪ar:حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَهُمْ أَنَّهُ ٱلْحَقُّ⟫ ۗ . until it becomes ABSOLUTELY CLEAR to us . that Allah is the ONLY truth.

So if you ask me. If you say to me. Asif mamu. you keep telling me Allah is magnificent. He is majestic. He is so glorious. How do I understand that? . how do I wrap my mind around around it. What does it mean that he is SO exalted and SO powerful. give me some example of that glory and majesty you speak of. What does he mean when he says in the Quran.

⟪ar:وھو الخلاق العظیم⟫  . He is the greatest of all creators.

I will tell you . look at the size of this universe!. And look at your own size in comparison to the size of that universe. And you will get some sense.  of where you stand in relation to Allah.  Because we human beings create. and Allah creates. Look what we're capable of creation . and look at what he created. Just reflect on the size of this universe for a second!. You know. Nasa has reported this. true or false. I don't know. but they say that from what we have observed through the eye of the telescope so far. we have found so many stars in the KNOWN universe. Not the unknown universe. JUST the known universe. they say we have found so many stars. that if you start counting these stars. at an interval of one star a second. So every second you count one star. it will take approximately 300 trillion years to count all of them. 300 trillion years. And this is JUST from the part of the universe that has been explored so far. ⟪ar:وھو الخلاق العظیم.⟫AllahuAkbar.

### Explanation of size of universe to Moosa

And we've known this all along. long before science found this out . The old testament talks about this in one of the old biblical stories . Moosa AS asked Allah. Ya Allah! When you commanded the heavesn and the earth to submit to you.

⟪ar-quote:فَقَالَ لَهَا ٱئْتِيَا طَوْعًا أَوْ كَرْهًۭا قَالَتَآ أَتَيْنَا طَآئِعِينَ⟫

Submit to me wether you do it willingly or unwillingly. They said we submit to you willingly. Had they refused to submit . what would you have done? . Allah replied. I would have unleashed a beast on them that would have swallowed both of them. Moosa started thinking. a beast that could swallow (not chew). because when you chew you have to break things down. You can only swallow something that is very small in size . So Moosa . completely amazed thinking. if this beast could swallow both the 7 heavens and the earth in one gulp. how big must be his jaw. his throat. his body. how big must this beast be to swallow the heavens and the earth!. So completely dazed . he asks Allah. ⟪ar:یا اللہ! أین تلک الدابۃ ؟⟫. Ya Allah. where is this beast?. Allah replied. ⟪ar:فی مَرجٍ مِن مروج⟫. He is gazing in one of my pastures. Moosa AS completely lost it. He was like . whaaaaa. Here he was thinking that the beast is huge. what is the size of a pasture compared to the beast?. If this beast can swallow the heavens and the earth in one gulp. to graze. how big must the pasture be. And then Allah said . فی مَرجٍ مِن مروج. in one of my pastures. meaning there are multiple pastures. Yes? . Moosa As asks. ⟪ar:این ذالک المرج؟⟫. Ya Allah where is this pasture? . Allah replies. ⟪ar:فی علمٍ من علومِ، موسی⟫ . Its in the treasures of my unseen knowledge Moosa!. What you are seeing around you is not even a tiny fraction of what I have created. ⟪ar:وھو الخلاق العظیم⟫. He is the greatest of all creators

And I think this story is remarkable. considering it's being said several thousand years ago when man didn't have ANY knowledge of what the size of this universe is . So Allah created this immense universe. Because He is Kabeer. He is Jaleel. He is Musawwar. the fashioner. He is Azeem . the great.  And if you want to understand how powerful He is. then just think about how long would it take YOU and I . ALL human beings combined. to create a fully functional universe of this size. And then think about how ALlah created this universe . with his single command. Kun . Be. Fa Yakoon. and it was.

So Allah created this universe around us . as a constant reminder for us. so that we never forget. who HE is.

Life is a journey

See . whether we like it or not.  we are all in a  journey. And every journey has a beginning. it  has a middle . and it has an end. And we are in the middle right now.  This worldly life is actually the middle.  and anything that is in the middle is in a temporary. transitionary phase.  It is not something that is permanent. because it is not the destination. 

There are these three worlds. There is the ⟪ar:عالم الجبروت⟫. the world of omnipotence. That's where Allah resides. Then there is the ⟪ar:عالم الملکوت⟫. which is the spiritual world . and then there is this ⟪ar:عالم المُلک⟫ . The physical world. And Allah is the Malik. He is the king. He is  ⟪ar:مالک الجبروت و مالک الملکوت و مالک الملک⟫

He is the owner of these three realms. He is the king of the Mulk, the Malakoot and the Jabaroot. So this world that we live in . this is the lowest of all the worlds. and it comes out of the Malakoot. the spiritual realm in which Allah created us. And the malakoot comes from the jabaroot.

So when we were in the Malakoot. in the spiritual realm. we were in the state of observation. ⟪ar:مشاہدۃ⟫. And this is why Allah. he made all the souls testify. اشھد الارواح. And what did he make them testify?. ⟪ar:الست بربکم؟⟫. Am I not your lord?. ⟪ar:بلا شھدنا⟫. we all  replied. No doubt we testify!. and all of us testified regardless of what our belief is today. weather we believe in a Allah or not. doesn't matter. We all testified. We were all made witness to Allah AWJ. and we all testified.

And then when we transitioned into this physical realm. Allah  put our soul into this vessel which is the body.   much like a bird in the cage.  So we're in this cage.  and this cage is made up of flesh and blood. This is the mulk. This body of ours is from the mulk. It's made from this earth. But the rooh. the soul that resides within this body . that's from the Malakoot.  and so.  the soul is a prisoner inside this body. And every prisoner will leave the prison at the end of its sentence. He's going to move on and return to the world he came from.  Just like when you open the cage.  the bird flies out and leave the cage behind.  and it does not look back.  If you open the cage the bird will fly out and it will not look back at the cage.  it just flies out and it's gone. So we came into this world.  and so what happens is.  that when you come in this world.  See the nature of this world is zulmaani. it is darkness. But the nature of the malakoot is noor. it is light. and Allah created the heavens and the earth from light.
⟪ar-quote:ٱللَّهُ نُورُ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ. ⟪ar-quote:ٱللَّهُ مُنَوِّرُ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ⟫⟫

Allah is the illuminator of the heavens and the earth.  All of this physical realm came from light.  There was a time when all of this was light.  and then there was a degradation that took place.  and the light dimmed. and eventually degraded into darkness . and this physical world came into existence. 

And so Allah AWJ. has made us human beings. this. this interstitial space.
⟪ar-quote:سَنُرِيهِمْ آيَتِنَا فِى ٱلأٓفَاقِ وَفِىٓ أَنفُسِهِمْ⟫

I will show them my signs in the horizon. If you look at the horizon. the horizon is the meeting place of the heavens and the earth.  the horizon is where the heavens and the earth meet.  and you can only really see this in the ocean. Ocean is the place where you can really see the heavens and the earth meet at the horizon . And Allah says that we will show them in their existence . that this is the meeting place. of the heavens and the earth. their soul and their body. Human being is where the soul and the body. the heaven and the earth. the malakoot and the mulk. they both come together. Allah made human beings the microcosm. against the microcosm for our solar system. The horizon is the macrocosm. and we are its microcosm.

### Microcosm Macrocosm - Reminder

Because today. modern science wants to tell us that we are insignificant. right? We are nothing. Science today tries to reduce us to nothing. They say look.  you're from an insignificant planet . in an insignificant solar system . in an insignificant galaxy . in the midst of billions of galaxies. You are nothing. And  that is all true.  they are not lying.  but if you go inside a human being.  all of those vast spaces that are out there in the solar system.  in the horizon.  they are also in you.  inside you. Maulana Ali said. 
⟪ar-quote:وتـَحسب أنك جِرم صغير . وفيكَ انطوى العالمُ الأكبرُ⟫

you think you are some insignificant speck . Indeed within you exists all of the cosmos.  all of the cosmos are in you. This is from one of the verses of Maulana Ali's poems .

⟪ar-quote:لدواؤك فيـكَ وما تـُبصـِـرُ . وداؤك منـــكَ وما تشــعرُ

وتـَحسب أنك جِرم صغير . وفيكَ انطوى العالمُ الأكبرُ⟫

Your medicine . your cure . is within you . but you do not see it. Your problems exist BECAUSE of you. but you are not aware of it

You think that you are an insignificant thing. but this entire universe around you exists within you

We have organs within our bodies. each an independent planet. performing its own function . as well as working together to keep the human body alive and functional. If we have shining stars in the sky. we have eyes that shine with light. If there are oceans and rivers flowing within this world. we have blood flowing within our veins. If there are mountains . with deep caves in it. reflect on the structure of the nose and nostrills . If there are trees and forests in the world . we have hair and facial hair . If there are minerals and metals in this earth. we have bones and teeth and nails. If this earth contains the 4 primary elements . of water, fire, earth, air. we too have all those 4 elements inside us . in the form of heat, water, gases and carbon. If this world goes through 4 seasons . of spring, summer, fall and winter. our life goes through 4 seasons of birth, childhood, youth and old age. If this world is capable of producing beautiful soothing sounds like the sounds of waterfall, and rain. and the music of winds and the oceans. And at the same time . if this world is capable of producing loud and harsh noises like that of thunder. human beings too are capable of both. beautiful speech as well as horrodeous speech. If this world is a state of constant change. human beings are in a state of constant change. I as an individual. You as an individual. we are an entire solar system. that exists in the galaxy of our families. Each member of our family is an entire solar system on its own. living with other families. other galaxies. within communities. that exists within towns. that exists within states. that exists within countries. so now you tell me. aren't we human beings . the perfect symbol of these billions of galaxies that contain billions of solar systems?. Because we too are billions of people . living in billions of families. each operating independently as a complete universe.

You think you are an insignificant thing. This entire universe exists within you

The hearing and the sight. they all affect the soul. and this is why what you look at will affect you. what you will listen to . it will affect your soul.

### Learn Islam from a child

A child constantly manifests the beautiful attributes of Allah . because it has witnessed those attributes in the Malakoot. And that is why it is so easy to love a child. Doesn't even have to be my own child. The love comes gushing out of when we take a child in our hands. because he is subconsciously reminding us of the love of Allah that we once had.

You wanna learn about Islam. learn it from a child. No one exhibits the traits of Islam like a child does. And that is why Rasul Allah said.

Study of the heart

So when Allah created us in this physical realm. and put his divine attributes in ALL of his creation . outside us AND inside us. ⟪ar:فی الافاق وفی الانفس⟫ .  He gave us a gift. He gave us something very special . that could help us recognize these attributes. and that could help us connect back with Him. And that is the heart. He gave us  a heart. a qalb. which a medium to see and recognize his divine glory. He gave us this spiritual heart. and he made it the center of our consciousness. so that we can recoginize his attributes. his signs. his logo in everything around us. 

And he made the physical heart. a symbol for that spiritual heart.

Just look at the physical heart. It is THE most astonishing organ of the body. We now know. that the human heart is pulsating approximately 40 million times a year. In an average human lifespan.  your heart will pulsate about 3 billion times. It takes about 40 gallons of blood in our. If you get 40 buckets. Not 40 gallons. Just 40 buckets.  and you fill them with water. and start moving those buckets from one room to another. You'll see how quickly you get tired. right? . And yet this extraordinary organ that Allah has put into our bodies. it continues to pump throughout our lives.  effortlessly. Not asking us for ANYTHING in return. Not even asking us to tell it to pump this blood for us.

And what's even more unusual is that we now know that the human heart. is not only self-regulating. it begins beating before there is a central nervous system. During embryonic development, the heart is one of the few organs that must function almost as soon as it is formed. And the fact.  that the heart is one of the earliest organs to develop speaks.  to its importance. The human heart begins to beat and pump blood through the embryo around the 22nd day of pregnancy. Who made the heart beat before there was even a central nervous system? Who made the heartbeat? The one who created the heart made it beat. And sustain its beat. Why? . Because it is the heart that has been created to recognize Allah. That's why it is the first thing that develops to symbolize the human need.  of understanding its maker. And it keeps doing its job until one day it stops beating. And then this form called the soul. Rooh.  leaves this physical realm and goes into a different realm.

And this heart. this Qalb. Qalb is spelled. Qaf laam and ba. Now if you take those letters and you switch them around. You get the word qabal. which means to come before. To preceed. To be the first and foremost.  And there is this science in the Arabic language . that when you switch the letters around. For example you have a word like ⟪ar:علم⟫. Which means knowledge. When you switch the same letters around you get the word ⟪ar:عمل⟫. Which means action. Because knowledge is related to action. So when the letters of a word are switched around to form a different word. they're always connected in meaning. This is another miraculous aspect of the Arabic lanuage. And that's why Qalb and Qabl. heart and to preceed . or to come before are related. And then the word Qabl and Qibla are also related.And Qibla means direction. And a direction is always pointed towards a destination. If there is no destination. there is no need for directions. So then.  what is the direction of the heart?.  Who is the destination of the heart? . It's the one it learnt about . BEFORE it learnt anything else? Who is this heart yearning for? Who is it pointing to. Who is it taking precedence for? Its doing it for Allah! . Because the heart knows something. that it knew even BEFORE it came into this realm. You see the heart knows.Alastu be rabbikum. Am I not your lord?

The heart knows the answer to that question. Am I not your master? Bala shahidna. Indeed we testify that you are . So every human heart that came into this world knows this truth. this spiritual truth. I bet you're feeling it right now. because everything that I'm saying . you already know that its the truth .

So we were made a witness in the spiritual realm. and now in this physical realm the . human being has been given the task of testifying again. by recognizing the divine attributes of his master within the horizons and his soul. He is tasked with repeating his testimony. the same testimony that he gave in the primordeal world. with Allah AWJ. He has to now testify that same thing in this physical world. with Sidq. ⟪ar:صدقاً من قلبہ⟫ .  testify the truth. with sincerity of heart.

### Heart is saying LA ILAHA ILLA ALLAH

And what does he need to testify? What is it. that the heart needs to see. understand. believe and then testify? What is that? It is ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ . It has to testify that there is no Ilah. except Allah. he needs to purfiy the uniqueness and absoluteness. the ahadiyat and samadiyat. of Allah. from all His creation. He needs to purify his faith. Purify with what? . With his heart. and what is the human heart constantly doing. even in the physical realm? . It is purifying blood. SubhanAlah! . It is constantly working to exchange the deoxygenated blood . with the oxygenated blood. Oxygen is life. Eman . faith is spiritual life. It is constantly exchange kufr . for Emaan. and then supplying that oxygenated blood to the various parts of the body.

And so the human heart has been made a symbol for the spiritual heart.  Why has He made it a symbol? Because Allah (SUBHANHU WA TA'ALA) is manifesting himself from an unseen realm. You see . in the spiritual realm Allah was manifest. he was Zaahir. But in this physical realm he is Baatin. He is hidden. Allah has hidden himself from us. by manifesting himself. through his attributes.  in creation . from an unseen realm. And it is only the human heart. the spiritual heart that can recognize this.And this is why the heart is the organ of cognition. It's not the brain.

Now why does the heart beat? . Why does the heart beat? . Why does it go from contraction to expansion? . You see. Diastolic. Systolic. Why does it do that? . There are lots of ways you could get the blood around to the different parts of the body . without a beat. Why did Allah make it a beat? . And then why did Allah make the breadth. expansion and contraction?

. See . doctors can tell you the how. A doctor can tell you how the heart beats. HOW it gets the blood to the body. How the expansion and contraction works. but whaty they can't tell you is the WHY. And so they say. I don't know if its true or not. quite a few doctors present in the group. But I heard they say . that the easiest way to stump a doctor. is to switch from how to why.

So why did Allah create this process of the heart through contraction and expansion?

Doctors can't answer that. Because medical science can explain the how. How does the heart beat?. medical science can explain that. Why does it beat?. Why isn't there a different mechanism to pump the blood. THAT science cannot explain.  But the Quran can!. The heart beats . it expands and contracts. because one of the attributes of Allah is AlBaasit. he is the expander. He is AlBasit and he is Al-Qabid. He is the Expander and the contractor. And that's what the heart is constantly doing. It is constantly contracting and expanding. Why? Because it needs to testify. It needs to testify that there is no Ilah except Allah. That's La Ilaha . Illa Allah.

La Ilaha. that's the contraction. That's negation of all Ilah. narrowing down all forms of false deities. contracting the space. removing and squeezing out every drop of deoxygenated blood.  until there is no Ilah left in our lives. That is contraction. That is La Ilaha . .  And then there is Illa Allah. filling it back with the life giving oxygen of Emaan. of faith. Recognizing and affirming Allah . THROUGH his divine attributes. and testifiying that there is ONLY Allah.  That's expansion . That's the oxygenated blood being pushed into every tissue . every muscle of our spiritual deeds. Our salaah. our fasts. our zakaat . our hajj.  The spiritual heart is constantly beating to the tune of La Ilaha. Illa Allah. It is contracting and expanding. to testify a message that is made up of contraction and expansion.

La Ila Illa Allah. is the beat of our spiritual hearts. It is what's constantly removing shirk and kufr from our actions. and replacing it with the life giving oxygen of faith. And its a continuous and constant process of purification. just as the heart is constantly and continuously engaged in the purification of the blood. Once the hearts stops pumping. what happens to the body? . It dies. What happens to the spiritual heart. that stops purifying itself from shirk and kufr?. It dies.

### Pronunciation of word Allah

And now look at how the word Allah is pronounced. When you hear the heart through a stethoscope. Doctors say. it's lubbadubb. right? . They say it's making that lubb a dubb. sound. But when one of the Imams was asked. I hear my heart beating and making a sound. What is my heart saying? . The imam replied. It's saying.  Allah. Allah. Now if you actually listen to the sound. you don't hear the word Allah. right?.  So then what did the Imam mean? . This is not the word of an ordinary man. these are the words of an Imam.

⟪ar:کلام الامیر. امیر الکلام⟫

speech of a king. and the king of all speech.

So what does it mean that the heart is saying Allah?. If you look at how this name Allah is pronounced. It is a also a contraction and an expansion. That's what it is. That's what the tongue is doing. All-lah! All-laah. That's what its doing. Say the word Allah right now. and see what happens when you pronounce the laam? You have to PRESS your tongue against top of your mouth. That's contraction. That's La Ilaha.  and then you need to expand the tongue.  bring it down. opening your mouth. to complete it. That's expansion. That's Illa Allah.  The name Allah is contraction and expansion. La Ilaha Illah Allah is contraction and expansion. In both contraction is first. expansion is second.

The heart is constantly contracting and expanding. calling out to its master. Allah. because the heart remembers its master. But the nafs. the soul. has forgotten who its master is. And this is because. we have become tainted with the duniya. we have become so involved in this physical and material world. that we have forgetten who our lord is. And that's why Allah SWT. sent us messengers. to remind us who our master is. so that we can return. so that we can return to him.

See we as Muslims today. as sulemanis. our hearts are dead. We went into auto-pilot a long time ago. And now we're into this state called "Ghafla". or heedlessness. And that's what a pilot does when he gets up in the air. If you ever open that cockpit door. you'll have a heart attack. because they're snoring. they're in deep sleep. and the plane is on auto pilot. And that's what has happened to us. We've gone into this mechanical mode. We say Allah Akbar. Allah is great. without actually meaning it in anyway. We start our namaz and few minutes later forget which rakaat we're in. Did i do one sajda or two sajda?

That is why in Islam. everything begins with an intention.  A niyah? Why is that?. Because the intention controls the action.  And where does intention lie?

⟪ar-quote:محلُ النِّیَّۃ القلب⟫

The place of intention is in the heart. But we say the niyah. and we go into auto pilot. This is what we do. We go to sleep. And then there are different levels and degress  of sleep. That's why Maulana Ali said. ⟪ar:الناس النیام⟫. People of this world are in a state of sleep.

Someone asked Maulana Ali. What is all of this? What is all this creation? . He replied.

ھباءٌ لا یُرَا اِلَّا حِ‏ینَ ما یَقَعُ عَلَیہِ النُّورَ اللہ

This is like the dust in the air that only becomes visible when the light of Allah strikes it. You see this was an Arif Billah. He was a man who knews Allah SWT. What a profound description of the atomic realm . All of these atoms that are floating in this etherial space that Alah has created. And the only reason it is visible is because Allah is Noor AsSamaawat wal Ard. Allah illuminated the heavesn and the earth . And heart is the organ of the human being that is capable of perceiving that light in the most profound and deep ways.

Our hearts.  is a precious gift from Allah . and we have to protect this precious gift. Just look where he put it. He put it behind the sternum. the strongest thing in the body . and then he put a rib cage around it. he didn't put it like the other organs that are out there. where a person has no protection. And that's why if you want to bring down a man in martial arts. that's the first thing they teach you. Go for the groin. because there is no protection. because both physicaolly and spiritually. it is the most inferior ranking organ of the body. But for the heart. Allah put a protection there. A powerful protection. And then he gave it . this oscilating power . in which the blood is flowing in every single cell of the body with every pulse. That's the reason . blood reaches every single cell of the body.

### Entrainment

And if you know anything about oscilatory physics. that's a big word I just learnt so I'm using it. Oscilitory physics is the study of entrainment. how things entrain with other things. The word entrain means. when there is a rhythym. which causes other things to gradually fall into synchronism with it. When the rhythym of oscillating device. synchronizes the rhythym of another device. that's called entrainment .

We know soldiers entrain naturally . when they march. It becomes hard to walk with someone out of step. You naturally entrain and sync up with the steps of the other person.right? And that's why soldiers naturally entrain. And this entrainment results in amplification. which is even more frightning. You know what happens to a bridge when soldiers walk in entrainment. right? . That's the first thing taught to every engineer. When soldiers walk on a bridge in one step. the force of the weight . gets amplified exponentially. because it was all together. you see. And that's the power of being unified. When you are unified. you have power. And when you are disunited. you are weak.

Now the heart. the beats of the spiritual heart. understanding the meaning of this beat of La Ilaha Illa Allah. it entrains the mind, the body and the soul. And when this entrainment occurs. when everything gets synchrnoized. there is exponential amplification in the form of actions. The intensity of every action changes.

And that's why Rasul Allah said.

{{IMG_URL:http://www.livingislam.org/m/_img2/qalbbodyGC430.png}}

Know that in the body of a human being. there is a lump of flesh. if it is sound the entire body is sound. and if it is corrupt the entire body is corrupt. why? Because the entire body is in entrainment with the heart. If the heart is diseased. the entrainment will be diseased. If the heart is sound. the entrainment will be sound. La Ilaha Illa Allah. is the constant entrainment for the soul. Look at salaah. which is the practical application of this testimony. La Ilaha Illa Allah. The heart is towards Allah . and the body is towards Qibla. Everything is being entrained all at the same time. And then there is the sajda. the ultimate contraction. I told you. sajdah in ancient arabic means when the camel relinquishes its control. and submits to the will and command of its master. In Sajda we are contracting the entire body. bringing everything close together. isnt' that the case?. And we are placing our foreheads. that which contains our intellect. we place that intellect on the ground . And we do that. to elevate the heart. That's an incredible gesture. During our day to day life. when we are standing up or sitting down. the intellect is always above the heart isn't it? . Sajda in salaah. is a deliberate action.  of lowering the intellect in order to elevate the heart. it is symbol. that highlights the precedence of the heart OVER the intellect. SubhanAllah. There is not a single action in this beautiful relgion that is without profound wisdom in it.

And so we really need to protect our hearts. we have to protect this amazing gift of Allah. because just as the physical heart dies. the spiritual heart can also die. And so in order to keep the spiritual heart alive. we have the knowledge of this Quran. This is why we have

⟪ar-quote:تلاوۃ القرآن بالتدبر⟫

Reading the Quran with reflection. And this is important. becausae you need to know why. Why things happen?. Once you understand why Allah AWJ has asked us to do these things. it strengthens the heart . and you develop a desire to fulfill that thing. Because you are now using your intellect. and when the intellect is behind something. it is not the same . as when you are just following something blindly. To believe with conviction is a powerful belief. When there is conviction. there is action. And when there is action. there is change. And so you will change. and things around you will change. So the recitation of Quran with understanding and reflection what keeps the heart alive .

<!-- section 8 (id=5745, raw_sort=8): Meaning of Rehman and Raheem -->
We looked at the meaning of the word Allah. And now InshaAllah today we'll begin looking at his two attributes AlRehman and AlRaheem. 

To quickly recap. Allah comes from the word Ilah. with the AL applied to it. So Allah is AL+ILAH. And because of the grammatical rules of Arabic there is ⟪ar:اِضغَام⟫. there is annexaction. the Alif of Ilah drops. and then the two laam. they merge . and you get Allah. So with this exclusivity clause applied to the word Ilah. Allah then becomes the one I should completely submit to. the one I should be truly loyal to. He is someone I turn to for protection and refuge in my desperate times. He is someone I am passionately in love with. someone I am obsessed about. He is beyond my imagination. and beyond my  capabilities of comprehension and understanding. He is someone who's glory and majesty dumb-founds me. everytime I try to approach Him. He is someone I can completely trust. lean on . put my entire weight on knowing that He will not let me fall.  And finally . and most important meaning of all . He is the one I worship. And as I explained earlier. worship or عبادۃ  in Arabic means two things. It means worship and it means obedience. both stemming from the sum of all these different meanings of the word Ilah.

And then we looked that perfection of his attributes. perfect because they are unique and they are absolute. which then makes him worthy of my worship. Because the one who is worthy of worship. must naturally be characterized by ALL the attributes of perfection. All attributes of Majesty. All attributes of glory. So Because Allah is Allah . He must also be Ghafoor. Because Allah is Allah . He must also be AlReheem . Because Allah is Allah . He must also be AsSamee AlAleem etc. So each and every attribute of Allah. by nature of its being unique. and by nature of its being absolute. it is an explanation of why Allah is Allah. And because he has these 99 PERFECT attributes. that is why Allah is worthy of my worship.

---

Now that we studied the meaning of the word Allah and his attributes. we find two attributes mentioned along with his name. AlRehman and AlRaheem. Now out of all of his 99 attributes . why did Allah choose these two specific attributes? And notice that this is not the only verse in which he used these 2 attributes.  Just one verse later . After he says.⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العلمین⟫. he immediately says again. AlRehman AlRaheem. So we can see. right off the bat. that this surah highlights these two attributes. indicating how important they are to allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . For example if I say. Erum is my daughter and and I love her. I REALLY love her !!.  What did I just do?.  I'm stating two facts. The first that Erum is my daughter. And the second that I love her. But then by saying I lover her AGAIN. what I'm doing. is I'm HIGHLIGHTING my love for her. I am giving MORE importance to the fact . that I love her . than the fact that she is my daughter. you understand?

---

So now let's understand the meaning of these two words AlRehman and AlRaheem. The meanings are SO incredibly beautiful. I remember I had goosebumps when I first experienced the beauty of these words.

First lets look at how these two words are commonly translated. If you open any english translation. you will find. With the name of Allah. the most gracious. the most merciful. OR. The merciful the merciful . The most beneficient the most merciful. the merciful the most kind. the merciful the beneficient. the beneficient the beneficient. 

The thing is. these words are so difficult to process in English. When do you ever use the word beneficient in your normal day to day conversation?.  Like if somebody helped you with something. Oh! Jee You are so beneficient.  You don't do that.  I at least don't.  My point is.  the purpose of translation is that.  we get to understand the text. but if we start using words for translation that we ourselves do not use and cant relate to. then it defeats the whole purpose. We need to have translations that are close to the text.  but then they also need to be close to us. Thats how translation makes sense.

[diagram: Teaching diagram of the root r-ḥ-m (mercy). Bottom box: the root 'رحم' surrounded by clouds 'SUBTLE / ONE SIDED / PROTECTION / STRUGGLE'. Arrow up to 'رحمۃ' labelled 'Unconditional LOVE / CARE / Genuine CONCERN / MERCY'. From there, two arrows up to 'الرحیم' (labelled 'PERMANENT NOT EXTREME') and 'الرحمن' (labelled 'EXTREME IMMEDIATE TEMPORARY').]
  (see ../images/011.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:الرحیم · الرحمن · رحمۃ · رحم⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical: contrasts the divine names al-Rahman (intense + immediate mercy) and al-Rahim (sustained mercy) as derived from the root rḥm and the noun raḥma.

Both these words . AlRehman and AlRaheem. they both have to do with the word ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. Thats the underlying word for both these words AlRehman and AlRaheem. And the word ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. it is generally understood as Mercy. but that's not the best translation for the word Rehmah. I'm not saying its the wrong translation. I'm saying it's a weak translation. Because the word mercy is generally used in the English language when you are being spared from a punishment. In other words, the soldiers showed no mercy . What does that mean? It means they did not spare anyone . The criminal ask the judge for mercy . In other words he asked the judge to be spared . So generally the idea of mercy, is that something bad was about to happen and then someone intervened and showed you mercy . You understand?. So there is  a subconscious association with punishment when the word mercy is used . and then the concept of getting away from that punishment. In mercy . the default position is punishment. Now, if we use that word mercy constantly for Allah . And we repeat it over and over again for him . Then it sort of brings up the idea that Allah wanted to do something bad to us and then he decided not to do it . Therefore he spared us and showed us mercy  . In other words, when Allah is being merciful. what he is actually doing . is sparing me from punishment.But that is not the true intent of the word Rehmah. Rehma has nothing to do with punishment. it has no concept of the word punishment in it.

Rehma in classical Arabic has 4 meanings.

1. Unconditional love. 2. care. 3. genuine concern. and 4. mercy. 

Mercy is the last piece of it. not the first.  Love is first . then care then concern. and then mercy. This is Rehma.

When we call Allah Rehman and Raheem. we acknowledge 4 things. that Allah has INTENSE love for us. he cares for us. he is genuintely concerned about us. and He shows us mercy. That is the implict acknowlegment in any word that derives from the word ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. And another thing to understand about this word Rehma is. it means to show love and care.  in order to bring benefit to someone.

⟪ar-quote:رِقَّۃٌ تَقتَدِ الأحسانُ أِلی المَرحوم⟫

It is a love or tenderness that is intended to benefit the beloved. So ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫is not JUST love and care. it is a type of love and care that is intended to benefit. it actually ends up benefiting the beloved.So if you have real ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. it will translate into action. and not just in theory .  And by deriving these two words from the same root word. that is AlRehman and AlRaheem. By deriving these two words . Allah is emphasizing his loving nature. He is emphasizing that he has ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. and he is characterized by ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. This is a trait. a characteristic. that is EXTREMELY important to Allah. There are many ayats in the Quran in which Allah mentions his ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫by saying . ⟪ar:و من رحمتہ⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن رَّحْمَتِهِۦ جَعَلَ لَكُمُ ٱلَّيْلَ وَٱلنَّهَارَ⟫

out of his love. he created the night and the day

⟪ar-quote:مِّن رَّحْمَتِهِۦ وَيُهَيِّئْ لَكُم مِّنْ أَمْرِكُم مِّرْفَقًۭا⟫

out of his love he will make your tasks easy for you

⟪ar-quote:وَمِنْ آيَتِهِۦٓ أَن يُرْسِلَ ٱلرِّيَاحَ مُبَشِّرَتٍۢ وَلِيُذِيقَكُم مِّن رَّحْمَتِهِ⟫

out of his love he sends the winds that delivers good tidings

⟪ar-quote:مَّا يَفْتَحِ ٱللَّهُ لِلنَّاسِ مِن رَّحْمَةٍۢ فَلَا مُمْسِكَ لَهَاۖ⟫

When allah opens the doors of his love. no one can close them

And the purpose of all of this is to explain one thing to us. We've talked about Allah being our master. right?.  And when you think of the word master. you think of the word authority. and when you think of authority. the LAST thing you think of is what? . Unconditional Love! . And Allah is telling us right away. Right after mentioning his name Allah. He is telling us. I am a different kind of master. You will NEVER EVER find a master in this world . who is AS POWERFUL as me. YET has the kind of ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫that I have.

You pick any other master in this world. they will not give you unconditional love the way I will love you. They'll tell you what to do. They will force you to fulfill their needs and desires. they will judge you by THEIR standards. not by your capabilities. but by their own standards.  They'll put you through painful punishments when you don't obey. They might even take care of you once in a while. but they will NEVER love you.  Isn't that the case? . Isn't this true of every other master who owns a slave. Masters will always only give love to their own. but they will never love their slave. But this master. OUR master. Allah. he says the VERY first emotion that I have towards you. is unconditional love!. Any other master will not care about you. but I will always care about you. No other master will genuinely be concerned about you. I will ALWAYS be concerned for you . No other master will show you mercy when you disobey them. or do not complete the job up to THEIR standards. But I will ALWAYS have mercy on you. My judgment will be . not by MY standards. but by YOUR capabilities.

And In a hadees . Rasul Allah(SAWAS) said. then when Allah created the creation. He wrote a rule book for himself. He made something compulsory upon himself. Think about this for a second. Allah as our master . And in our interactions with him.  he has made certain things compulsory on us. He made salaah, hajj, zakaat, saum. all of these things compulsory on us. These are all forms of our interaction with him. But then when it came to his interaction with us. he too made something compulsory upon himself. Rasul Allah(SAWAS) said Allah wrote a rule book for himself. that he keeps over his throne.

⟪ar-quote:إن الله لَمَّا قضى الخلق.  كتب فوق عرشه⟫

And in that rule book he wrote.

⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:اِنَّ رَحمَتِی تَغلِبُ غَضَبِی⟫⟫

My love and my care for my creation. will ALWAYS extinguish my wrath.  My ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫will always extinguish my anger. My ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫will always overcome my wrath. Allah has made it compulsory. He has made it mandatory upon himself. that whenever he will deal with his creations . His dealings will always be motivated by love and care. And his love will ALWAYS overpower his anger.  He has imposed this rule of love and care upon himself for us . SubhanAllah.
