And there is another hadees. in which Rasul Allah said. that Allah has 70 times more love and care for his slaves. than a mother has for her child.  This world that we live in. the best exhibition of Rehma. the best exhibition of mercy. the best display of love and care . is that what a mother has for her child. This is the highest example for our imagination. And what did Rasul Allah say? He said. Indeed. I swear.  Allah's love for his slaves is 70 times more . than a mother has for her child. . Thats why some people in their supplications . they would quote this hadees and say. Oh Allah. your prophet has told us that your love and mercy for me is more than the mercy of my own mother for me. and i know that my mother would not want to see me in pain and in suffering. so Allah. with your mercy. remove my pain and suffering. Oh Allah! no mother wants to see her child burn in hell. Oh Allah. with your mercy. forgive my sins and draw me closer to yourself.

So both words AlRehman and AlRaheem . they come from this word ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫.

---

Now let's look at these two words.   AlRehman and AlRaheem. Let's first understand Rehman.

Al-Rehman

This specific attribute of AlRehman . it has certain characteristics that no other attribute has. And these are interesting to note because it highlights the importance of this attribute. 

The most prominent characteristic is that this is a name that ONLY applies to Allah. it is not used for anyone OTHER than Allah. You can call a human being Raheem. If a person is very loving and caring and shows mercy. you can call him Raheem. But you can never use the word Rehman for another human being. That is just for Allah. In fact. this attribute is SO important to Allah. that he equates it with his ⟪ar:اسم الجلالۃ⟫. the name of his essence. Allah. He says.

⟪ar-quote:قُلِ ٱدْعُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ أَوِ ٱدْعُوا۟ ٱلرَّحْمَنَ ۖ أَيًّۭا مَّا تَدْعُوا۟ فَلَهُ ٱلْأَسْمَآءُ ٱلْحُسْنَىٰ⟫

Allah says . Call upon Allah OR call upon AlRehman. which ever name you choose.  know that to him belongs all the beautiful names. So Allah quite literally said, to call upon Allah or to call upon AlRehman. doesn't matter. they're both the same. So it is almost like he highlighted the name AlRehman  and made it complementary to the name Allah.

Another speciality that this name AlRehman has.  is that it is the ONLY name of Allah. that Allah revealed an entire Surah to explain. That is Surah AlRehaman. Allah did not reveal a surah named AlMalik, AlQuddus, AlSalaam, AlAziz, AlJabbar. NO. But AlRehman is the only name of Allah that exists in the form of a surah. And every single Ayah of Surah AlRehman is an explanation of the word Rehman.

He is ⟪ar:‏ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ‎⟫Why?⟪ar:عَلَّمَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ⟫. Because He taught him the Quran

He is ⟪ar:‏ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ‎⟫Why?⟪ar:خَلَقَ ٱلْإِنسَنَ⟫. Because He created man

He is ⟪ar:‏ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ‎⟫Why?⟪ar:عَلَّمَهُ ٱلْبَيَانَ⟫ . Because he taught him how to articulate

and on an on an on. Every single ayah of Surah AlRehman is an explanation of why AlRehman is AlRehman. And there is no other name that Allah chose to reveal an entire surah on.

Another interesting fact is that the name Allah . typically occurs all by itself in the Quran. Because we know that all other attributes of Allah are mentioned as pairs in the Quran. When you read the Quran. typically the attributes occur together in pairs. ⟪ar:السمیع العلیم؛ الغفور الرحیم؛ العزیز الحیم⟫ .  The names of Allah typically occur in pairs in the Quran. but the name Allah itself.  rarely occurs with any other name. and so does the attribute AlRehman. it NEVER occurs with any other attribute . except Raheem.

⟪ar-quote:رَّبِّ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا ٱلرَّحْمَنِ⟫

⟪ar-quote:يَوْمَ يَقُومُ ٱلرُّوحُ وَٱلْمَلَٓئِكَةُ صَفًّۭا ۖ لَّا يَتَكَلَّمُونَ إِلَّا مَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ ٱلرَّحْمَنُ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قُلْ هُوَ ٱلرَّحْمَنُ آمَنَّا بِهِ⟫

⟪ar-quote:مَّا تَرَىٰ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلرَّحْمَنِ مِن تَفَوُتٍۢ⟫

So Rehman always comes independently. and when it is paired. it is always and only paired with Raheem.  as in

⟪ar-quote:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫

⟪ar-quote:هُوَ ٱللَّهُ ٱلَّذِى لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ۖ عَلِمُ ٱلْغَيْبِ وَٱلشَّهَدَةِ ۖ هُوَ ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَإِلَهُكُمْ إِلَهٌۭ وَحِدٌۭ ۖ لَّآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ٱلرَّحْمَنُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ⟫

And there are VERY profound reasons for it. but that's beyond the scope of our sessions. InshaAllah when you study haqaiq you'll know why.  But these are some very prominant traits of this word Rehman. Most of all that is ONLY used for Allah.

Raheem. also one of the most beloved attributes to Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . and he has therefore given it only to those he loves. . And he gave this to no one more . than he gave to our beloved propeth Muhammad Mustafa SAS. BECAUSE ALlah is alRehman. he has sent ⟪ar:النبی الرحمۃ⟫ .

⟪ar-quote:وَمَآ أَرْسَلْنَكَ إِلَّا رَحْمَةًۭ لِّلْعَلَمِينَ⟫

Because Allah is AlRheman . He has chosen for us the best human being and sent for us the best message. and our prophet (Salawaat) said

⟪ar-quote:انا نبی الرحمۃ⟫

I am the prophet of ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫.

So you can see that Allah described himself.  identified himself with ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. He gave us a book which he called ⟪ar:کتاب الرحمۃ⟫. In that book. he imposed upon his own soul ⟪ar:رحمۃ .⟫

⟪ar-quote:كَتَبَ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِ ٱلرَّحْمَةَ⟫

I have written. I have imposed. I have made ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫compulsory upon myself.  And then this loving and caring and merciful master . this RabbAl-Alameen. he gave us a prophet who is Rehmatul lil Alameen.

---

Linguistic meaning of Al-Rehman

Now let's linguistically understand the meanings of these words.  We'll start with AlRehman.  You understand now that both words means love and care.

But Rehman. has 3 characteristics. I want you to remember 3 things about the word AlRehman.

The first is. the love, care, concern and mercy of Allah are EXTREME . they are beyond expectations. thats the first thing. What that means is . that Allah is loving. but not just loving. He is EXTREMELY loving and his love is beyond all expectations. He's not JUST caring. He is EXTREMELY caring.  So whatever you expect from Allah in terms of love care concern and mercy. know that it is beyond your expectation. Thats the first meaning.

The second meaning of AlRehman. is that it is something that is happening IMMEDIATELY. You don't have to wait for it. it is happening right now. Let's think about this for a second. In english. what is the difference between someone who IS patient.  and someone who is BEING patient. ? Which one is showing patience right now? The one who is BEING patient. Like for example if I say about my wife.  that she is patient woman.  But I don't know if she's going crazy right now with the kids or not.  Maybe she's yelling at them. maybe she's throwing them against the wall. I don't know that. She is generally a patient person.  but I don't know if she is patient right this very second. But when I say. she is BEING patient. I'm talking about her when? Right now! You understand the difference? . The love and care of AlRehman is not something that is happening generally. It is happening RIGHT NOW. In other words in AlRehman we acknowledge that we don't have to wait for Allah to show us love. we don't have to wait for him to care for us. we don't have to wait for him to be concerned about us . when we are in the middle of a difficulty. He is doing all of that RIGHT NOW!.  He loves all of us RIGHT NOW. He cares for all of us RIGHT NOW. He is genuinely concerned for all of us RIGHT NOW and he's being merciful to us RIGHT NOW. All of that is happening. in its EXTREME form. Right now! . You understand?

So the first one is extreme. the second one is IMMEDIATE.  Now here's the third part of the meaning. This third part of the meaning is a bit hard to take in.  when you hear it for the first time. It feels wrong. And that third characteristic of the word AlRheman is . that it is temporary. It's not permanent. And I'll explain why it is temporary.

But for now understand that these are the 3 characteristics of the love and care of Allah in AlRehman. It is INTENSE. It is IMMEDIATE. and it is TEMPORARY. And these are actually the characteristic of every other word that follows this phonetic pattern. If you take any other word that rhymes with the word AlRehman in Arabic. Words like ⟪ar:عطشان، جوعان، غضبان⟫ . they all have these same traits in common.

So for example Let's take ⟪ar:غضبان⟫. It means EXTREMELY angry. and extremely angry RIGHT NOW. but that anger is temporary. Someone who is extremely angry.  he is not going to stay angry forever. He cannot. His head will burst and he will die.  Even the hulk chills out eventually. Similary ⟪ar:جوعان⟫. EXTREMELY Hungry. and hungry RIGHT NOW (like you crazy teenagers). but temporary. You eat something and the hunger goes away. ⟪ar:عتشان⟫. EXTREMELY Thirsty. Thirsty right now. but as soon as you have a drink. you're no longer thirsty. so its temporary.

So now when we say AlRehman. what are we saying? . We're saying that Allah's love is extreme. it is beyond expectations.  it is coming right now. but it's not permanent. It can go away. But it doesn't just go away on its own. That's what this pattern suggests. These states . they don't just change on its own. Thirst doesn't just go away on its own, you have to drink something. Hunger doesn't just disappear by itself, you need to eat something. Similarly, Allah's care and love is there.  and it is extreme. But if we do something seriuosly bad. something really horrible. if we do something to mess up royally. that state of ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫can change. It can go away. You understand?

Linguistic meaning of Al-Raheem

Then there is the word AlRaheem. His love and care manifests also through Raheem. And there are two characteristics we need to know about Raheem.  It has two qualities.  The first is . that it is permanent. and the second quality of Raheem is . that it is not necessarily happening right now. It is long-term.  For example if I say. my khala is loving to me. Thats a long term quality. isn't it? . But does that mean she is being loving to me right now? Not necessarily . I know she will always love me. but she may not be showing that love to me right now . but her love for me is always there.

And there are other attributes of Allah that follow the same pattern of AlRaheem. Hakeem, Kareem, Jameel, Aleem. And they too share the same 2 characteristics . Hakeem means wise. which means he is always wise.  Aleem means all knowing . which means he is always all-knowing. Jameel means beautiful, which means he is permanently beautiful. So AlRaheem is a state that is not intense, but it is permanent.

---

Rehman before Raheem

Now the next question is why is AlRehman first. and why is AlRaheem second. Please listen to his very carefully.

If Allah had ONLY said AlRehman.  then his love, care, concern and mercy would have been EXTREME. it would have been immediate. but it wouldn't have been permanent. If Allah only said AlRaheem. The love and mercy of Allah would have been permanent. but it would not have been EXTREME. So how do I talk about the love, care, concern and mercy of Allah.  so that it is extreme. AND it is beyond expectations. ANDit is right now. ANDit is permanent. ANDit is long term. all at the same time.?. The only way to do that is AlRheman AlRaheem. SubhanAllah!  You cannot talk about the qualities of the love and care of Allah . in better terms than AlRehman and AlRaheem.

I'll give you an example to better understand this. You are at work. Today is pay day . Your boss is not there at the office. and you have a flight booked to Timbuktoo for 7:00pm.  so you need to leave the office at exactly 5 o'clock.  or you will not make it to the airport. and its already 4:45 and you still haven't gotten your paycheck. and you desperately need your paycheck. because you need the money for your trip. You were counting on this paycheck for the expenses of your trip. You're getting desperate. Its 4:50 now. and your boss is still isnt there. And your co-worker says. don't worry. our boss is reliable. He'll be here. Relax!!.

Now its 4:55. and you are totally freaking out. And your coworker is still telling you . Don't worry. he's reliable. he'll be here. Now what will you say to him at that point? .

*No don't say that . that's very rude.*

You'll say.  Listen. I know he's reliable.  but I need him to be reliable RIGHT NOW. Right this very minute. I need his quality of reliability. RIGHT NOW! Isn't that the case?

When I'm in trouble. I need Allah's help when? RIGHT NOW! So I need the name of Allah. that gives me the help I need RIGHT NOW! That is AlRheman. And then I want the other name. AlRaheem. which takes care of my future.  Because when Allah says AlRaheem . its permanant right? . which is a guarantee for the future. But when Allah says AlRehman. it is a guarantee for the present. So short-term love and care . and long-term love and care. are both covered by AlRehman AlRaheem

Another example. You teenagers will be able to relate to this. I come home and I'm REALLY REALLY hungry. I dind't have breakfast. there was too much work at the office. didn't get a chance to have lunch. so I come home and I'm starving. So I sit at the dinning table and Nazneen comes and asks me. SO. what do you want me to cook for next week? . I'll be like. WOMAN! Who cares about next week?. Give me something to eat right now!! . When you're extremely hungry. the only thing you can think about is what? Right now. And when my RIGHT NOW is taken care of. Once I've finished eating my dinner tonight. and I go BURP. Aaaah. AlHamdulillah !.  Then I'll be like. So what are we eating next week?.

When you pay this months bill. you start worrying about next months bills. When you've paid this semesters fee. you start worrying about next semesters fees. You understand? So we only think about the futre. when our immediate concerns are taken care of. So Allah says.  I am AlRheman. I'm taking care of your immediate needs right now. But when my immediate concern is taken care of. where does my mind go? into the future. so he says I'm AlRaheem too. Don't worry. I'll take care of you in the future too.

Someone asked Ibn Abbas RA. One of the great companions of the Prophet. about the difference between AlRehman and AlRaheem. He said Allah is Rehman in this life. and he is Raheem in the after life. Because the love and care of Allah will go away for disbelievers on the day of judgment. Until that day he is AlRehman for both. the believers and disbelievers. For all of us. every human being. So he does not just love you and care about you. And he does not just love me and care about me. He loves and cares for every single being that he ever created. plans, animals, humans.  No matter what religion color or race they belong to. Muslim . Non-Mulsim. He actually even loves and cares for those who hate him. who deny his existence . His doors of Rehmaniyat are always open to everyone. hoping they will choose to turn back to him. His invitation never expires. because Rehman is a universal quality.

⟪ar:رحمتی وسعت علی کل شیء⟫. My mercy extends to all.  The rain comes down from the sky.  all human beings drink from it. they all draw their sustenance from it. the good drinks. the wretched drinks. the sinner drinks. the pious drinks. the friend of Allah drinks. the enemy of Allah drinks.  the scolar drinks. the ignorant drinks.  everybody drinks.  this is the universal mercy of this world.

But once judgment day comes. He is no longer Rehman to the disbelievers. Now on this day He is Qahhar.

⟪ar-quote:لِّمَنِ ٱلْمُلْكُ ٱلْيَوْمَۖ لِلَّهِ ٱلْوَحِدِ ٱلْقَهَّارِ⟫

Who does dominion belong on this day?. For Allah the one. the subduer.

On the day of judgment there is no Rehma for the disbelievers. there is ONLY ghadab. there is only wrath. and that wrath is to exact justice. Allah's ghadab. his wrath is not the same emotion that we feel. See . our ghadab is directed towards hurting .  When we go into a rage. all we want to do is to hurt the other person. to offset some of the pain . that they have caused us. In fact we want to hurt them EVEN more if we can. But Allah's ghadab . is not out of a desire to hurt the disbelievers. or cause them pain. It is not personal. It is to exact justice. And we'll talk about this when we get to Malik Yaum AlDeen. But the point is. on that day. his Rehmaniyat will get replaced with ghadab to establish justice against the disbelievers. But until judgment day he is Rehman . to the believers as well as the disbelievers. But then for the believers on judgment day. He is Raheem. Because this word has the trait of permanence . and aakhira is a place of permanence.

So Rehman is general love. and AlRaheem is very specific love. because he specifically decrees it for those who have piety.  this is the love, care and mercy of the afterlife.  which he has decreed only for the believers. The mercy of eternal peace. This is why you find in the Quran in Surah Yaseen.

⟪ar-quote:سلم قولا من رب الرحیم⟫

you don't find

⟪ar-quote:سلم قولا من رب الرحمن⟫

Allah says that in paradise.  Allah will turn to the believers and declare eternal peace for them.  Salaam . This Salaam  will come from a master that is Raheem.

⟪ar-quote:وَكَانَ بِٱلْمُؤْمِنِينَ رَحِيمًۭا⟫

he is Raheem with the momineen. not with the kafireen.

So Ibn Abbas said. Allah is AlRehman in this world and He is AlRaheem in the next world. because this world is temporary and the next world is permanent.

And I can really appreciate the genius of this man. because he saw something. He saw that this world is temporary and which Rehma is temporary? AlRehman.  and he saw that the next life is permanent. and which Rehma is permanent? AlRaheem.  SubhanAllah! The sahaba saw it right away. We need hours to figure this stuff out. it needs to be explained to us. But they just saw it as soon as they heard it.  SubhanAllah!.

Anyway. So that's one interpretation of these two words. Another interpretation is that AlRehman indicates that Allah is loving and caring by nature. and AlRaheem indicates that Allah is loving and caring in his actions.  Rehman means that by his nature Allah is loving and caring. And Raheem means that in his actions Allah is loving and caring.

AlRehman is the one who gives when you ask him.  and AlRaheem is the one who gets upset . when you DON'T ask him.I'll repeat. AlRehman is the one who gives when you ask. Muslim Kafir . believer. disbeliver. doesnt matter. AlRehman will always give. But AlRaheem is the one that if you dont ask.  he will get annoyed. why didn't you ask me?. This is that special kind of closeness that Allah has for the believers. Like us with our best friends right. Your best friend needs something and turns to someone else. You get upset. Why didn't you ask me?. I wanted to be there for you?. right? . So this is a very intimate love. that Allah (Azza Wa Jal) has for his believers.  SubhanAllah!

---

Womb of a mother

So we looked at how AlRehman and AlRaheem they both come from Rehma. which means intense love, care, genuince concern and mercy. Now let's look at where the word Rehama comes from.  OMG. Once you understand this. you will appreciate Allah like nothing else InshaAllah .

The word Rehma. it comes from the word . Reham. The word Reham in Arabic means the womb of a mother when she is carrying a child .  The place where the baby lives inside the mother is called Reham in Arabic.

A mother's womb is what describes the relationship between Allah and his creation. This is what makes it SO beautiful. See both parents love their child. but in the Quran when Allah compares his love for his creation. he never uses the example of a father. he ALWAYS uses the example of a mother. So to truly understand the meaning of the word Rehma. to understand the kind of relationship Allah has with us. we first have to understand the relationship of a mother with her child.  when she is carrying it in her womb.

There is this famous hadees . in which Allah is speaking directly to the womb. and here the womb means the archetypal womb . because the womb of the mother is how humanity was spread. All of us came as a result of the womb of our mothers. And Allah spoke to this creation. the womb . and he said

⟪ar-quote:اِنِّی سَمَّیتُکَ بِاسْمی⟫

I named you from my names. I am AlRehman and AlRaheem. and I am naming you REHAM. I am making you a symbol of my Rehma. my unconditional love. because EVERY human being will come THROUGH you. and you will remind them of MY love for them. This is what Allah says to the womb.

Now what is it about the womb of the mother that is important for us to understand. Well. there are a few things. First of all. when the child is inside the womb of its mother. is it being punihsed?.  Is there ANY association with the concept of punishment for the baby when its inside the womb of its mother?.  No! . What's the relationship of the mother with the baby?.  Its pure love. right?. So that's the very first relationship of Allah with His creation. it is based on pure love . and has nothing to do with punishment. The moment a woman finds out she's pregnant. she falls in love with the baby. She hasnt even seen the baby yet.  Hasn't even met it. and yet she falls completely and unconditionally in love with her baby.

Now did the womb exist even before the mother conceived?. Or does the body just create the womb when she gets pregnant and then discards it later?. It exists with the mother. Baby or no baby. the womb is always there. Similarly . Allah's ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫is always there. His ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫does not exist because of us. His ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫is ALWAYS there.

Now . when the child is inside the womb of its mother.  does the child even know that it is being taken care of?.  Does it even know that the mother exists? . It doesn't. It is being taken care of in ways . that it cannot even realize.  Allah is taking care of us.  in ways that we cannot possibly even realize. He is taking care of us in such a subtle manner . that forget his ⟪ar:رحمۃ⟫. even his presence is not visible to us. He is taking care of us in such a subtle manner. That's why one of his name is Lateef. Lateef means something EXTREMELY subtle. It's there and its working for you. but you don't even feel it's presence. That's Lateef. But what's amazing . is in the Quran everytime the attribute Lateef is mentioned. which other attribute do you hear with it? . Khabeer. The All knowing.

⟪ar-quote:لَّا تُدْرِكُهُ ٱلْأَبْصَرُ وَهُوَ يُدْرِكُ ٱلْأَبْصَرَ ۖ وَهُوَ ٱللَّطِيفُ ٱلْخَبِيرُ⟫

YOUR eyes cannot see him. but HE is aware of what your eyes are seeing. He is EXTREMELY subtle. but ALL KNOWING at the same time.  SubhanAllah! . So the child doesn't even know that the mother is taking care of it

The next thing that comes to mind. when you think of the womb.  is protection. The mother is constantly protecting the baby.  She watches the corners of the table when she walks. she tries to stay safe. she sleeps on her side. she watches what she eats.  she's constantly caressing the baby. She LOVES the baby. She CARES for the baby. And she is EXTREMELY PROTECTIVE of it. That is what Allah is doing for us. CONSTANTLY. You don't just make it to school like that. Can you even imagine how many things can go wrong . in just the time you leave the house and enter your school?. Millions of things can go wrong. but Allah is protecting you. keeping you safe. I have to walk 20 minutes to my bus stop every morning . and back home every evening. I have to cross a highway. and streets and parking lots. I could be hit by a car any time. Takes only one second. And on top of that I have my headphones on. I'm not even being SUPER careful. But I am making it to work everyday. and making it back home everyday. without incident. SubhanAllah! That's Allah constantly protecting me.

Then. this mother puts up with a LOT of difficulties for her baby. She deals with constant morning sickness. Some have to take these horribly painful tests. They have to take extremely nauseating medicines for the health and growth of the baby. constant blood tests. one painful thing after another. A mother goes through SO MUCH pain for  the sake of her child. which again.  the child is COMPLETELY unaware of. The child takes the mother completely for granted.

And this child is technically doing NOTHING for the mother. And the mother is doing EVERYTHING for the child.  The baby eats her food. right? . The poor woman eats.  but the damn baby takes everything.  and she's like. seriously?? Stop it!!.  She just ate this huge meal and minutes later she's hungry again.  And then the poor husband has to run in the middle of the night to the store for ice cream. So the baby is taking everything from her. and its not giving ANYTHING back to its mother. In fact . when the baby does thank her. how does it thank the mother? . By kicking her from inside. right?.  It just decides to stretch from time to time. does the insanity workout whenever it feels like it.  bench presses with her ribs. right?. The mother is in a CONSTANT state of discomfort because of this baby. Yes or no?

We are doing NOTHING for Allah. But Allah is still doing EVERYTHING for us. We do nothing for Allah! . We CAN do nothing for Allah EVEN if we wanted. We cannot add to his kingdom. We cannot take away anything from his kingdom. Our good deeds do not add to his kingdom. Our sins do not reduce anything from his kingdom. We cannot make him any wealthier than he is. We cannot make him any poorer than he is. We cannot praise him any more than he is already praised. We cannot add anything to him. .  We cannot do ANYTHING for him. There is ABSOLUTELY NOTHING that we can offer Allah. And yet, he is constantly doing things for us. Without even us realizing his presence. In many cases even without acknowledging his presence.

⟪ar-quote:كُلَّ يَوْمٍ هُوَ فِى شَأْنٍۢ⟫

Every moment He is busy in work. to keep this universe and EVERYTHING within this universe functional . SubhanAllah.

Then we see that all of the needs of the child.  are being met by its mother. The child is completely surrounded. It is completely enveloped by the care of its mother. His food, his drinks even when the child excretes. All of that is taken care by the body of the mother. Everything the child needs.  is completely provided for. The rent is paid. Housing and lodging is free. It does not have to pay for any of the utilities. All meals are included. In other words, the baby is completely wrapped up in the love and care of its mother .

Similarly WE are completely wrapped up in the unconditional love of Allah. He provides us with our sustenance. He gives us the luxuries of a good life. He's making the OUTSIDE world functional for us. He's keeping the world INSIDE of us functional. My heart is beating. my organs are working. my breadth is coming in and out. I can walk. I can speak. He's making ALL this happen for me. He gave me parents. He gave me teachers. He gave me knowledge. He gave me my own family. He surrounded me with all the comforts of my life.

You know we complain about paying the bills. about mortgage. utilities. Just think for a second. How much do we pay for our sight?. How much do we pay Allah for our ability to hear. our ability to speak. Our ability to breadth. forget everything else. how much are we paying for each breadth?. How much would you pay for your breadth?. If you couldn't breadthe and Allah asked you to pay for the next breadth? . What amount would you be willing to pay Him for the next breadth?. How much would you pay for your hands?. What would they be worth to you?. We are going through life. IMMENSELY blessed with his bounties. IMMENSELY blessed with the riches he created us with. ALL of which we take COMPLETELY for granted. AllahuAkbar.

Now let's talk about the motivation for this mother? . The baby is not paying  the mother. The baby is not giving anything back to the mother. So then what is the motivation of this mother to carry on?. Despite ALL the discomfort this child is putting her through. what is motivating this mother to carry on?. The only motivation the mother has for the baby is an extreme form of unconditional love. Just think about this. As the child grows in the womb of its mother. it becomes more and more a problem for the mother. from a physical standpoint. Yet, as it becomes more and more of a problem for her . she falls  more and more in love with her baby. She is CONSTANTLY increasing in her love. This is incredible! . And then when the baby comes out.  it almost kills her. If 9 months of torture wasn't enough. this baby causes this incredibly intense pain of child birth. I've been in the delivery room twice. and I feel I've been traumatized for life. Nazneen was in labor for 8 hours at the time of Erum. I've NEVER seen anyone go through so much pain. And yet when she's finally out. She tries to hand Erum to me. and she's covered up in all that GUI stuff . and I'm like EWOOO. But then she brings Erum to Nazneen. and she SO lovingly touches her cheeks and says. Hi baby. and then passes out.  That was such an insane moment in my life. I still don't get it. I probably never will . I would have thought she'd hate this baby who caused her SO much pain. she'd yell at her. scream at her. curse her out. You almost killed me! I hate you! . No! that not what happened!. And then the first time they brought Erum to her. she gives her a big hug. Kisses her . She starts crying because she is SO happy to see her. And then she starts feeding her. SubhanAllah!

Anybody else who causes SO much pain to you. that makes you bleed this way . you would NOT give them a hug!.  We make our mothers bleed.  almost to death. and as soon as we come out. she has MORE love for us now . than she did ever before.  and this is right after we tried to kill her. 

This is a completely illogical relationship. This is not a relationship you can make any sense of. It is beyond all logic. This does not happen with any other relationship. There is NO other relationship that works this way. Where you never give. you NEVER EVER give.  you ONLY take. and still . all she does is keep giving you her love.  You keep taking more. she keeps giving more.

And BTW. your mother bled so much to give you life. She just went through childbirth. or surgery.  and what happens right after you're born? . She now has to feed you!. And I've heard feeding for a lot of woman can be extremely painful too . Anybody else in this world who goes through surgery  or such intense pain. says.  I need 6 weeks off. I need 2 months off. I need a break. I need a vacation. Does a mother get a 2 month vacation after she gives birth? . NO! . You break a leg. you get 6 months off.  She just gave birth. and now she's on the clock. working full time . the second the baby is born. And what does the baby give her back  in return? . She gives it milk. she gives it love. she gives it care. she gives it protection. she bathes it. oils it. changes diapers. all through countless sleepless nights. months after months. year after year.  And what does the baby do in return?.  Does it say thank you? . Does it show gratitude?.  Does it praise the mother? NO! . But does the mother still keep loving and caring for the baby over and over and over again? She does! . She gets nothing from the baby. The most the baby does. is reward her by urinating on her. pooping on her.  throwing up on her. and even when the baby does that. she says. Aww so cute. and then she cleans it up. Oh it's OK my little baby. Isn't this INCREDIBLY BEAUTIFUL. But isn't this an EXTREMELY insane relationship at the same time?

But this is what Allah is doing for us. This is what Allah is doing for us . on a MUCH GREATER scale.  and that also doesn't make sense?.  Allah's love for us . just doesn't make sense. It is beyond all logical reasoning. We cannot limit Allah's love to common sense. Because we don't deserve this kind of love from Allah. That is what common sense dictates. If we compare our actions.  If we look at our ingratitude towards Allah. We don't even remember him 5 times a day . 2 hours. That's all it takes. We can't even do that much . just to say thank you. After EVERYTHING he does for us. We CONSTANTLY disobey him. We do EVERYTHING he tells us NOT to do . Some don't even acknowledge his existence. Who knows if there is an Allah or not. And who cares if there is. After EVERYTHING he does for us. We do not even have the decency to say Thank you! . just by praying 5 times to him. Even just the Farz. 30 minutes a day if you JUST do farz. We don't even give him that much. And yet. he keeps giving us. keeps giving us. Despite my constant ingratitude. my constant disloyalty. my constant defiance to his every command. I am still waking up. I am still breadthing. I am still going about my day. eating . drinking . enjoying. partying. And he does not take that away from me. This doesn't make sense. It JUST doesn't make sense.

Just look at what we do with food. How much food do we waste?. His greatest blessings for his mankind. the means of sustenance. Look how we disrespect food?. Look at the ettiquettes of eating. The prophet (Salawaat) said. sit before the food like a slave sits before his master. Cover your head before you eat.  to show it respect. Do not place it on the floor. elevate the table from the ground to honor it. When you're done. fine and eat the crumbs that are left behind. THAT'S how much esteem food should hold in our lives. Do we ever think of the amount of effort it took . behind the scenes . to get that food on our plate? . Do we think about the time. the effort. the protection. the management. the design. that went into taking that seed and growing it into a plant. from taking that animal. growing it till it reached the proper age. feeding it all that time.  getting it into the hands of the one who does zabeeha. who makes it halal for us. then to get it to the supermarket and the meat shop. so that YOU end up buying it. giving you the tools to cook it . until it finally makes it to you plate. That's years and years of Allah's labor that sits before us in our plate. Do we care?. NO. We take a few bites and we toss it away. Just because it's not warm enough. not fresh enough. not enough salt.

You work on a school project for months and months. only for it to get thrown out in the end. And then you tell me how that feels to you. You tell me what your response will be the next time you're asked to develop a project.

We constantly disrespect and disregard Allah's efforts. And YET he constantly keeps giving us food. one better than the next. Just like the mother keeps feeding her baby regardless of what it does. Does the baby care about the months of intense effort that went.  into growing it from a drop to a child. and then from a child to an adult. NO. But does the mother stop loving the child?. NO!. THIS is insane love. There is ABSOLUTELY NO reason for Allah to love us in this way. But he does!. He does. Why? Because he has Rehma for us. Because his relationship with us. as his creation. is that of Rehma.

⟪ar-quote:اِنِّی سَمَّیتُکَ بِاسْمی⟫

Oh Womb. I have named you from my names. I have named you REHAM. because I am AlRehman and AlRaheem. I have made you a symbol of my love. so that EVERY human being recognizes my unconditional love for them . THROUGH you. and BECAUSE of you. And this is why Allah is AlRehman and AlRaheem. SubhanAllah. We can never understand the love and care of Allah. but to get some understanding of this relationship. he gave us mother. If you want to taste one drop of that endless ocean of love . you think of who? . Your mother

---

Rehma is his universal attribute. Over  gods wrath is his rehma.  over his ghadab he has rehma.

إن الله لما قضى الخلق كتب فوق عرشه ….  رحمتي سبقت غضبي

The rehma of Allah is over his anger. an anger of God is about justice. which we will look at when we study Malik Yaum Aldeen.

the essence of human Rehma  is from the womb. Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)  told the womb.  and this is the archetypal womb from which all the wombs of women come from. Allah told this Reham.

إِنَّآ أَنزَلْنَهُ قُرْءَنًا عَرَبِيًّۭا لَّعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ

Arabic has a unique capacity in igniting the intellect by its nature because of these different elements of the Arabic language that are not found particularly in the European languages like English.  the Coran demands that you think it does not let you off easily.  the Quran makes you think by its nature in Arabic.  you cannot understand it without due contemplation.

so Allah has made reham the source of rehma. ٓallah says.

وَٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ ٱلَّذِى تَسَآءَلُونَ بِهِۦ وَٱلْأَرْحَامَ ۚ

## And fear Allah , through whom you ask one another, and the wombs

this is the few times when God says be conscious of God and something else.  God mentions this only two times in the book as far as I know.

we have to have a conscious awareness of God.  and the conscious awareness of the arhaam.  if the humanity is not nurtured in the house amongst our relatives.  then there is no way it is going to exist outside.  if we not treating  our own blood properly.  we will never be able to treat anyone else properly.  this is one of the worst things in Islam to cut off ties with relatives. Why?.  because if you cannot  learn to live with these people that you have a blood bond with.  how can you live with the rest of the people who do not have this bond  with you.  if we are not humanized in the house then how is the society function.  where will rehma  come from if it's not from our own flesh and blood.  how can I extend out of the rest of the society.

کان بالمومنین رحیما.  he is Raheem with the momineen. not with the kafireen. So Rehman is for everybody. Raheem only for the believers. Rehman for this world. Raheem for the after life.

<!-- section 9 (id=5747, raw_sort=9): Akhlaaq - Silatur Reham -->
We are studing the Basmallah. We've looked at the word Allah and his attributes in quite a bit of depth. We've talked about the heart as the center of all consciousness that Allah gave us to witness his attributes within his creation. And in the last session we talked about Rehman and Raheem. We looked at how it came from the word Rehma. which in turn comes from the Reham which is the womb of a mohter. Now assuming you guys were awake during those sessions. today I want to talk about Akhlaaq. or character. But Akhlaaq is such a VAST topic. that it would take a LOT of sessions to cover all aspects of it. So what I thought is. today I'll just try to explain what akhlaaq means. and the science behind akhlaaq. and then we can cover the rest in later sessions as stuff comes up InshaAllah.

### Seen vs Unseen - body vs soul

Today when we look at any functional entity. we find it has two parts. There is the SEEN. which is the body or the exterior.  and then there is the UNSEEN. which is the energy that is moving or animating that body. And this principle holds true for everything that "WORKS". From a battery operated toy car.  to massive construction machines.  like tractors and cranes. And this is something we've come to recognize almost instinctively in today's day and age. There is the object. and then there is the energy or force controlling the object. Your phone doesn't turn on. the first thing you check is if it's charged or not. right? . If the battery of your phone goes dead. no matter how expensive it may be.  it becomes completely useless. 

Your phone might have some really awesome hardware. Let's say it has a 20 mega pixel camera. a microphone. a million pixel resolution. TONS of memory. TONS of harddrive space. So the phone hardware is awesome. and that's all great!!. But without the software. without the APPS . that are controlling the hardware. that are actually putting the hardware of your phone TO its proper use. your phone would be useless to you. You would not be able to draw any benefit from it. right? . And how would you know if my phone has an app installed on it?. by the functions of the hardware. Things are happening on the screen. the camera is working. the microphone is capturing and transmitting my voice. right? . So the functions of the hardware prove the existence of the app that is controlling it.

And between the hardward and the software. between the object and the energy utilizing and animating that object. between the SEEN. and the UNSEEN. it is ALWAYS the UNSEEN. that holds REAL value. Both are important. Both the hardware and software are important. but BETWEEN the two. it is the software . and not the hardware that takes the prize. Because the software is the master and the hardware is its slave. It's existence is simply to serve at the commands of the apps utilizing it.

Now Allah too created us human beings with a hardware and a software. We have a body which is the hardware. and we have a soul controlling the body. which is the software. And following the same logic of the phone. how do I know I have a soul?. By the movement of my body. As the Arabs would say. ⟪ar:حرکۃ الجسم.  دلیلُ المُحَرِّک⟫. The movement of the body proves the existence of the one moving it. So Allah created us with these two . completely distinct . completely different entities. Just as the hardware and software are two completely different entities.

The way in which the body develops. is completely different from the way in which the soul develops. The both even come from different places. The body is created from the earth.
⟪ar-quote:وَٱللَّهُ أَنۢبَتَكُم مِّنَ ٱلْأَرْضِ نَبَاتًۭا⟫

We raised you from this earth. like a plant. because just like the plant. the body grows over a period of time. and through stages . from a child. to a toddler. to a teenager. to a mature adult. 

But the soul does not come from the earth. It is a subtle essence that was created by the command of Allah. 
⟪ar-quote:وَيَسْـَٔلُونَكَ عَنِ ٱلرُّوحِ.  قُلِ ٱلرُّوحُ مِنْ أَمْرِ رَبِّى⟫

 they ask you about the soul.  tell them it is  from the command of their master.

So the source of the body is the earth.  and the source of the soul is the heavens.  and then in the 4th month of pregnancy. Allah combines the two. and human life begins. As the child grows and matures. he starts working towards achieving certain goals. He becomes a doctor, or an engineer or a scientist . or a CEO or even the president of a country. These are all accomplishments and achievements of the soul.  WHILE it is connected with the body.

But then a day comes. when Allah  disconnect the two.  And as soon as that happens. all worldly titles. all accomplishments. all achievements.  all relationships. everything comes to an end. and the ONLY title that remains.  is that of a "Mayyat". a dead body. a corpse. When I die. and its time for you to take me to my grave. you're not going to say. Let's take Asif Mamu to his grave. Even my own children won't say. let's pickup babu. You know what you and everyone else will say?. Let's take the body. I've been to so many mayyats in Karachi. and I never once heard anyone every say . چلا بابا کو اٹھاؤ. I've always heard them say. چلو میت اٹھاؤ. Let's take the body.

When King Faisal of Saudi Arabia died. I don't know if you know this. but in Saudia. after every Zohr Asar prayer. they hold the prayer for the deceased . It's called صلواۃ المیت. When Shah Faisal was alive.  and he would go visit a place. it would take 15 minutes to announce his arrival. They would go on and on with his titles. Pride of Arabia. Glory of the desert. The Wise . The generous. and they would go on and on . Like Apolo creed in Rocky 4. If you haven't seen Rocky 4 then please pray 2 rakaats of Astaghfaar after this session.

But anyway. So they would go on an on with his titles. for 10 minutes. But when he died and his body was brought into the masjid. for prayer. everyone in the masjid was thinking. that maybe today too they will announce him by all his titles. But everyone was left in a state of complete shock. when the Imam said. ھذا صلواۃ المیت. That's it!. The pride of Arabia. glory of the desert. and god knows what else. all of that reduced to one single word. Mayyat.

For the wise. this is the true nature of this world. Why are you calling him that?. What has changed about him? . Just yesterday you were calling this man by a thousand titles. What happened today? What changed?.  He still has the same body. the same face . the same eyes. the same organs. He's still the same person as he was yesterday. How come suddenly he's lost all his value?. He's lost all his value. because something valuable. something essential. no longer exists within this body. which is the soul.

All titles . all degrees. accomplishments. that's all what the soul earns. NOT the body. The body was merely a facilitator. a subservient slave. that was working FOR the soul. And as we know. once a master disowns his slave. the slave holds ABSOLUTELY NO VALUE in the market. No one will buy that slave again because his master disowned him.  Similarly once the soul departs from the body. the body is reduced to nothing more than an empty useless vessel. Even if it's still in excellent shape. Beautiful eyes. sharp features. perfectly good organs. yet all of that becomes completely useless without the soul.

So this is the true nature of existence. These two friends come together. one from the earth. the other from the heavens. They work together to accomplish a certain goal while they're together. and whether they succeed or not. at the appointed time they both depart.  and each goes back to its origin. ⟪ar:کل شئی یرجع الی اصلہ⟫. Everything return back to its origin. The body goes back into the earth where it came from. and the soul returns back to the heavens where it came from. right? So that's the process.

---

### Sould has needs like the body

But what I want to talk to you today. is about the that short duration of time when these two friends ARE together. The first thing is.  that they both have needs. And they both draw their needs . from their original source…. This body is created from this earth…. and so all its needs come from the earth as well…. Its needs are food…. air…. clothing…. housing…. precious metals like gold silver . i.e. money…. All of which are produce of this earth…. When the needs of the body are not fulfilled…. it becomes sick…. it becomes weak…. But when all its needs are properly met…. in a balanced way. the body becomes strong…. it becomes healthy…. vibrant…. attractive….

Just like the body…. the soul too has needs…. And those needs come from ITS original source. which is the heavens. or the spiritual world…. And that is revelation.

So the body and the soul are two separate entities that have completely separate needs. And it can't benefit from the nourishment of the other. These earthly things cannot fulfill the needs of the soul.  because it was not created from the earth…. It can be distracted for a while with these pleasures…. Sure!. In fact it happens all the time. But these pleasures cannot sustain its interest permanently…. The soul will eventually lose interest. it'll gets bored…. it'll  gets tired of whatever THING. or relationship it is attached to…. And we see this all the time. When a new game comes out. we're ALL OVER IT. Once we've played it for a while. you need the next game. When your phone first came out. it was the MOST INCREDIBLE thing. You spent half the day spit shining it to perfection. Hey do you like your phone?. OH I LOOOVVVVEEEE ITT. It's SO FREAKING AWESOME. 6 months later when the next version comes out. Hey! you like your phone. Ehhhh . It's OK. It's not the 6s. it's not the S6 edge.  but its OK. What happened? . Just 6 months back it was the MOST incredible thing. What happened today?. But this is the nature of this world. and EVERYTHING that comes from it. Interest rises. reaches its peak . and then its descend begins. And now you need the next new thing. Look at anything in your life. This holds true for everything of this world. It's temporary. it's a phase. it passes. and this is because these pleasures have to do with the body . which is also temporary. which comes from this earth . which is also temporary. and so ANY and ALL attachment the soul forms. with anything or anyone in the worldly sense. it will always be temporary.

But the soul is different. it is eternal. and that's why it needs an attachment that is eternal. And that attachment is Allah. because Allah is eternal. And just like the body . the soul too needs nourishment to grow and develop. and that nourishment is revelation…. Revelation is the nourishment of the soul. Just like food is the nourishment of the body. The body grows in STRENGTH with physical nourishment. the soul grows in CHARACTER. with spiritual nourishment. It's grows in what's called AKHLAAQ.  The perfection of the body is measured by its  STRENGTH. and the perfection of the soul is measured by its Akhlaaq. It's character.

Now what is Akhlaaq. The word Akhlaaq comes from the word Khulq. And this is really interesting. Because we are called Khalq. Khalq means creation. which is related to the body. and Khulq means character which is related to the soul. They're both made up of the same letters. IN the same sequence. And I've shown you how there is this science in Arabic.  that when two words share the same letters in the same sequence…. they are identical in meaning…. And when they share the same letters in a different sequence…. they are connected in meaning…. For example…. we looked at the words Ilm and Amal…. knowledge and action….  They both have the same letters but in a different sequence …. And that's why they are CONNECTED in meaning…. because knowledge produces action…. Or action is based on knowledge…. And then we saw Qalb and Qabl …. Heart and precedence and qibla…. direction…. and they're all connected in meaning because they share the same letters in a different sequence…. But when the letters and the sequence are the same…. They both represent identical things…. For example…. There is Ilm which means knowledge…. and then there is ⟪ar:عَلَم⟫…. which means flag…. And what a flag does. is it identifies and honors a country…. And what knowledge does. is it identifies and honors a scholar…. So they're both IDENTICAL in meaning. because they both share the same letters in the same sequence…. This is why Arabic is SO beautiful. because it is EXTREMELY precise. and it's PERFECT in its form and construction.  SubhanAllah!

And so now we haev Khalq…. and we have Khulq…. because Khalq is the body…. nourished by this physical world . And khulq …. is character which is a nourishment from the spiritual world. Khalq represents the existence of the body. and Khulq represents the existence of the soul. And they both start with Kha…. which I explained to you . is a sound of friction…. It is a sound of effort…. Because the body takes effort to develop…. And so does character…. Character takes a lot of effort to develop…. So if Khalq is the essence of the body…. then Khulq…. or character . is the essence of the soul…. When we die. the fully developed body. or as much as it has developed. it returns back into the earth. and the soul with its fully developed character. or of howmuch it has developed. it returns back to its master. What the soul returns back with. is what it has acquired. and developed in terms of its nature. That's the true earning. the real acquisition of the soul. A soul that returns back to its master without a developed Khulq. is an impoverished soul. When the body is week. it cannot benefit from the offerings of this world. This world has a LOT to offer in terms of temporal pleasures. but if you're so weak you can't even get up off the bed. you're not going to be able to enjoy those pleasures. Similarly a soul. that is devoid. that is bankrupt of Akhlaaq. will not be able to benefit from the pleasures of the after life.

---

And that's why it is EXTREMELY important that we develop our character. or we will be in the midst of all these heavently pleasures. and we will not be able to draw any benefit from it. So now what is character and how do we develop it?. Character is developed with revelation. See revelation. the Quran. in a sense. is nothing more than the explanation of divine attributes of Allah. If I over-simplify. that's all the Quran is doing. it is stating the attributes of Allah. and explaining why he has those attributes. He is Azeem. because he created this massive universe. He is Qawee. All powerful. because not only did he create this universe . he created it with one single command. KUN. Be and FAYAKOON. it was. So in essence Quran is just the description of Allah's attributes . explaining why he is THE ILAH. What he is Allah. And then as ALLAH. as our master what are his rights over us. The favors he has done for us. the favors he has given us right now. the favors he has in store for us later. What'll happen if we obey him. what'll happen if we disobey him. All of that relates back to his divine attributes. right?. So that's all revelation is.

So here's the sequence of events. Allah created this universe. and placed his divine attributes within all of his creation. He created us with a body and a soul. and he gave us a heart. Because it is the heart . that can witnesses these divine attributes of Allah through his revelation. It is the heart that sees the UNSEEN working behind the SEEN. and reaches the conclusion that I must have a master. and testifies لا الہ الا اللہ. There is no god except Allah. It is the heart that does all this. So the universe reflecting the attributes of Allah outside of us. A heart inside of us. that can witness the divine attributes in the light of revelation. which then creates BELIEF. The more the heart understands the revelation. the stronger the belief gets. and the strong the belief gets. the more the soul grows in character. And so character is nothing more.  than absorbing these divine attributes into the heart through revelation. and then reflecting those same divine attributes into the rest of Allah's creation. That's all character is…. It is internalizing…. developing and training the heart . in the light of these divine attributes. and then reflecting them in our interactions with Allah's creation. That is Akhlaaq. And that is Islam.

That's what Islam is. In its simplest form Islam is all about Interactions. It is ⟪ar:معاملات⟫. There are 3 types of interactions in Islam. interaction with Allah. interaction with the self. and interaction with the creation of Allah. Because Allah as our master has certain rights. Our soul has certain rights. and the people around us have certain rights. Huqooq Allah. Huqooq AlNafs. and Huqooq AlIbaad. Those are the 3 right. One towards Allah. which is huqooq Allah. and two towards his creation. Huqooq AlNafs and Huqooq AlIbaad. And even though these two are categorized separately. They're all ACTUALLY a part of the rights of Allah…. Because the self and others are all Allah's creation…. So fulfiling the rights of self and fulfilling the rights of others…. is in fact part of fulfilling the rights of Allah….

Now let's look at these individually.

Huqooq Allah

The first is Huqooq Allah…. The right of Allah…. How do we get to that?. By observing the divine attributes of Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) in his creation all around us. Because everything he created is a symbol of his love. And the purpose of a symbol is to point to that which is symbolizes. And he made the relationship of our body and soul as the perfect example for it. Because the SEEN points to the UNSEEN. The movement of my body points to the existence of an energy that is moving it. And also the master/slave relationship that exists between the soul and the body. That symbolizes the kind of relationship I'm supposed to have with my master. I should be in obedience to MY master. just like my body is in obedience to my soul. So all of this is recognizing the UNSEEN by means of the SEEN. And then being grateful for both. Because if I can't be grateful to the seen. how am I ever going to be grateful for the unseen? . Therefore I have to recognize the force working BEHIND the blessings in my life. through the symbols created for me in the SEEN world. you understand?. And ONLY when I do that. when I recognize the divine attributes of Allah mainifesting in all of his creation. within myself and within those around me. I can then recognize and accept Allah as my master.

For example I see the sun and the moon. Two magnificent creations of Allah. who are controlling the day and night. to benefit me. If there was no day. I would not be able to survive. If there was no night. I would not be able to survive. And so these are both a blessing for me. And who's giving me those blessings?. In the seen sense? It's the sun and the moon. But then these two heavenly bodies are not autonomous.  they're not self-governing. Sun doesn't just come out when it pleases. The moon isn't just full whenever it feels like.
⟪ar-quote:لَا ٱلشَّمْسُ يَنۢبَغِى لَهَآ أَن تُدْرِكَ ٱلْقَمَرَ وَلَا ٱلَّيْلُ سَابِقُ ٱلنَّهَارِ ۚ وَكُلٌّۭ فِى فَلَكٍۢ يَسْبَحُونَ⟫

It is not permissible for the sun to reach the moon. and the night cannot overtake the day. They're both floating in their own orbits. These are both gigantic bodies. The earth is nothing compared to them. And yet I see that have been made subservient. Despite how massive and gigantic these planets are. they are not doing whatever they want to do. I see they have been bound by forces of gravity. They have been assigned certain responsibilities and they're fulfilling it. without question. without arguments. without resistence.Who bound them?
⟪ar-quote:لَمْ تَرَ أَنَّ ٱللَّهَ يُولِجُ ٱلَّيْلَ فِى ٱلنَّهَارِ وَيُولِجُ ٱلنَّهَارَ فِى ٱلَّيْلِ.  وَسَخَّرَ ٱلشَّمْسَ وَٱلْقَمَرَ . كُلٌّۭ يَجْرِىٓ إِلَىٰٓ أَجَلٍۢ مُّسَمًّۭى⟫

Do you not see that Allah causes the night to enter the day and causes the day to enter the night.  and he has subjected the sun and the moon.  each running [its course] for a specified term
⟪ar-quote:فَالِقُ ٱلْإِصْبَاحِ وَجَعَلَ ٱلَّيْلَ سَكَنًۭا.  وَٱلشَّمْسَ وَٱلْقَمَرَ حُسْبَانًۭا⟫

He is the separator of daybreak and He has made the night for rest.  and Allah created the sun and moon for calculation.

So when I witness these gigantic. these extremely powerful heavenly bodies in complete submission and slavery to the forces that Allah has bound them with. it makes me think. How poweful must Allah be. How Jaleel. How Azeem. How Qawee. Allah must be. And then I see that these powerful gigantic plantes are constantly engaged in Allah's worship and obedience. And that makes me think. What am I in strength and might compared to them. They are Allah's creation and I'm Allah's creation. And if THEY are in a state of submission to their powerful master. despite their majesty and glory and enormity. then should I not be in a state of worship and obedience to that same powerful master?. This realization forces me to submit to Allah in worship and obedience. And that's where the rights of Allah come into play. Huqooq Allah. That's where all forms of worship come in. wilyah. taharah. salaah. zakaat. saum. hajj and Jehad. these are all Huqool Allah. The right of my powerful. yet EXTREMELY Rehman Raheem Kareem master over me.

Huqooq Nafs

Then the next thing is Huqooq AnNafs…. I mean this is something even the non-believers have come to see. all these talks about human rights. But this is what Quran teaches us. That my soul has a right. my body has a right. that they be properly nourished …. Nourishment of the body is food…. which comes from the harvest of this earth…. And nourishment of the soul is Akhlaaq…. that come from the harvest of the divine attributes…. So the next thing is. that I recognize and understand the divine attributes of Allah.  and train my heart in the light of these attributes to develop my character. He is Kareem…. He is generous. So I need to be generous with my self. And the greatest generosity that I can do with my self . is to protect it from sins…. And to put it to work in good deeds. I make it do what it was created to do. and that is to work for the pleasure of my master.

Allah is AlHaqq…. He is the truthful…. So I must now train my self. in becoming truthful…. Truthful with who?.  Truthful with myself. I need to stop deluding myself with the attractions of this temporal world. I need to wake up to the reality . that I am only here for a short period of time. Everything that I'm working for in the worldly sense will be left behind. I will be left with nothing other than the title of a Mayyat in this world when I die. My loved ones . the people that I am slaving for day and night. they'll be the first to put me in a grave and throw dirt in my face. So I better not sacrifice my afterlife for this temporary life. That's being truthful to the self. But that means waking up to harsh realities. That means to be ready to be unplugged from the matrix. (again if you haven't see the matrix you know what to do after the session) .

But this is not easy. Waking up from deep sleep is never easy. What I tell you in these sessions. if is difficult for us to hear. makes us uncomfortable. then it's actually working. Because we don't like it when someone tries to wake us up from a deep sleep. When someone tries to take you away from that sweet dream you were having ou don't like that. But that's all this duniya is in the end. A dream. A life filled with illusions and delusions. I mean I find these sessions really disturbing at times. Because I myself am an audience of my sessions. But that's OK.

you know. we're in deep sleep. dreaming about this delicious meal that we're eating. in our dream. And the prophet is waking us up. telling us. Look ALlah has prepared this delicious 7 course gourmet meal for you. It's all ready and laid out on the table. Wake up and enjoy it. And we're like. no no no . leave me alone. I'm too busy enjoying my meal in my dream. right?. but the meal in the dream is not real. That's training the self in the Haqq. the harsh realities. This is all part of the rights of the self. and rights of the body. Because this body doesn't belong to us. and we will be held accountable for it.
⟪ar-quote:ٱلْيَوْمَ نَخْتِمُ عَلَىٰٓ أَفْوَهِهِمْ وَتُكَلِّمُنَآ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَتَشْهَدُ أَرْجُلُهُم بِمَا كَانُوا۟ يَكْسِبُونَ⟫

On that Day, We will seal their mouths, and their hands will speak to Us, and their feet will testify about what they have earned.

We really need to wake up to the harsh reality of Huqooq AlNafs. The rights of our soul. because our souls are dead. our hearts are dead.
⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ ٱسْتَجِيبُوا۟ لِلَّهِ وَلِلرَّسُولِ إِذَا دَعَاكُمْ لِمَا يُحْيِيكُمْ.⟫

Oh believers. respond to Allah and to the Messenger when he calls you to that which gives you life.
⟪ar-quote:وَٱعْلَمُوٓا۟ أَنَّ ٱللَّهَ يَحُولُ بَيْنَ ٱلْمَرْءِ وَقَلْبِهِۦ وَأَنَّهُۥٓ إِلَيْهِ تُحْشَرُونَ⟫

And know that Allah intervenes between a man and his heart and that to Him you will be gathered.

When will we answer his call? When will we respond to the call of Allah and His Messenger.  Something that will bring us back to life. Because that's the implication in the ayah.  as long as we do not respond to Allah and His Messenger. we are dead people.  our hearts are dead.  our lives are dead.and our society is a society of death. We have today become a society that celebrates the death of the spirit.  in giving life to the lowest pursuits of humanity.  This is the death of the soul.  because the soul can only be brought back to life by recognizing why it was created.  what purpose it was created for.  and then setting out and striving to achieve that goal. recognizing that we WILL have shortcomings. That we WILL make mistakes.  that those mistakes are part of our humanity.  this is why we were created. We were created to respond to our Uboodiyah. to Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) .  and the only way a slave feels its Uboodiyah.  its servitude to Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)  is in its abject nature.  It is in its subjection to Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . and that occurs by desiring the atonement when one has done wrong. It is in desiring to reconnect with one's true nature.  and this is why we were given Wudu.  what a gift this gift of wudu. what a gift.  the gift of purifying ourselves.  what a gift is the gift of salaah. to pray to Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) .  what a gift to be able to recite munajaat. and call upon him.

We are literally wasting away the preciousness of this life with our distractions. Allah gave us this beautiful life.  he bestowed upon us his numerous blessings.  and we are throwing all of that away in entertainment and distractions.  One short life we have to do something.  to prove ourselves to Allah. that he did not make a mistake by creating us.  and here we are crashing birds into buildings in the name of entertainment.  The things we do . just to feel that adrenaline rush.  just to feel alive.

There is this guy. jumping off a bridge . tied to a rubber string.  and seeing a cement sidewalk.  heading right for it.  suddenly he feels alive. But literally trying to kill himself. he feels alive. And then he wants to repeat that experience over and over again. just because he wants to feel alive.  But that is not the life the human being was created for.  it's not through adrealine rushes.  it is not through the rush of drugs penetrating your brain. it is not through the rush of jumping out of a flying airplane. skydiving. It is not through meaningless affairs and sleeping around for temporary pleasures. It's not through intoxication.  Those are not the things that will make you feel alive.  The ONLY thing that will make you feel alive is to become the slave of the Hayye.  the ever living.  To become a slave of the ever living who never dies. that is the real secret of true life. This is the challenge of the human being.  and this is what we have to wake up to.

Reason Huquq Allah is first and then Huquq because once the heart becomes soft for Allah. it'll become soft for people

Huqooq Al-IBAAD

And then finally there is Huqooq AlIbaad…. The rights of creation…. Now that we have recognized Allah as your master THROUGH his divine attributes. and we have trained our hearts in the divine light of those attributes. it's now time that we reflect those divine attributes in our interactions with Allah's creation…. We trained ourselves to be generous with US. it's now time to reflect that generosity on to others in our dealings with them. We trained ourselves to be truthful. to be sincere with us.  it is now time to reflect that truthfulness. that sidq. that sincerity. in our dealings with others. We've recognized how allah is forgiving with us. how he is patient with us. We now have to reflect those attributes by being patient and forgiving towards others. And this begins with blood ties. The first group of people we have to reflect these attributes on to. is our our family. parents. grandparents. uncles. aunts. even that annoying cousin of yours. That's where this begins. Silatur Reham. blood ties. kinship. Allah said I work for you like a mother's womb works for the fetus. I have made myself a mother's womb for you. Now you must reflect those same characteristics to the people of your family. you have to become a mother's womb for them in your interactions with them. That's why it's called Silatur Reham. Ties of the Reham. To forgive your brother for Allah's sake. to forgive your sister for allahs' sake. NOT FOR THEM. To do it for Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . Really. there are people who have not talked to their brothers and sisters for years. There are some who haven't spoken to their parents for years. Never be that person. don't cut off your bloodship bonds. And you have to do it for the sake of Allah. not the person you are dealing with. A man once came to the messenger of Allah and said.
⟪ar-quote:یا رسول اللہ.  اَصِلُ اَخِیہِ.  وَ یَقطَعُنِی . وَ اُعطِیہِ وَ یَمنَعُنِی⟫

Oh messenger of Allah. I give him he withhold.  I come to him he cuts me off.  what should I do?  the Prophet replied. that is silatar Reham. What you doing is the right thing!. Continue doing it even though he is cutting you off. That's Islam. This is Islam. and its hard. Don't think this is an easy religion. But we WANT to be people that strive. we want to be people that honor ourselvs. because Allah has honored us when he said
⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ كَرَّمْنَا بَنِىٓ آدَمَ وَحَمَلْنَهُمْ فِى ٱلْبَرِّ وَٱلْبَحْرِ⟫

we have ennobled the children of Adam.  we've made you leaders over the land and the oceans.  We gave you a heart.  We gave you an intellect. We nourishem them with our revelation.  We give you the ability to overcome the worst aspect of yourself.  and even if from time to time you capitulate.  we've given you the means to renew and to restore the self. through tawba. through repentence. What a gift from Allah. So this is what we have to do. and we have to do it with Ikhlaas. with sincerity . only for the sake of Allah. But it's not easy. It's very hard to give up your akhlaaq in the moment of anger.

And this is actually a great litmus test for us. How we react to anger. how we react to desires. passions. How we react when things don't go our way. that's a true indication of where we stand on the scale of character. And our reaction will show us. how much we actually DO believe in the Quran. The next time someone mistreats you . talks to you disrespectfully. observe how you handle that situation. that'll tell you how well nourished your soul is. Really.

Once Rasul Allah saw a man talking to Maulana Ali in a very disrespectful manner…. But in return Maulana Ali responded with kindness…. And despire this kindness. this man continued to act in a disrespectful …. wretched manner with him . but Maulana Ali kept responding with kindness over and over again…. When the man left Rasul Allah asked him. Ya Ali…. I saw this man talk to you in such a disrespectful manner…. treat you in a horrible way…. over and over again…. But you kept showing him kindness and respect. Why is that?. And Maulana Ali replied…. Ya Rasul Allah…. If this man is not willing to give up his wretched and evil nature for me…. Why should I give up my good nature for him? SubhanAllah! What a beautiful statement…. If this man is not going to give up his wretched manners …. Then why should I give up my good manner?. Meaning if he is going to CONTINUE to hold on to something ugly. why should I let go of something beautiful that I posess. That's the beauty of Akhlaaq.

That's the beauty of Islam. Rasul Allah was sent with the beauty of this light. the light of divine attributes. And with this light he purified the MOST barbaric group that ever existed. Read the history of Islam. Understand the mentality of the poeple he was sent to reform. They were worst than animals. There was not one virtue that existed in them. They were literally barbarians. they would eat the flesh of elephants and corocodiles. When they would eat a goat or a sheet. they would even boil and eat the leather. they would burn their enemies alive. they would rip out their skin and wear it like a scarf. They would crack open their skull and drink wine in it. their women would dye their clothes in the blood of their enemeies. Not only they would kill the enemy. they would tie that persons camel to the mans gave until it starved to death. sons would marry their mohters. daughters were burried alive. they would use the children of their enemies for target practice. Even their prayers. even their prayers were barbaric.

⟪ar-quote:یا ربِّ فَلا  تَجعَل حَیَاتی مَذِلَّۃُ ولا مَوتَتِی بَینَ النِّسآءِ نوائِحِ⟫

⟪ar-quote:ولاکن قَتیلاً  تَمزَقُ الطَّیرِ حَولَہُ . و تَشرُبُ غِربانُ الدَّم من جوارح⟫

Oh lord, do not disgrace me in my life by letting me die on a bed between grieving women

Give me a death where birds are tearing out my flesh and crows are drinking my fresh blood gusing out of my limbs.

This was the state of the Arabs when Rasul Allah came between them. and he converted this nation. in the people. that when we mention their names. we say Rehmatullah Alayhe. May the mercy of Allah be with them. He transformed them in the sahaba that we use as examples for generosity. kindness and love today. How did he do that?. With his akhlaaq. with his character. And this is why on the day of Ghadeer when Rasul Allah asked. الست اولاکم من انفسکم. I am not more beloved to you than your souls?. What did they reply. بلا یا رسول اللہ. Indeed you are ya rasul allah. ⟪ar:كنا الحيوانات. كنت جعلنا البشر⟫. We were animals. you made us human beings.  Don't understimate the power of Akhlaaq. This is what Rasul Allah was sent for. He himself said.

 I was sent to perfect noble character. And Innama in classical arabic is taken to mean.  the ONLY reason I was sent. is to perfect noble character. 

### Two types of death

Because this is what we're going to take back with us. As Rasul Allah said in a hadees. at the moment of our deaths. angels descend.
⟪ar-quote:اخرِج اَنفُسِکُم الیوم⟫

Oh Soul come out now of this body. and when those who have not worked on the development of thier souls. they say.
⟪ar-quote:رَبِّ ارْجِعُونِی. لَعَلِّی عَمَلاً صَالِحا⟫

Oh Allah let me be for a little more while. so that I can do some good deeds. I promise I will now live like a true beliver. and the
⟪ar-quote:اَیَّتُھَا النَّفسَ الخَبِیثَۃ کاَنَت فِی الَجسَدِ الخَبِیث.⟫

Oh you wretched soul. living within a wretched body.

come out. And that soul experiences the greatest fear it has ever experienced. because it can now see the ugly face of its actions. the angel of death says.
⟪ar-quote:اَبشرِیِ بِحَمِیمٍ وَ غَسَّاق. و آخِرَ مِن شَکلِہِ اَزوَاج⟫

On the other hand when a Momin dies. as Allah says int he Quran
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ قَالُوا۟ رَبُّنَا ٱللَّهُ ثُمَّ ٱسْتَقَمُوا۟ تَتَنَزَّلُ عَلَيْهِمُ ٱلْمَلَٓئِكَةُ أَلَّا تَخَافُوا۟ وَلَا تَحْزَنُوا۟ وَأَبْشِرُوا۟ بِٱلْجَنَّةِ ٱلَّتِى كُنتُمْ تُوعَدُونَ⟫

Indeed, those who have said, "Our master is Allah " and then remained on the right course - the angels descend upon them, saying, "Do not fear and do not grieve but receive good tidings of Paradise, which you were promised.

We were your friends in the worldly life and in the Hereafter. . And in heaven.  you will have whatever your souls desire, and you will have whatever you request. as a gift from your master who is extremely Forgiving and Merciful.These angels . they descend from the sky and say to this believer.

Oh pious soul. living in a pious body. come out.
